  /* Background layer & stage are siblings at z-index 0; stage paints later in
     DOM. Original rule made stage 75% opaque black when a bg was active,
     which drowned out AI images (effective opacity dropped to ~9%). The
     visualizer canvas inside .stage retains its own appearance — we just
     make the stage's BACKGROUND transparent so the bg-img beneath can show.
     A tiny dim (15% black) keeps high-contrast visualizers readable without
     obscuring the image. */

       First Esc press during a session shows this. Pauses speech + drone,
       gives the user a breath, and offers two clear paths: continue, or
       commit to a full counted re-alert end. Second Esc (while open) commits.
       Layer 50 (above session, below full modals at 100). -->

      <h2 id="spTitle">Paused — you're safe</h2>
      <p class="sp-line">Take a breath. Feel your feet on the ground.</p>
      <p class="sp-sub">Nothing is happening. The session is on hold. You can continue when you're ready, or end with a full counted re-alert.</p>
      <div class="sp-time" id="spTimeNow"></div>
      <div class="sp-actions">
        <button type="button" class="sp-continue" id="spContinueBtn">▸ continue session</button>
        <button type="button" class="sp-end" id="spEndBtn">end now &amp; re-alert</button>
      </div>

<script>
  // ====================================================================
  // IDB STORAGE (ported from Adaptive Session Studio — MIT)
  // Replaces localStorage for reliable persistence
  // ====================================================================
  const IDB_NAME = 'stillness-db';
  const IDB_VER  = 1;
  const IDB_STORE = 'kv';
  let _idb = null;
  let _idbOpenP = null;

  function _openIdb() {
    if (_idb) return Promise.resolve(_idb);
    if (_idbOpenP) return _idbOpenP;
    _idbOpenP = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const req = indexedDB.open(IDB_NAME, IDB_VER);
      req.onupgradeneeded = e => {
        const db = e.target.result;
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(IDB_STORE)) db.createObjectStore(IDB_STORE);
      };
      req.onsuccess = e => {
        _idb = e.target.result;
        _idb.onclose = () => { _idb = null; _idbOpenP = null; };
        resolve(_idb);
      };
      req.onerror = e => { _idbOpenP = null; reject(e.target.error ?? new Error('IDB open failed')); };
    });
    return _idbOpenP;
  }
  async function idbGet(key) {
    try {
      const db = await _openIdb();
      return await new Promise((res, rej) => {
        const r = db.transaction(IDB_STORE, 'readonly').objectStore(IDB_STORE).get(key);
        r.onsuccess = () => res(r.result ?? null);
        r.onerror = e => rej(e.target.error);
      });
    } catch { return null; }
  }
  async function idbSet(key, value) {
    try {
      const db = await _openIdb();
      await new Promise((res, rej) => {
        const tx = db.transaction(IDB_STORE, 'readwrite');
        tx.objectStore(IDB_STORE).put(value, key);
        tx.oncomplete = res;
        tx.onerror = e => rej(e.target.error);
      });
    } catch {}
  }
  async function idbDel(key) {
    try {
      const db = await _openIdb();
      await new Promise((res, rej) => {
        const tx = db.transaction(IDB_STORE, 'readwrite');
        tx.objectStore(IDB_STORE).delete(key);
        tx.oncomplete = res;
        tx.onerror = e => rej(e.target.error);
      });
    } catch {}
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // TOAST NOTIFICATIONS (ported from Adaptive Session Studio — MIT)
  // Non-blocking replacements for alert()
  // ====================================================================
  const TOAST_ICONS    = { info: 'ℹ', success: '✓', warn: '⚠', error: '✕' };
  const TOAST_DURATION = { info: 3500, success: 3000, warn: 5000, error: 0 };

  function toast(type, message, ms) {
    const container = $('toastContainer');
    if (!container) return;
    const duration = ms !== undefined ? ms : TOAST_DURATION[type] || 3500;
    const el = document.createElement('div');
    el.className = `toast toast-${type}`;
    el.innerHTML = `<span class="toast-icon">${TOAST_ICONS[type] || 'ℹ'}</span><span class="toast-text">${escapeHtml(message)}</span><button class="toast-close">×</button>`;
    el.querySelector('.toast-close').addEventListener('click', () => dismissToast(el));
    if (duration === 0) el.addEventListener('click', () => dismissToast(el));
    container.appendChild(el);
    requestAnimationFrame(() => el.classList.add('show'));
    let timer = null;
    if (duration > 0) timer = setTimeout(() => dismissToast(el), duration);
    function dismissToast(t) { clearTimeout(timer); t.classList.remove('show'); setTimeout(() => t.remove(), 220); }
    return el;
  }
  const notify = {
    info:    (msg, ms) => toast('info', msg, ms),
    success: (msg, ms) => toast('success', msg, ms),
    warn:    (msg, ms) => toast('warn', msg, ms),
    error:   (msg, ms) => toast('error', msg, ms),
  };

  function confirmAsync(message, opts = {}) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      const backdrop = document.createElement('div');
      backdrop.className = 'modal-backdrop visible';
      backdrop.innerHTML = `<div class="modal" style="max-width:420px;">
        <div style="font-size:0.88rem;line-height:1.55;color:var(--text-dim);white-space:pre-line;">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>
        <div class="modal-actions" style="margin-top:16px;">
          <button class="btn secondary" id="_confirmNo">${opts.cancelText || 'cancel'}</button>
          <button class="btn" id="_confirmYes">${opts.okText || 'confirm'}</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
      document.body.appendChild(backdrop);
      const cleanup = (val) => { backdrop.remove(); resolve(val); };
      backdrop.querySelector('#_confirmYes').addEventListener('click', () => cleanup(true));
      backdrop.querySelector('#_confirmNo').addEventListener('click', () => cleanup(false));
      backdrop.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === backdrop) cleanup(false); });
    });
  }

  function alertModal(title, message) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      const backdrop = document.createElement('div');
      backdrop.className = 'modal-backdrop visible';
      backdrop.innerHTML = `<div class="modal" style="max-width:420px;">
        ${title ? `<h2 style="margin:0 0 12px;">${escapeHtml(title)}</h2>` : ''}
        <div style="font-size:0.84rem;line-height:1.55;color:var(--text-dim);white-space:pre-line;">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>
        <div class="modal-actions" style="margin-top:16px;">
          <button class="btn" id="_alertOk">ok</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
      document.body.appendChild(backdrop);
      const cleanup = () => { backdrop.remove(); resolve(); };
      backdrop.querySelector('#_alertOk').addEventListener('click', cleanup);
      backdrop.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === backdrop) cleanup(); });
    });
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // iOS Safari viewport fix (from Perchance skill reference)
  // ====================================================================
  try {
    const isTouchScreen = window.matchMedia("(pointer: coarse)").matches;
    const isSafari = navigator.vendor?.indexOf('Apple') > -1
      && !navigator.userAgent.includes('CriOS')
      && !navigator.userAgent.includes('FxiOS');
    if (isSafari && window.innerWidth < 800 && isTouchScreen) {
      const viewportMeta = document.querySelector("[name=viewport]");
      if (viewportMeta && !viewportMeta.getAttribute("content").includes("maximum-scale")) {
        viewportMeta.setAttribute("content",
          viewportMeta.getAttribute("content") + ", maximum-scale=1");
      }
    }
  } catch(e) { console.error(e); }

  const INTENTION_TYPES = {
    // ── Foundation ─────────────────────────────────────────────

    focus: { label: 'Deep focus / concentration', hint: 'Laser focus for study, work, or creative tasks.', guidance: `FOCUS TUNNEL: everything outside the task fades to grey.     // ── Body ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    pain: { label: 'Pain management / comfort', hint: 'Name the specific sensation and its location. Not a substitute for medical care.', guidance: `PAIN MANAGEMENT: NEVER deny the sensation exists.     amnesia: { label: 'Suggested amnesia', hint: 'Forget a specific thing temporarily.     surrender: { label: 'Surrender / ego dissolution', hint: 'Let go of control entirely. Deep trust required.', guidance: `SURRENDER: progressive release of control, agency, decision-making. The paradox: the less they do, the more happens. Frame as SAFETY, not loss: "There is nothing to hold onto, and nothing to fall from." Emergence must be thorough and grounding.` },
    conditioning: { label: 'Behavioral conditioning', hint: 'Pair a specific stimulus with a specific automatic response, over repetition.', guidance: `CONDITIONING PROTOCOL: this is classical conditioning via suggestion. Define STIMULUS clearly. Define RESPONSE clearly. Repeat the pairing MINIMUM five times in WORK phase, each time more vivid. "Every time you [stimulus], instantly and automatically you [response]." Progressive intensification. Future-pace: "Tomorrow, when [stimulus] happens, you'll notice [response] is already there, already happening." Include a test.` },
  };

  /** Sync state._debug from checkbox DOM. Called on load and on the debug toggle.
   *  Single source of truth: one `debugMode` checkbox enables every debug flag. */
  function _syncDebugState() {
    const d = state._debug;
    const on = !!document.getElementById('debugMode')?.checked;
    d.skipRescue       = on;
    d.skipCooldown     = on;
    d.skipSafetyGate   = on;
    d.skipMethodGating = on;
    d.verbose          = on;
    _renderDebugBanner();
  }

  /** Show/hide the floating "DEBUG" indicator whenever any debug flag is active. */
  function _renderDebugBanner() {
    const anyOn = Object.values(state._debug).some(Boolean);
    let el = document.getElementById('_debugBanner');
    if (anyOn && !el) {
      el = document.createElement('div');
      el.id = '_debugBanner';
      el.textContent = '\u26A0 DEBUG';
      el.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:8px;right:8px;z-index:99999;background:rgba(220,60,60,0.92);color:#fff;font-size:0.62rem;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:0.08em;padding:4px 8px;border-radius:4px;pointer-events:none;box-shadow:0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);';
      document.body.appendChild(el);
    } else if (!anyOn && el) {
      el.remove();
    }
  }

  /** Verbose Smart Director logger. No-op unless state._debug.verbose is on. */
  function sdLog(...args) {
    if (state._debug?.verbose) console.log('[SmartDirector]', ...args);
  }

  const PHASE_DURATIONS = {

  const _FALLBACK_PERSONA = { id: 'fallback', name: 'Guide', tagline: '', category: 'contemplative', systemPrompt: '' };
  const _FALLBACK_METHOD = METHODS[0];
  const getMethod = () => METHODS.find(m => m.id === state.selectedMethodId) || _FALLBACK_METHOD;
  const getPersona = () => (state.personas.find(p => p.id === state.selectedPersonaId) || state.personas[0]) ?? _FALLBACK_PERSONA;
  const PERSONA_KEY = 'stillness_personas_v1';

  // ── Persona schema, v2 (Perchance Character-aligned) ──────────────────────
  // The historical HNE shape was { id, name, tagline, category, systemPrompt }.
  // The Perchance Character spec (see perchance-api skill §4.1) is richer:
  // { id, uuid, name, roleInstruction, reminderMessage, imagePromptPrefix,
  //   imagePromptSuffix, metaTitle, metaDescription, metaImage, customData,
  //   creationTime, ... }. v2 is additive — back-compat preserved by writing
  // BOTH `roleInstruction` and `systemPrompt` on save and reading either on
  // load. Builtin personas don't need rewriting; normalizePersona() backfills
  // missing fields at runtime.
  const PERSONA_SCHEMA_VERSION = 2;

  /** Read a persona's role/system prompt with back-compat across schema versions.
   *  Reads `roleInstruction` first (Perchance-canonical) then falls back to the
   *  legacy `systemPrompt` field so existing data and shared personas keep working. */
  function getPersonaRole(persona) {
    if (!persona) return '';
    return persona.roleInstruction || persona.systemPrompt || '';
  }

  /** Lazily upgrade a persona to v2 schema — backfills missing fields with
   *  sensible defaults. Called at load time (refreshPersonas) and at save
   *  time (savePersonaFromForm). Idempotent — running it twice is a no-op.
   *  Returns a NEW object; never mutates input. */
  function normalizePersona(p) {
    if (!p || typeof p !== 'object') return p;
    const role = p.roleInstruction || p.systemPrompt || '';
    return {
      // ── Core (kept) ─────────────────────────
      id:       p.id,
      name:     p.name,
      tagline:  p.tagline || '',
      category: p.category || 'contemplative',
      // ── Role text — write BOTH for back-compat when shared between versions ─
      roleInstruction: role,
      systemPrompt:    role, // alias maintained for older code paths + share recipients on older versions
      // ── New v2 fields (Perchance-aligned) ─────────────────────────
      uuid:                  p.uuid || _genPersonaUuid(),
      reminderMessage:       p.reminderMessage || '',
      imagePromptPrefix:     p.imagePromptPrefix || '',
      imagePromptSuffix:     p.imagePromptSuffix || '',
      metaTitle:             p.metaTitle || '',
      metaDescription:       p.metaDescription || '',
      metaImage:             p.metaImage || '',
      creationTime:          p.creationTime || Date.now(),
      customData:            (p.customData && typeof p.customData === 'object') ? p.customData : {},
      schemaVersion:         PERSONA_SCHEMA_VERSION,
      // ── HNE-specific recommendations (optional; null = no recommendation) ──
      recommendedSpeechRate: Number.isFinite(p.recommendedSpeechRate) ? p.recommendedSpeechRate : null,
      recommendedVisual:     p.recommendedVisual     || null,
      recommendedSoundscape: p.recommendedSoundscape || null,
      // ── Flags preserved ─────────────────────────
      ...(p.isCustom    && { isCustom:    true }),
      ...(p.isCommunity && { isCommunity: true }),
      ...(p.packName    && { packName:    p.packName }),
    };
  }

  /** Generate a per-persona UUID (used for share-link dedup). Cheap, no deps. */
  function _genPersonaUuid() {
    // crypto.randomUUID is widely supported but fall back to a manual generator
    // for older browsers / non-secure contexts.
    if (typeof crypto !== 'undefined' && crypto.randomUUID) {
      try { return crypto.randomUUID(); } catch {}
    }
    return 'p-' + Date.now().toString(36) + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10);
  }


  // IDB-backed storage with localStorage migration
  let _personaCache = null;

  async function _initStorage() {
    // Migrate personas from localStorage → IDB
    _personaCache = await idbGet(PERSONA_KEY);
    if (!_personaCache) {
      try {
        const lsRaw = localStorage.getItem(PERSONA_KEY);
        if (lsRaw) { _personaCache = JSON.parse(lsRaw); await idbSet(PERSONA_KEY, _personaCache); localStorage.removeItem(PERSONA_KEY); }
      } catch {}
    }
    if (!Array.isArray(_personaCache)) _personaCache = [];

    // Normalize legacy history/settings/analytics stores
    try {
      const legacyHistory = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
      if (Array.isArray(legacyHistory) && legacyHistory.length) {
        const normalizedHistory = legacyHistory.map(normalizeHistoryEntry).sort((a,b)=>(b.date||0)-(a.date||0));
        await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', normalizedHistory);
      }
    } catch {}
    try {
      const analytics = await idbGet(ANALYTICS_KEY) || await idbGet('stillness_analytics_v2');
      if (analytics) await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, normalizeAnalyticsData(analytics));
    } catch {}
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem('stillness_settings_v4') || localStorage.getItem('stillness_settings_v3') || localStorage.getItem('stillness_settings_v2');
      if (raw && !localStorage.getItem(SETTINGS_KEY)) {
        localStorage.setItem(SETTINGS_KEY, JSON.stringify(normalizeSettings(JSON.parse(raw))));
      }
    } catch {}

    // Persist browser storage so IDB isn't cleared
    if (navigator.storage?.persist) await navigator.storage.persist();
  }

  const loadCustomPersonas = () => _personaCache || [];
  const saveCustomPersonas = arr => { _personaCache = arr; idbSet(PERSONA_KEY, arr); return true; };

  // ====================================================================
  // AUDIO-REACTIVE VISUALIZER — mode/gain mapping + setter
  // ====================================================================
  // The user-facing toggle is 3-state: off / subtle / dramatic. Each maps
  // to a gain multiplier applied at visualizer read-time (not write-time)
  // so flipping modes takes effect on the next frame with no engine restart.
  // ====================================================================
  const GAIN_FOR_MODE = { off: 0, subtle: 0.3, dramatic: 1.0 };
  function setAudioReactiveMode(mode) {
    if (!(mode in GAIN_FOR_MODE)) mode = 'off';
    state.audioReactiveMode = mode;
    state.audioReactive.gain = GAIN_FOR_MODE[mode];
    // Live-panel + Step 5 segmented controls re-render
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-audio-mode]').forEach(btn => {
      btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.audioMode === mode);
    });
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // AUDIO UPDATE LOOP — single RAF producing state.audioReactive
  // ====================================================================
  // Polls the soundscape AnalyserNode + ticks the voice envelope. Started
  // by startAudioReactiveLoop() when entering a session; stopped on
  // session end. Cheap — ~0.3ms per frame.
  // ====================================================================

  // Bin ranges at fftSize 256, 48kHz sample rate (typical):
  //   bins 0..5    → ~0–1050Hz (bass)
  //   bins 6..40   → ~1050–7500Hz (mid)
  //   bins 41..100 → ~7500–18750Hz (treble)
  const BASS_BINS   = [0, 5];
  const MID_BINS    = [6, 40];
  const TREBLE_BINS = [41, 100];

  function _avgBins(buf, lo, hi) {
    let sum = 0, count = 0;
    const end = Math.min(hi, buf.length - 1);
    for (let i = lo; i <= end; i++) { sum += buf[i]; count++; }
    return count > 0 ? sum / (count * 255) : 0;  // normalize 0..1
  }
  function _rmsBins(buf) {
    let sum = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < buf.length; i++) sum += buf[i] * buf[i];
    return Math.sqrt(sum / buf.length) / 255;
  }

  function updateAudioReactiveFrame() {
    const a = state.audioReactive;
    // `drone` is the main SoundscapeEngine instance defined later in this IIFE.
    // We reference it lazily via the enclosing scope — it's non-null once a
    // session has started and the soundscape has begun.
    const haveSoundscape = (typeof drone !== 'undefined') && drone && drone.analyser && a._fftBuffer;
    const now = performance.now();

    // FFT signals (soundscape)
    if (haveSoundscape) {
      drone.analyser.getByteFrequencyData(a._fftBuffer);
      a.bass    = _avgBins(a._fftBuffer, BASS_BINS[0],   BASS_BINS[1]);
      a.mid     = _avgBins(a._fftBuffer, MID_BINS[0],    MID_BINS[1]);
      a.treble  = _avgBins(a._fftBuffer, TREBLE_BINS[0], TREBLE_BINS[1]);
      a.overall = _rmsBins(a._fftBuffer);
    } else {
      a.bass = a.mid = a.treble = a.overall = 0;
    }

    // Voice pulse envelope (synthesized from speechSynthesis boundary events).
    //   voicePulse   — instant spike that decays linearly over 300ms
    //   voiceEnvelope — 1-pole low-pass of voicePulse (smoother, for visuals)
    const dt = (now - a._voicePulseSpawnedAt) / 300;
    a.voicePulse = Math.max(0, 1 - dt);
    a.voiceEnvelope = a.voiceEnvelope * 0.85 + a.voicePulse * 0.15;

    // active = any signal source producing meaningful data
    a.active = haveSoundscape || a.voiceEnvelope > 0.02;
  }

  function startAudioReactiveLoop() {
    const a = state.audioReactive;
    if (a._rafHandle) return; // already running
    let _lastTickMs = performance.now();
    const tick = () => {
      if (!a._rafHandle) return; // stopped
      updateAudioReactiveFrame();
      tickStateEngine(); // state-engine reads from audioReactive; needs to run after update
      // Rules engine reads engineState and fires actions when conditions hold.
      // Runs only when opt-in flag is true; default off to preserve current behavior.
      const nowMs = performance.now();
      const frameSec = Math.min(0.1, (nowMs - _lastTickMs) / 1000); // cap at 100ms (e.g. tab backgrounding)
      _lastTickMs = nowMs;
      if (state.runtimeRulesEnabled) {
        tickRulesEngine(frameSec);
        tickTriggerWindows(); // trigger windows use same opt-in flag as rules
      }
      // Playback dynamics — independent opt-in flag (state.playbackDynamics.enabled).
      // No-op when disabled, so safe to call unconditionally.
      tickPlaybackDynamics(frameSec);
      a._rafHandle = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    };
    a._rafHandle = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
  }

  function stopAudioReactiveLoop() {
    const a = state.audioReactive;
    if (a._rafHandle) { cancelAnimationFrame(a._rafHandle); a._rafHandle = null; }
    a.bass = a.mid = a.treble = a.overall = 0;
    a.voicePulse = 0; a.voiceEnvelope = 0; a.active = false;
  }

  /** Per-frame modulation values for visualizers. Returns all-zeros when
   *  inactive or mode=off, so retrofitted visualizers are zero-regression.
   *  Callers should keep their existing autonomous motion and treat these
   *  as ADDITIVE modulators, not replacements. */
  function getAudioMod() {
    const a = state.audioReactive;
    if (!a || !a.active || a.gain === 0) {
      return { overall: 0, bass: 0, mid: 0, treble: 0, pulse: 0, envelope: 0 };
    }
    // Apply ambient-brightness dim scale — when the room is dark, viz amplitude
    // drops to 0.6×; when bright, climbs to 1.2×. Default 1.0 when webcam is off.
    const dim = state.ambientDimScale ?? 1.0;
    const g = a.gain * dim;
    return {
      overall:  a.overall       * g,
      bass:     a.bass          * g,
      mid:      a.mid           * g,
      treble:   a.treble        * g,
      pulse:    a.voicePulse    * g,
      envelope: a.voiceEnvelope * g,
    };
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // STATE ENGINE — canonical runtime metric bundle
  // ====================================================================
  // Normalizes playback signals into a single object (state.engineState)
  // that rules-engine and trigger-windows read without caring about the
  // source. EMA-smoothed `engagement` is a weighted fusion of voice +
  // audio + time signals. External callers can inject extra signals via
  // setEngineSignal().
  //
  // Published state.engineState shape:
  //   voiceEnvelope    0–1   smoothed narrator voice presence
  //   voicePulse       0–1   transient voice spike (near 1 on word onset)
  //   audioOverall     0–1   full-mix audio energy (FFT-derived)
  //   engagement       0–1   EMA-fused engagement score
  //   sessionSec       sec   wall-clock elapsed since session start (minus pauses)
  //   completedFraction 0–1  fraction of estimated total runtime elapsed
  //   sinceVoiceSec    sec   seconds since last voiceEnvelope > threshold
  //   currentPhase     str   phase id currently playing (e.g. 'settling', 'work-2')
  //   phaseKind        str   base kind ('settling'|'induction'|'deepener'|...)
  //   phaseSec         sec   seconds elapsed in current phase
  //   playing          bool  session active and not paused
  //   paused           bool  mirrors state.paused
  //
  // Adapted from /mnt/user-data/uploads/Adaptive-Session-Studio — js/state-engine.js
  // ====================================================================
  const ENGINE_DEFAULT_WEIGHTS = {
    voiceEnvelope: 0.55,  // narrator presence dominates — silent narrator = low engagement
    audioOverall:  0.30,  // soundscape + voice combined energy
    voicePresence: 0.15,  // binary "any voice heard recently" bonus
  };
  const ENGINE_EMA_ALPHA      = 0.05;   // ~3s time constant at 60fps
  const VOICE_PRESENCE_THRESHOLD = 0.12; // voiceEnvelope above this counts as "speaking"

  let _engineSmoothedEngagement = 0;
  let _engineLastVoiceAt        = 0;    // wall-clock ms of last voiceEnvelope crossing threshold
  let _enginePhaseEnteredAt     = 0;    // wall-clock ms when current phase was entered
  let _engineLastPhase          = null; // track phase transitions
  const _engineExternalSignals  = {};   // name → { value: 0–1, weight: 0–1 }

  // Seed engineState so consumers reading pre-init don't crash
  if (!state.engineState) {
    state.engineState = {
      voiceEnvelope: 0, voicePulse: 0, audioOverall: 0, engagement: 0,
      sessionSec: 0, completedFraction: 0, sinceVoiceSec: 0,
      currentPhase: null, phaseKind: null, phaseSec: 0,
      playing: false, paused: false,
    };
  }

  /** Inject an external signal into the engagement fusion. Value + weight both 0–1.
   *  Example: a physiological sensor adapter could push its own signal this way. */
  function setEngineSignal(name, value, weight = 0.3) {
    _engineExternalSignals[name] = {
      value:  Math.max(0, Math.min(1, value)),
      weight: Math.max(0, Math.min(1, weight)),
    };
  }
  function clearEngineSignals() {
    Object.keys(_engineExternalSignals).forEach(k => delete _engineExternalSignals[k]);
  }

  function _engineDeriveEngagement(voiceEnv, audioOverall, voicePresence, playing) {
    if (!playing) return _engineSmoothedEngagement;
    const weights = { ...ENGINE_DEFAULT_WEIGHTS };
    const signals = { voiceEnvelope: voiceEnv, audioOverall, voicePresence };
    for (const [name, { value, weight }] of Object.entries(_engineExternalSignals)) {
      signals[name] = value;
      weights[name] = weight;
    }
    const totalWeight = Object.values(weights).reduce((s, w) => s + w, 0) || 1;
    let raw = 0;
    for (const [name, w] of Object.entries(weights)) {
      raw += (signals[name] ?? 0) * (w / totalWeight);
    }
    raw = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, raw));
    _engineSmoothedEngagement += ENGINE_EMA_ALPHA * (raw - _engineSmoothedEngagement);
    return +_engineSmoothedEngagement.toFixed(3);
  }

  /** Main tick — call every RAF frame while a session is active.
   *  Reads audioReactive + playback state, produces engineState. */
  function tickStateEngine() {
    const now     = Date.now();
    const playing = !!state._sessionStartTime && !state.paused;
    const ar      = state.audioReactive || {};
    const voiceEnv     = ar.voiceEnvelope || 0;
    const voicePulse   = ar.voicePulse || 0;
    const audioOverall = ar.overall || 0;

    // Track last voice activity — used by triggers/rules to detect narrator silence
    if (voiceEnv >= VOICE_PRESENCE_THRESHOLD) _engineLastVoiceAt = now;
    const voicePresence = voiceEnv >= VOICE_PRESENCE_THRESHOLD ? 1 : 0;
    const sinceVoiceSec = _engineLastVoiceAt ? (now - _engineLastVoiceAt) / 1000 : Infinity;

    // Track phase transitions
    const curPhase = state._currentPhase || null;
    if (curPhase !== _engineLastPhase) {
      _enginePhaseEnteredAt = now;
      _engineLastPhase = curPhase;
    }
    const phaseSec = playing && _enginePhaseEnteredAt ? (now - _enginePhaseEnteredAt) / 1000 : 0;

    // Session time (minus pauses) — mirrors finishSession's elapsed calculation
    let sessionSec = 0;
    if (state._sessionStartTime) {
      let pausedMs = state._pausedTotalMs || 0;
      if (state._pauseStartedAt) pausedMs += (now - state._pauseStartedAt);
      sessionSec = Math.max(0, (now - state._sessionStartTime - pausedMs) / 1000);
    }

    // Completion fraction against estimated total runtime (from script metrics)
    const estTotalSec = (state._estimatedTotalSec || 0);
    const completedFraction = estTotalSec > 0 ? Math.min(1, sessionSec / estTotalSec) : 0;

    state.engineState = {
      voiceEnvelope: voiceEnv,
      voicePulse,
      audioOverall,
      engagement:    _engineDeriveEngagement(voiceEnv, audioOverall, voicePresence, playing),
      sessionSec:    +sessionSec.toFixed(2),
      completedFraction: +completedFraction.toFixed(3),
      sinceVoiceSec: Number.isFinite(sinceVoiceSec) ? +sinceVoiceSec.toFixed(2) : null,
      currentPhase:  curPhase,
      phaseKind:     curPhase ? phaseBase(curPhase) : null,
      phaseSec:      +phaseSec.toFixed(2),
      playing,
      paused:        !!state.paused,
    };
  }

  /** Read a single metric by name — used by rule conditions. */
  function getEngineMetric(metric) {
    const es = state.engineState || {};
    switch (metric) {
      case 'voiceEnvelope':     return es.voiceEnvelope ?? 0;
      case 'voicePulse':        return es.voicePulse ?? 0;
      case 'audioOverall':      return es.audioOverall ?? 0;
      case 'engagement':        return es.engagement ?? 0;
      case 'sessionSec':        return es.sessionSec ?? 0;
      case 'completedFraction': return es.completedFraction ?? 0;
      case 'sinceVoiceSec':     return es.sinceVoiceSec ?? 0;
      case 'phaseSec':          return es.phaseSec ?? 0;
      // Webcam-derived. Returns 0 when webcam is off (signals not injected).
      // attention/wakefulness pull from the external-signal cache the webcam
      // adapter writes into via setEngineSignal.
      case 'attention':         return _engineExternalSignals?.attention?.value ?? 0;
      case 'wakefulness':       return _engineExternalSignals?.wakefulness?.value ?? 0;
      case 'faceDetected':      return state._webcam?.faceDetected ? 1 : 0;
      case 'ambientBrightness': return state.ambientBrightness ?? 0.5;
      default:                  return 0;
    }
  }

  /** Evaluate a [metric, op, value] condition against the current engine state.
   *  Also supports pseudo-metrics 'phaseKind' (string equality) and
   *  'currentPhase' (exact phase-id match). */
  function evalEngineCondition(condition) {
    if (!condition) return false;
    const { metric, op, value } = condition;
    // String-valued pseudo-metrics — support only '==' and '!=' ops
    if (metric === 'phaseKind' || metric === 'currentPhase') {
      const es = state.engineState || {};
      const actual = String(es[metric] || '');
      const expected = String(value || '');
      if (op === '==') return actual === expected;
      if (op === '!=') return actual !== expected;
      return false;
    }
    const actual = getEngineMetric(metric);
    switch (op) {
      case '<':  return actual <  value;
      case '>':  return actual >  value;
      case '<=': return actual <= value;
      case '>=': return actual >= value;
      case '==': return Math.abs(actual - value) < 0.001;
      case '!=': return Math.abs(actual - value) >= 0.001;
      default:   return false;
    }
  }

  /** Reset — call on session end so a new session starts with a clean slate. */
  function resetStateEngine() {
    _engineSmoothedEngagement = 0;
    _engineLastVoiceAt        = 0;
    _enginePhaseEnteredAt     = 0;
    _engineLastPhase          = null;
    clearEngineSignals();
    state.engineState = {
      voiceEnvelope: 0, voicePulse: 0, audioOverall: 0, engagement: 0,
      sessionSec: 0, completedFraction: 0, sinceVoiceSec: 0,
      currentPhase: null, phaseKind: null, phaseSec: 0,
      playing: false, paused: false,
    };
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // RULES ENGINE — behavioral scripting over runtime metrics
  // ====================================================================
  // Rules fire actions when a metric condition holds for `durationSec`,
  // with a `cooldownSec` gate between re-fires. Evaluated every RAF tick
  // during active sessions.
  //
  // Rule schema (stored in state.session.rules[] for portability — but
  // since HNE sessions are generated from config not authored, rules
  // actually live on state.runtimeRules and can be declared via
  // DEFAULT_RUNTIME_RULES or added programmatically):
  //
  // {
  //   id:           string (unique),
  //   enabled:      bool,
  //   name:         string (for notify messages),
  //   condition:    { metric, op, value } — see evalEngineCondition
  //   durationSec:  number   (cond must hold this long before firing)
  //   cooldownSec:  number   (min gap between re-fires; 0 = no gap)
  //   action:       { type, param }
  // }
  //
  // Supported action types:
  //   pause              — pauses playback (via togglePause if not already paused)
  //   resume             — resumes playback
  //   emergencyExit      — triggers full rescue sequence
  //   notifyMessage      — shows a toast (param: message string)
  //   showOnScreenText   — full-screen transient overlay (param: text)
  //   duckAudio          — temporarily reduces soundscape (param: volume 0-1 or null for default)
  //   unduckAudio        — restores soundscape to state.droneVolume
  //   setSpeechRate      — adjust TTS rate (param: 0.5..2.0)
  //   setSoundscapeVolume — set drone volume (param: 0..1)
  //
  // Adapted from /mnt/user-data/uploads/Adaptive-Session-Studio — js/rules-engine.js
  // ====================================================================
  const RULES_VALID_ACTIONS = new Set([
    'pause', 'resume', 'emergencyExit', 'notifyMessage', 'showOnScreenText',
    'duckAudio', 'unduckAudio', 'setSpeechRate', 'setSoundscapeVolume',
  ]);
  const RULES_VALID_METRICS = new Set([
    'voiceEnvelope', 'voicePulse', 'audioOverall', 'engagement',
    'sessionSec', 'completedFraction', 'sinceVoiceSec',
    'phaseSec', 'phaseKind', 'currentPhase',
    // Webcam-derived signals (only populated when state._webcam.status === 'active').
    // Rules using these are no-ops when the webcam is off because the signals
    // simply aren't injected — `getEngineMetric` returns 0, so '> 0.5' never fires.
    'attention', 'wakefulness', 'faceDetected', 'ambientBrightness',
  ]);
  const RULES_VALID_OPS = new Set(['<', '>', '<=', '>=', '==', '!=']);

  function _rulesUid() {
    return 'r_' + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8);
  }

  /** Normalize a partial rule spec into a canonical runtime rule. */
  function normalizeRule(r) {
    const raw = r || {};
    const cond = raw.condition || {};
    const act  = raw.action || {};
    return {
      id:          typeof raw.id === 'string' && raw.id ? raw.id : _rulesUid(),
      enabled:     raw.enabled !== false,
      name:        typeof raw.name === 'string' && raw.name ? raw.name : 'Rule',
      condition: {
        metric: RULES_VALID_METRICS.has(cond.metric) ? cond.metric : 'engagement',
        op:     RULES_VALID_OPS.has(cond.op)         ? cond.op     : '<',
        value:  Number.isFinite(cond.value) || typeof cond.value === 'string' ? cond.value : 0.3,
      },
      durationSec: Number.isFinite(raw.durationSec) ? Math.max(0, raw.durationSec) : 5,
      cooldownSec: Number.isFinite(raw.cooldownSec) ? Math.max(0, raw.cooldownSec) : 30,
      action: {
        type:  RULES_VALID_ACTIONS.has(act.type) ? act.type : 'notifyMessage',
        param: act.param ?? null,
      },
    };
  }

  // Per-rule runtime state: { conditionHeldSec, lastFiredSec }
  // `lastFiredSec` uses sessionSec so cooldowns work relative to session start.
  const _runtimeRuleState = {};

  function _getRuntimeRuleState(id) {
    if (!_runtimeRuleState[id]) _runtimeRuleState[id] = { conditionHeldSec: 0, lastFiredSec: -Infinity };
    return _runtimeRuleState[id];
  }

  function clearRuntimeRuleState() {
    Object.keys(_runtimeRuleState).forEach(k => delete _runtimeRuleState[k]);
  }

  /** Execute a rule's action. Silent on unknown types — already caught at normalize. */
  async function executeRuleAction(rule) {
    const { type, param } = rule.action;
    const n = rule.name;
    try {
      switch (type) {
        case 'pause':
          if (!state.paused) togglePause();
          notify.info(`Rule "${n}": paused`);
          break;
        case 'resume':
          if (state.paused) togglePause();
          notify.info(`Rule "${n}": resumed`);
          break;
        case 'emergencyExit':
          notify.warn(`Rule "${n}": initiating rescue`);
          emergencyEnd();
          break;
        case 'notifyMessage':
          notify.info(String(param || 'Rule fired: ' + n).slice(0, 200));
          break;
        case 'showOnScreenText': {
          if (!param) break;
          _showRuleOverlay(String(param).slice(0, 200));
          break;
        }
        case 'duckAudio': {
          // Temporary duck — the existing ducking system in the app is complex and
          // managed at speakScript level; here we just lower drone volume directly.
          // The matching unduckAudio action (or next ducking event from speakScript)
          // restores volume. Record the pre-duck value so unduckAudio can restore it.
          if (typeof drone !== 'undefined' && drone?.setVolume) {
            if (state._rulesPreDuckVolume == null) state._rulesPreDuckVolume = state.droneVolume;
            const targetVol = Number.isFinite(Number(param)) ? Math.max(0, Math.min(1, Number(param))) : 0.1;
            drone.setVolume(targetVol);
          }
          notify.info(`Rule "${n}": ducked`);
          break;
        }
        case 'unduckAudio':
          if (typeof drone !== 'undefined' && drone?.setVolume) {
            const target = state._rulesPreDuckVolume != null ? state._rulesPreDuckVolume : state.droneVolume;
            drone.setVolume(target);
            state._rulesPreDuckVolume = null;
          }
          break;
        case 'setSpeechRate': {
          // Apply the local 0.5..2.0 hard-floor first (sanity bound), then the
          // user-tunable safety layer cap. Two layers: never below 0.5 or above 2.0
          // regardless of safety config (those are TTS-engine bounds), then further
          // clamped by safetyConfig.minSpeechRate / maxSpeechRate (default 0.6..1.5).
          const raw = Math.max(0.5, Math.min(2.0, Number.isFinite(Number(param)) ? Number(param) : 1));
          const rate = gateSpeechRate(raw);
          state.speechRate = rate;
          // Note: in-progress utterances keep their original rate — only new ones pick up the change.
          notify.info(`Rule "${n}": speech rate → ${rate.toFixed(2)}×`);
          break;
        }
        case 'setSoundscapeVolume': {
          const raw = Number.isFinite(Number(param)) ? Number(param) : 0.35;
          const vol = gateSoundscapeVolume(raw);
          state.droneVolume = vol;
          if (typeof drone !== 'undefined' && drone?.setVolume) drone.setVolume(vol);
          const slider = $('droneVolume'); if (slider) slider.value = Math.round(vol * 100);
          const lbl = $('droneVolVal'); if (lbl) lbl.textContent = Math.round(vol * 100);
          notify.info(`Rule "${n}": soundscape volume → ${Math.round(vol * 100)}%`);
          break;
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[rules] action failed:', rule.name, type, e);
    }
  }

  /** Transient full-screen overlay text (2.5s fade). Used by showOnScreenText
   *  action. Creates style block once, then appends/removes a div. */
  function _showRuleOverlay(text) {
    if (!document.getElementById('rule-overlay-style')) {
      const s = document.createElement('style');
      s.id = 'rule-overlay-style';
      s.textContent = `@keyframes ruleOverlayFade { 0%{opacity:0;transform:translate(-50%,-45%)} 15%{opacity:1;transform:translate(-50%,-50%)} 75%{opacity:1;transform:translate(-50%,-50%)} 100%{opacity:0;transform:translate(-50%,-55%)} }`;
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    }
    const el = document.createElement('div');
    el.style.cssText = `position:fixed;top:50%;left:50%;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);
      z-index:9000;background:rgba(4,4,7,0.85);border:0.5px solid rgba(196,154,60,0.35);
      border-radius:12px;padding:20px 30px;font-size:1.1rem;color:var(--text);
      font-family:var(--font-body);text-align:center;max-width:70vw;
      backdrop-filter:blur(8px);pointer-events:none;
      animation:ruleOverlayFade 2.5s ease forwards`;
    el.textContent = text;
    document.body.appendChild(el);
    setTimeout(() => el.remove(), 2600);
  }

  /** Rules list source. state.runtimeRules is the live list; falls back to
   *  DEFAULT_RUNTIME_RULES if user hasn't customized. Writable for future UI. */
  let DEFAULT_RUNTIME_RULES = [];

  function _activeRuntimeRules() {
    const r = state.runtimeRules;
    if (Array.isArray(r)) return r;
    return DEFAULT_RUNTIME_RULES;
  }

  /** Main tick — call after tickStateEngine in the RAF loop.
   *  frameSec is the time since the previous tick (for durationSec accumulation). */
  function tickRulesEngine(frameSec) {
    const rules = _activeRuntimeRules();
    if (!rules.length) return;
    const es = state.engineState;
    if (!es || !es.playing) return;
    const now = es.sessionSec;
    for (const rule of rules) {
      if (!rule.enabled) continue;
      const rs = _getRuntimeRuleState(rule.id);
      const condMet = evalEngineCondition(rule.condition);
      if (condMet) {
        rs.conditionHeldSec += frameSec;
        if (rs.conditionHeldSec >= rule.durationSec) {
          const cooldownElapsed = now - rs.lastFiredSec;
          if (rs.lastFiredSec === -Infinity || cooldownElapsed >= rule.cooldownSec) {
            rs.lastFiredSec = now;
            rs.conditionHeldSec = 0;
            executeRuleAction(rule);
          }
        }
      } else {
        rs.conditionHeldSec = 0;
      }
    }
  }

  // ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  // Default runtime rules — shipped as sane starters. User toggles or
  // replaces via state.runtimeRules (future UI). These run only when
  // state.runtimeRulesEnabled is true (opt-in; default off).
  // ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  DEFAULT_RUNTIME_RULES = [
    normalizeRule({
      name: 'Gentle nudge on prolonged narrator silence',
      enabled: true,
      condition: { metric: 'sinceVoiceSec', op: '>', value: 45 },
      durationSec: 0,      // condition already has time built in — fire as soon as it holds
      cooldownSec: 300,    // at most every 5 minutes — not spammy
      action: { type: 'notifyMessage', param: 'Still here — take your time.' },
    }),
    normalizeRule({
      name: 'Lower soundscape during deep work phases',
      enabled: true,
      condition: { metric: 'phaseKind', op: '==', value: 'work' },
      durationSec: 8,      // sustained 8s in a work phase before ducking
      cooldownSec: 60,
      action: { type: 'duckAudio', param: 0.18 },
    }),
    normalizeRule({
      name: 'Restore soundscape when leaving work phase',
      enabled: true,
      condition: { metric: 'phaseKind', op: '!=', value: 'work' },
      durationSec: 2,
      cooldownSec: 10,
      action: { type: 'unduckAudio', param: null },
    }),
    // Webcam-aware rules. These no-op when webcam is off (the metrics read 0
    // because the adapter doesn't push signals into the fusion engine).
    normalizeRule({
      name: 'Re-alert nudge when eyes stay closed during Wake/Reintroduction',
      enabled: true,
      condition: { metric: 'wakefulness', op: '<', value: 0.35 },
      durationSec: 15,                  // give it real time — surfacing is a process
      cooldownSec: 60,
      action: { type: 'showOnScreenText', param: 'Take your time opening your eyes.' },
    }),
    normalizeRule({
      name: 'Pause when user has left the camera view',
      enabled: true,
      condition: { metric: 'faceDetected', op: '==', value: 0 },
      durationSec: 60,                  // 60s of no face = user actually walked away
      cooldownSec: 120,
      action: { type: 'pause', param: null },
    }),
    normalizeRule({
      name: 'Gentle hint that user can close their eyes anytime',
      enabled: true,
      condition: { metric: 'attention', op: '>', value: 0.7 },
      durationSec: 600,                 // 10 minutes of staring at the screen
      cooldownSec: 1800,                // at most every 30 minutes
      action: { type: 'notifyMessage', param: 'You can close your eyes anytime.' },
    }),
  ];

  // ====================================================================
  // TRIGGER WINDOWS — time-bounded conditional triggers
  // ====================================================================
  // Complements rules-engine: rules fire repeatedly when a condition holds;
  // triggers fire once per window (opens at `atSec`, waits up to
  // `windowDurSec` for the condition, then closes). Good for time-specific
  // interactions like "at the 10-minute mark, offer a mood check".
  //
  // Trigger schema (lives alongside rules on state.runtimeTriggers):
  // {
  //   id:           string,
  //   enabled:      bool,
  //   name:         string,
  //   atSec:        number    (session-seconds when window opens)
  //   windowDurSec: number    (how long the window stays open)
  //   condition:    { metric, op, value } — same evalEngineCondition
  //   successAction: { type, param } — fires if condition becomes true within window
  //   failureAction: { type, param } — fires if window closes without condition
  //   cooldownSec:  number    (min gap before same trigger can re-arm)
  // }
  //
  // Shares the action set with rules-engine (via executeRuleAction). The 'none'
  // action type means "do nothing" — useful on failureAction when you only
  // want positive reinforcement for success.
  //
  // Adapted from /mnt/user-data/uploads/Adaptive-Session-Studio — js/trigger-windows.js
  // ====================================================================

  function _trigUid() {
    return 't_' + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8);
  }

  function normalizeTrigger(t) {
    const raw = t || {};
    const cond = raw.condition || {};
    const normalizeAct = (a) => ({
      type:  a && (RULES_VALID_ACTIONS.has(a.type) || a.type === 'none') ? a.type : 'none',
      param: a?.param ?? null,
    });
    return {
      id:           typeof raw.id === 'string' && raw.id ? raw.id : _trigUid(),
      enabled:      raw.enabled !== false,
      name:         typeof raw.name === 'string' && raw.name ? raw.name : 'Trigger',
      atSec:        Number.isFinite(raw.atSec)        ? Math.max(0, raw.atSec)        : 60,
      windowDurSec: Number.isFinite(raw.windowDurSec) ? Math.max(1, raw.windowDurSec) : 10,
      condition: {
        metric: RULES_VALID_METRICS.has(cond.metric) ? cond.metric : 'engagement',
        op:     RULES_VALID_OPS.has(cond.op)         ? cond.op     : '>=',
        value:  Number.isFinite(cond.value) || typeof cond.value === 'string' ? cond.value : 0.6,
      },
      successAction: normalizeAct(raw.successAction),
      failureAction: normalizeAct(raw.failureAction),
      cooldownSec:   Number.isFinite(raw.cooldownSec) ? Math.max(0, raw.cooldownSec) : 120,
    };
  }

  // Runtime window state per trigger id:
  // { status: 'idle'|'open'|'success'|'failed', openedAt: sessionSec, lastFiredAt: sessionSec }
  const _triggerWindowState = {};

  function _getTriggerWindowState(id) {
    if (!_triggerWindowState[id]) _triggerWindowState[id] = { status: 'idle', openedAt: 0, lastFiredAt: -Infinity };
    return _triggerWindowState[id];
  }

  function clearTriggerWindowState() {
    Object.keys(_triggerWindowState).forEach(k => delete _triggerWindowState[k]);
  }

  /** Execute a trigger action. Shares the rule action set, plus 'none' as a
   *  no-op (useful for failureAction when you want no penalty). */
  function executeTriggerAction(action, triggerName, outcome) {
    if (!action || action.type === 'none') return;
    // Adapt to executeRuleAction's shape — it expects { action: {...}, name: '...' }
    executeRuleAction({ name: `${triggerName} ${outcome}`, action });
  }

  function _activeRuntimeTriggers() {
    const t = state.runtimeTriggers;
    if (Array.isArray(t)) return t;
    return DEFAULT_RUNTIME_TRIGGERS;
  }

  /** Main tick — call after tickRulesEngine. Idempotent to missing triggers. */
  function tickTriggerWindows() {
    const triggers = _activeRuntimeTriggers();
    if (!triggers.length) return;
    const es = state.engineState;
    if (!es || !es.playing) return;
    const now = es.sessionSec;

    for (const trigger of triggers) {
      if (!trigger.enabled) continue;
      const ws = _getTriggerWindowState(trigger.id);

      if (ws.status === 'idle') {
        const cooldownOk = now - ws.lastFiredAt >= trigger.cooldownSec;
        if (now >= trigger.atSec && cooldownOk) {
          ws.status   = 'open';
          ws.openedAt = now;
        }
      }

      if (ws.status === 'open') {
        const elapsed = now - ws.openedAt;
        const condMet = evalEngineCondition(trigger.condition);
        if (condMet) {
          ws.status      = 'success';
          ws.lastFiredAt = now;
          executeTriggerAction(trigger.successAction, trigger.name, '✓');
          // Re-arm briefly — so the next atSec window can open on a repeat trigger.
          // In HNE sessions don't loop, so this is mostly for safety.
          setTimeout(() => { if (_triggerWindowState[trigger.id]) _triggerWindowState[trigger.id].status = 'idle'; }, 500);
        } else if (elapsed >= trigger.windowDurSec) {
          ws.status      = 'failed';
          ws.lastFiredAt = now;
          executeTriggerAction(trigger.failureAction, trigger.name, '✗');
          setTimeout(() => { if (_triggerWindowState[trigger.id]) _triggerWindowState[trigger.id].status = 'idle'; }, 500);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  // Default triggers — opt-in via state.runtimeRulesEnabled (shares the flag with rules).
  // Ship with one starter: a gentle mid-session check-in that fires a quiet nudge
  // if engagement is low 8 minutes in. Users can replace via state.runtimeTriggers.
  const DEFAULT_RUNTIME_TRIGGERS = [
    normalizeTrigger({
      name: 'Mid-session engagement check',
      enabled: true,
      atSec: 480,                   // 8 minutes in
      windowDurSec: 30,
      condition: { metric: 'engagement', op: '>=', value: 0.4 },
      successAction: { type: 'none', param: null },                                      // quiet success
      failureAction: { type: 'notifyMessage', param: 'Drifted? That can be part of it.' }, // gentle nudge
      cooldownSec: 999999,          // one-shot per session
    }),
  ];

  // ====================================================================
  // WEBCAM AWARENESS — local-only attention + ambient sensing
  // ====================================================================
  // Per-session opt-in. All inference runs in-browser via MediaPipe Face
  // Landmarker (lazy-loaded from CDN on first enable). Frames never leave
  // the device. No persistence — signals exist in memory until session ends.
  //
  // Signals published into state.engineState.engagement via setEngineSignal:
  //   attention   — face present + oriented toward camera (weight 0.25)
  //   wakefulness — phase-aware eye-state (weight 0.15)
  //                 CRITICAL: eyes-closed is POSITIVE during trance phases.
  //                 See _computeWakefulness for the phase mapping table.
  //
  // Separate signals (not engagement-fused):
  //   state.ambientBrightness — 0..1 room luminance, EMA-smoothed
  //   state.ambientDimScale   — 0.6..1.2 viz intensity multiplier
  //
  // See /mnt/user-data/outputs/2026-04-24-webcam-awareness-design.md
  // ====================================================================
  const WEBCAM_INFER_FPS         = 8;     // 8 inferences per second — much cheaper than RAF
  const WEBCAM_BRIGHTNESS_FPS    = 2;     // ambient sampled 2/sec — cheap and slow-changing
  const EAR_CLOSED_THRESHOLD     = 0.20;  // EAR below this = eyes closed
  const EAR_OPEN_THRESHOLD       = 0.32;  // EAR above this = eyes clearly open
  const FACE_PRESENCE_TIMEOUT_MS = 3000;  // grace period before flipping faceDetected → false
  const AMBIENT_EMA_ALPHA        = 0.05;  // ~10s time constant at 2fps
  const AMBIENT_DIM_DARK_THRESHOLD   = 0.25; // ambient < this → dim viz to 0.6
  const AMBIENT_DIM_BRIGHT_THRESHOLD = 0.70; // ambient > this → boost viz to 1.2

  // MediaPipe Face Mesh eye-landmark indices (from the 478-point face mesh).
  // Each eye uses 6 landmarks: outer corner, top-2-points, inner corner, bottom-2-points.
  // EAR (Eye Aspect Ratio) = (||p2-p6|| + ||p3-p5||) / (2 * ||p1-p4||)
  const RIGHT_EYE_IDX = [33, 160, 158, 133, 153, 144]; // user's right (image left)
  const LEFT_EYE_IDX  = [362, 385, 387, 263, 373, 380]; // user's left  (image right)

  // CDN paths — pinned version for stability. WASM + model lazy-loaded on first enable.
  const MP_VISION_VERSION = '0.10.14';
  const MP_VISION_ESM_URL = `https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@mediapipe/tasks-vision@${MP_VISION_VERSION}/+esm`;
  const MP_WASM_PATH      = `https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@mediapipe/tasks-vision@${MP_VISION_VERSION}/wasm`;
  const MP_MODEL_PATH     = 'https://storage.googleapis.com/mediapipe-models/face_landmarker/face_landmarker/float16/1/face_landmarker.task';

  let _mpFaceLandmarker = null;
  let _mpLoadPromise    = null; // de-dupe concurrent load attempts

  /** Lazy-load MediaPipe FaceLandmarker. Idempotent — returns cached instance after first load.
   *  ~3-5MB WASM + model on first call; cached by browser thereafter. */
  async function _loadFaceLandmarker() {
    if (_mpFaceLandmarker) return _mpFaceLandmarker;
    if (_mpLoadPromise)    return _mpLoadPromise;
    _mpLoadPromise = (async () => {
      const mod = await import(MP_VISION_ESM_URL);
      // jsdelivr +esm bundles MediaPipe with both named and default exports;
      // accept either shape so a future build change doesn't break us.
      const lib = mod.FaceLandmarker ? mod : (mod.default || {});
      const FaceLandmarker  = lib.FaceLandmarker;
      const FilesetResolver = lib.FilesetResolver;
      if (!FaceLandmarker || !FilesetResolver) {
        throw new Error('MediaPipe imports missing — CDN may be unreachable or version changed');
      }
      const filesetResolver = await FilesetResolver.forVisionTasks(MP_WASM_PATH);
      _mpFaceLandmarker = await FaceLandmarker.createFromOptions(filesetResolver, {
        baseOptions: { modelAssetPath: MP_MODEL_PATH, delegate: 'GPU' },
        runningMode: 'VIDEO',
        numFaces: 1,
        outputFaceBlendshapes: false,            // we don't use expressions
        outputFacialTransformationMatrixes: false,
      });
      return _mpFaceLandmarker;
    })();
    try { return await _mpLoadPromise; }
    finally { _mpLoadPromise = null; } // allow retry on transient failure
  }

  function _euclideanDist(a, b) {
    const dx = a.x - b.x, dy = a.y - b.y;
    return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
  }

  /** Eye Aspect Ratio for one eye. Returns null if landmarks missing. */
  function _eyeAspectRatio(landmarks, eyeIdx) {
    const p = eyeIdx.map(i => landmarks[i]);
    if (p.some(x => !x)) return null;
    const v1 = _euclideanDist(p[1], p[5]);
    const v2 = _euclideanDist(p[2], p[4]);
    const h  = _euclideanDist(p[0], p[3]);
    if (h < 1e-6) return null;
    return (v1 + v2) / (2 * h);
  }

  /** Phase-aware wakefulness — the most important inversion in the spec.
   *  During trance phases (settling..affirm), eyes-closed is POSITIVE signal.
   *  During wake/reintroduction, eyes-closed indicates the user hasn't fully
   *  surfaced yet (low wakefulness, may need a gentler nudge). */
  function _computeWakefulness(rawEAR, phaseKind) {
    if (rawEAR == null) return null;
    const closed = rawEAR < EAR_CLOSED_THRESHOLD;
    const open   = rawEAR > EAR_OPEN_THRESHOLD;
    switch (phaseKind) {
      case 'settling':
      case 'induction':
      case 'deepener':
      case 'work':
      case 'affirm':
        // Trance phases — closed eyes are appropriate, expected, GOOD.
        return closed ? 0.9 : (open ? 0.5 : 0.7);
      case 'lightener':
        // Transition — neutral; eyes may be on the way to opening.
        return 0.5;
      case 'wake':
        // Script is instructing eyes-open. Open = full wakefulness; closed = still drifting.
        return open ? 0.95 : (closed ? 0.3 : 0.6);
      case 'reintroduction':
        // User should be fully back. Closed eyes here = user drifted re-tranced.
        return open ? 0.95 : (closed ? 0.1 : 0.5);
      default:
        return 0.5;
    }
  }

  /** Show consent modal. Returns true (user agreed) or false (declined / cancelled).
   *  Modal text per spec §5.1 — explicit about local-only, no persistence. */
  function requestWebcamConsent() {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      const backdrop = document.createElement('div');
      backdrop.className = 'modal-backdrop visible';
      backdrop.style.zIndex = 9999;
      backdrop.innerHTML = `<div class="modal" style="max-width:480px;">
        <h3 style="margin:0 0 12px;font-size:1.05rem;font-weight:500;">Enable webcam awareness?</h3>
        <div style="font-size:0.84rem;line-height:1.55;color:var(--text-dim);">
          Your webcam will be used <strong>locally only</strong> to detect:
        </div>
        <ul style="margin:8px 0 12px 18px;padding:0;font-size:0.78rem;line-height:1.65;color:var(--text-dim);">
          <li>Whether you're present (for automatic pausing)</li>
          <li>Eye state — phase-appropriate (closed eyes are <em>good</em> during trance)</li>
          <li>Room brightness (for visualizer comfort)</li>
        </ul>
        <div style="font-size:0.76rem;color:var(--text);background:rgba(120,180,240,0.06);border:0.5px solid rgba(120,180,240,0.2);border-radius:5px;padding:10px 12px;line-height:1.55;">
          <strong style="display:block;margin-bottom:4px;">What is NOT collected:</strong>
          <span>No frames saved to disk · No data leaves this device · No identity or facial recognition</span>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-top:10px;font-size:0.72rem;color:var(--text-faint);line-height:1.55;">
          Processing happens in your browser via Google's MediaPipe (loaded from a CDN on first use, ~3–5MB WASM + model).
          You can disable anytime via the camera icon during the session. <strong>This permission applies to this session only.</strong>
        </div>
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:flex-end;gap:8px;margin-top:18px;">
          <button id="webcamConsentNo"  class="preview-btn">Not now</button>
          <button id="webcamConsentYes" class="preview-btn primary">Enable webcam</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
      document.body.appendChild(backdrop);
      const cleanup = (val) => { backdrop.remove(); resolve(val); };
      backdrop.querySelector('#webcamConsentNo')?.addEventListener('click', () => cleanup(false));
      backdrop.querySelector('#webcamConsentYes')?.addEventListener('click', () => cleanup(true));
      // Click outside to dismiss = decline
      backdrop.addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (e.target === backdrop) cleanup(false); });
    });
  }

  /** Start the webcam: getUserMedia → load MediaPipe → start inference + brightness loops.
   *  Caller is responsible for having obtained consent first. */
  async function startWebcam() {
    const w = state._webcam;
    if (w.status === 'active' || w.status === 'requesting' || w.status === 'loading') return;

    // API availability check — old browsers, insecure contexts (file://), iframes without permission.
    if (!navigator.mediaDevices?.getUserMedia) {
      w.status = 'error';
      w.errorMessage = 'getUserMedia not supported in this browser/context';
      _renderWebcamStatus();
      notify.warn('Webcam not supported in this browser');
      return;
    }

    w.status = 'requesting';
    w.errorMessage = null;
    _renderWebcamStatus();

    try {
      // Low resolution — face detection works fine at 320x240, saves CPU and bandwidth (n/a since local).
      w.stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({
        video: { width: { ideal: 320 }, height: { ideal: 240 }, facingMode: 'user' },
        audio: false,
      });

      // Hidden video element — never rendered to UI. 1px so it has dimensions for the <video> draw calls.
      if (!w.videoEl) {
        w.videoEl = document.createElement('video');
        w.videoEl.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:1px;height:1px;opacity:0;pointer-events:none;z-index:-1;';
        w.videoEl.muted = true;
        w.videoEl.autoplay = true;
        w.videoEl.playsInline = true;
        w.videoEl.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
        document.body.appendChild(w.videoEl);
      }
      w.videoEl.srcObject = w.stream;
      await w.videoEl.play().catch(() => {}); // autoplay may need user gesture; try-and-continue

      // Load MediaPipe (lazy, cached after first call)
      w.status = 'loading';
      _renderWebcamStatus();
      await _loadFaceLandmarker();

      // Start the inference + brightness loops
      w.status   = 'active';
      w.enabled  = true;
      w.lastFaceAt = 0;
      _renderWebcamStatus();
      _startWebcamLoops();
      notify.info('Webcam awareness on — local processing only');
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[webcam] start failed:', e);
      w.status = 'error';
      w.errorMessage = e?.message || String(e);
      _renderWebcamStatus();
      // User-friendly error — don't dump getUserMedia internals on the user
      if (e?.name === 'NotAllowedError')      notify.warn('Camera permission denied');
      else if (e?.name === 'NotFoundError')   notify.warn('No camera found');
      else if (e?.name === 'NotReadableError') notify.warn('Camera is in use by another application');
      else                                     notify.warn('Webcam error: ' + (e?.message || 'unknown'));
      stopWebcam();
    }
  }

  /** Stop the webcam: release stream, kill loops, clear signals.
   *  Idempotent — safe to call repeatedly. */
  function stopWebcam() {
    const w = state._webcam;
    if (w.inferTimerHandle)      { clearInterval(w.inferTimerHandle);      w.inferTimerHandle = null; }
    if (w.brightnessTimerHandle) { clearInterval(w.brightnessTimerHandle); w.brightnessTimerHandle = null; }
    if (w.stream) {
      try { w.stream.getTracks().forEach(t => t.stop()); } catch {}
      w.stream = null;
    }
    if (w.videoEl) {
      try { w.videoEl.srcObject = null; w.videoEl.remove(); } catch {}
      w.videoEl = null;
    }
    w.status        = 'idle';
    w.enabled       = false;
    w.faceDetected  = false;
    w.rawEAR        = null;
    w.motion        = 0;
    w._brightnessCanvas = null;
    w._brightnessCtx    = null;
    // Clear externally-injected engagement signals so they don't linger
    if (typeof clearEngineSignals === 'function') {
      // Surgical clear — only OUR signals; leave any other adapter's signals alone.
      // (clearEngineSignals nukes all of them; safer to delete just ours.)
      try {
        const sigs = _engineExternalSignals;
        if (sigs) { delete sigs.attention; delete sigs.wakefulness; }
      } catch {}
    }
    state.ambientBrightness = 0.5;
    state.ambientDimScale   = 1.0;
    _renderWebcamStatus();
  }

  function _startWebcamLoops() {
    const w = state._webcam;
    const inferIntervalMs      = Math.round(1000 / WEBCAM_INFER_FPS);
    const brightnessIntervalMs = Math.round(1000 / WEBCAM_BRIGHTNESS_FPS);
    w.inferTimerHandle = setInterval(() => {
      try { _tickWebcamInfer(); } catch (e) { console.warn('[webcam] infer tick failed:', e); }
    }, inferIntervalMs);
    w.brightnessTimerHandle = setInterval(() => {
      try { _tickWebcamBrightness(); } catch (e) { console.warn('[webcam] brightness tick failed:', e); }
    }, brightnessIntervalMs);
  }

  /** One face-landmark inference frame. Publishes attention + wakefulness signals. */
  function _tickWebcamInfer() {
    const w = state._webcam;
    if (w.status !== 'active' || !w.videoEl || !_mpFaceLandmarker) return;
    if (w.videoEl.readyState < 2) return; // HAVE_CURRENT_DATA — video not ready yet

    const result = _mpFaceLandmarker.detectForVideo(w.videoEl, performance.now());
    const faces  = result?.faceLandmarks || [];
    const facePresent = faces.length > 0;

    if (facePresent) {
      w.faceDetected = true;
      w.lastFaceAt   = Date.now();
      const lm = faces[0];
      const earR = _eyeAspectRatio(lm, RIGHT_EYE_IDX);
      const earL = _eyeAspectRatio(lm, LEFT_EYE_IDX);
      const ear  = (earR != null && earL != null) ? (earR + earL) / 2 : (earR ?? earL);
      w.rawEAR = ear;
    } else {
      // Don't immediately flip faceDetected — give a few frames of grace for momentary
      // occlusion (user moves head, hand passes by, blink that confuses the detector).
      if (w.lastFaceAt && Date.now() - w.lastFaceAt > FACE_PRESENCE_TIMEOUT_MS) {
        w.faceDetected = false;
        w.rawEAR = null;
      }
    }

    // Publish signals into the state-engine fusion. Weights from the design spec.
    if (typeof setEngineSignal === 'function') {
      setEngineSignal('attention', w.faceDetected ? 0.8 : 0.0, 0.25);
      const phaseKind   = state.engineState?.phaseKind || null;
      const wakefulness = _computeWakefulness(w.rawEAR, phaseKind);
      if (wakefulness != null) {
        setEngineSignal('wakefulness', wakefulness, 0.15);
      }
    }
    _renderWebcamStatus();
  }

  /** One ambient-brightness sample. Cheap — just full-frame mean luminance via tiny canvas. */
  function _tickWebcamBrightness() {
    const w = state._webcam;
    if (w.status !== 'active' || !w.videoEl || w.videoEl.readyState < 2) return;

    if (!w._brightnessCanvas) {
      // 16x12 px is enough for a stable mean — saves a lot of getImageData CPU.
      w._brightnessCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      w._brightnessCanvas.width = 16;
      w._brightnessCanvas.height = 12;
      w._brightnessCtx = w._brightnessCanvas.getContext('2d', { willReadFrequently: true });
    }
    try {
      w._brightnessCtx.drawImage(w.videoEl, 0, 0, 16, 12);
      const data = w._brightnessCtx.getImageData(0, 0, 16, 12).data;
      let sum = 0;
      for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i += 4) {
        // ITU-R BT.601 luma — fast and good enough; we don't need photometric accuracy
        sum += 0.299 * data[i] + 0.587 * data[i + 1] + 0.114 * data[i + 2];
      }
      const meanLuma = sum / (data.length / 4) / 255;

      // EMA smooth over ~10s at 2fps (alpha 0.05 with 0.5s steps ≈ 10s time constant)
      const prev = state.ambientBrightness ?? 0.5;
      state.ambientBrightness = prev + AMBIENT_EMA_ALPHA * (meanLuma - prev);

      // Map smoothed brightness → viz dim scale, with linear ramps in the transition zones
      // so the visualizer doesn't flicker between modes near the threshold boundaries.
      const b = state.ambientBrightness;
      let scale;
      if (b < AMBIENT_DIM_DARK_THRESHOLD)        scale = 0.6;
      else if (b < 0.45)                          scale = 0.6 + (b - AMBIENT_DIM_DARK_THRESHOLD) * 2.0; // 0.6 → 1.0 over 0.25..0.45
      else if (b > AMBIENT_DIM_BRIGHT_THRESHOLD)  scale = 1.2;
      else if (b > 0.55)                          scale = 1.0 + (b - 0.55) * 1.33;                      // 1.0 → 1.2 over 0.55..0.70
      else                                        scale = 1.0;
      state.ambientDimScale = scale;
    } catch (e) {
      // SecurityError if cross-origin video, NotReadableError if stream died — silent fail.
      console.warn('[webcam] brightness sample failed:', e);
    }
  }

  /** Update the status dot indicator. Called from start/stop/tick paths. */
  function _renderWebcamStatus() {
    const dot = document.getElementById('webcamStatusDot');
    if (!dot) return;
    const w = state._webcam;
    let color = 'transparent', title = 'Webcam off', opacity = 0;
    switch (w.status) {
      case 'requesting': color = 'var(--neon-amber)'; title = 'Requesting camera permission…'; opacity = 0.8; break;
      case 'loading':    color = 'var(--neon-amber)'; title = 'Loading face detection model…'; opacity = 0.8; break;
      case 'active':
        opacity = 1;
        if (w.faceDetected) { color = '#7dc87a'; title = 'Webcam active — face detected (local processing only)'; }
        else                { color = 'var(--neon-amber)'; title = 'Webcam active — no face detected'; }
        break;
      case 'error': color = '#ff6b6b'; title = 'Webcam error: ' + (w.errorMessage || 'unknown'); opacity = 0.9; break;
      case 'idle':  color = 'transparent'; title = 'Webcam off'; opacity = 0; break;
    }
    dot.style.background = color;
    dot.style.opacity = String(opacity);
    dot.title = title;
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SAFETY LAYER — consolidated runtime guards
  // ====================================================================
  // Single source of truth for runtime safety constraints. Wraps mutators
  // that can be commanded by the rules engine (setSpeechRate,
  // setSoundscapeVolume) with hard caps, so a misconfigured rule can't
  // crank speech rate to 2× or drown the narrator under loud soundscape.
  //
  // Existing photosensitivity caps (audio-reactive 3Hz burst rate limiter,
  // breathing-tempo lock) are documented here but enforced inline at their
  // visualizer points — moving them now would risk regressions.
  //
  // Adapted from /mnt/user-data/uploads/Adaptive-Session-Studio — js/safety.js
  // ====================================================================
  const SAFETY_DEFAULTS = {
    maxSpeechRate:        1.5,
    minSpeechRate:        0.6,
    maxSoundscapeVolume:  0.85,
    emergencyCooldownSec: 30,
    maxSessionMinutes:    60,
  };

  /** Read current safety config with default fallback. Pure read. */
  function getSafetyConfig() {
    return { ...SAFETY_DEFAULTS, ...(state.safetyConfig || {}) };
  }

  /** Clamp a requested speech rate to [minSpeechRate, maxSpeechRate].
   *  Used by rules-engine setSpeechRate action AND any direct setter that
   *  wants gating. NaN-safe — returns 1.0 (default) for non-finite input.
   *  Notifies if the requested value was out of range. */
  function gateSpeechRate(requested) {
    const c = getSafetyConfig();
    const r = Number(requested);
    if (!Number.isFinite(r)) return 1.0;
    const clamped = Math.max(c.minSpeechRate, Math.min(c.maxSpeechRate, r));
    if (Math.abs(clamped - r) > 0.001) {
      notify.warn(`Safety: speech rate clamped from ${r.toFixed(2)}× to ${clamped.toFixed(2)}×`);
    }
    return clamped;
  }

  /** Clamp a requested soundscape volume to [0, maxSoundscapeVolume]. */
  function gateSoundscapeVolume(requested) {
    const c = getSafetyConfig();
    const v = Number(requested);
    if (!Number.isFinite(v)) return 0;
    const clamped = Math.max(0, Math.min(c.maxSoundscapeVolume, v));
    if (Math.abs(clamped - v) > 0.001) {
      notify.warn(`Safety: soundscape volume clamped from ${Math.round(v*100)}% to ${Math.round(clamped*100)}%`);
    }
    return clamped;
  }

  /** Returns seconds remaining on emergency cooldown, or 0 if not active. */
  function getEmergencyCooldownRemaining() {
    if (!state._cooldownUntil) return 0;
    return Math.max(0, Math.ceil((state._cooldownUntil - Date.now()) / 1000));
  }

  /** Pre-flight check — call before session start. Returns null if OK or
   *  an info object [warn, message] if the user should be warned. The caller
   *  decides whether to block or just notify. */
  function checkSessionLengthSafety() {
    const c = getSafetyConfig();
    const m = getScriptMetrics(state.fullScript || '');
    if ((m.estimatedMin || 0) > c.maxSessionMinutes) {
      return {
        warn: true,
        message: `This session is estimated at ${m.estimatedMin} minutes — over the ${c.maxSessionMinutes}-minute soft cap. Consider a shorter session, or proceed if you're sure.`,
      };
    }
    return null;
  }

  /** Render the safety panel inputs from state. Idempotent — call after
   *  load, reset, or any external change. The change listeners are wired
   *  once in the init block; this just refreshes input values. */
  function _renderSafetyPanel() {
    const c = getSafetyConfig();
    const setVal = (id, v) => { const el = $(id); if (el) el.value = v; };
    setVal('safety_minSpeechRate',        c.minSpeechRate.toFixed(1));
    setVal('safety_maxSpeechRate',        c.maxSpeechRate.toFixed(1));
    setVal('safety_maxSoundscapeVolume',  Math.round(c.maxSoundscapeVolume * 100));
    setVal('safety_emergencyCooldownSec', c.emergencyCooldownSec);
    setVal('safety_maxSessionMinutes',    c.maxSessionMinutes);
  }

  /** Reset safety config to defaults. Persists immediately. */
  function _resetSafetyConfig() {
    state.safetyConfig = { ...SAFETY_DEFAULTS };
    _renderSafetyPanel();
    saveUserSettings();
    notify.info('Safety limits reset to defaults');
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SESSION MODES — preset bundles of rules + triggers + safety overrides
  // ====================================================================
  // Each mode is a coherent posture for the runtime reactivity layer. Applying
  // a mode overrides state.runtimeRules, state.runtimeTriggers, and (optionally)
  // safetyConfig fields. The 'standard' mode reverts to defaults.
  //
  // Modes don't affect the AI script itself — they shape *how* the script plays
  // (caps, nudges, ducking aggressiveness, silence tolerance). Think of it as
  // "delivery tone for the rules engine."
  //
  // Adapted from /mnt/user-data/uploads/Adaptive-Session-Studio — js/session-modes.js
  // (HNE adaptation: no intensity-ramp/dynamic-pacing yet, so modes use rules +
  //  triggers + safety overrides as their levers.)
  // ====================================================================
  const SESSION_MODES = [
    {
      id:          'standard',
      name:        'Standard',
      icon:        '○',
      description: 'Default rules and caps. Use this unless you have a specific reason to change.',
      // null = use built-in defaults (DEFAULT_RUNTIME_RULES / DEFAULT_RUNTIME_TRIGGERS / SAFETY_DEFAULTS)
      rules:           null,
      triggers:        null,
      safetyOverrides: null,
    },
    {
      id:          'deep-sleep',
      name:        'Deep Sleep',
      icon:        '🌙',
      description: 'Quiet posture for sleep-intention sessions. No nudges, aggressive ducking, low volume cap. The narrator can fade out without waking you.',
      rules: [
        // No silence-nudge — silence is the goal, not a problem.
        // Aggressive duck during work + maintain through transitions.
        {
          name: '[Deep Sleep] Soft duck across all phases',
          enabled: true,
          condition: { metric: 'voiceEnvelope', op: '<', value: 0.05 },
          durationSec: 4,
          cooldownSec: 30,
          action: { type: 'duckAudio', param: 0.10 },
        },
        {
          name: '[Deep Sleep] Restore on voice activity',
          enabled: true,
          condition: { metric: 'voiceEnvelope', op: '>', value: 0.15 },
          durationSec: 1,
          cooldownSec: 5,
          action: { type: 'unduckAudio', param: null },
        },
        // Webcam-aware: don't pause when face leaves view (sleep = closed eyes, often turned head)
      ],
      triggers: [], // no mid-session check-ins — would wake the sleeper
      safetyOverrides: {
        maxSoundscapeVolume: 0.5,    // never blast soundscape when targeting sleep
        maxSessionMinutes:   90,     // sleep sessions can run longer
      },
    },
    {
      id:          'active-practice',
      name:        'Active Practice',
      icon:        '🎯',
      description: 'For focus and learning sessions. Earlier engagement check, tighter speech rate range, more responsive feedback.',
      rules: [
        {
          name: '[Active] Silence nudge — quicker to fire',
          enabled: true,
          condition: { metric: 'sinceVoiceSec', op: '>', value: 30 },  // 30s vs default 45s
          durationSec: 0,
          cooldownSec: 180,                                              // 3min vs default 5min
          action: { type: 'notifyMessage', param: 'Still with me?' },
        },
        {
          name: '[Active] Heavy duck during work for focus',
          enabled: true,
          condition: { metric: 'phaseKind', op: '==', value: 'work' },

      ],
      triggers: [
        {

          enabled: true,

          windowDurSec: 30,

          successAction: { type: 'none', param: null },
          failureAction: { type: 'notifyMessage', param: 'Notice where attention is. No judgment.' },

        },
      ],
      safetyOverrides: {
        minSpeechRate: 0.8,    // narrower range — keeps pacing energetic
        maxSpeechRate: 1.4,
      },
    },
    {
      id:          'gentle-exploration',
      name:        'Gentle Exploration',
      icon:        '🌱',
      description: 'For first-timers, sensitive topics, or just easing in. Conservative caps, extra reassurance, no startling actions.',
      rules: [
        {
          name: '[Gentle] Reassurance after long silence',
          enabled: true,
          condition: { metric: 'sinceVoiceSec', op: '>', value: 60 },    // patient — wait a full minute
          durationSec: 0,

        },
        {

          enabled: true,

      triggers: [
        {

          condition: { metric: 'engagement', op: '>=', value: 0.3 },     // very forgiving
          successAction: { type: 'none', param: null },
          failureAction: { type: 'showOnScreenText', param: 'You\'re doing fine. Stay or step away — both are okay.' },
          cooldownSec: 999999,
        },
      ],
      safetyOverrides: {
        maxSpeechRate:        1.2,    // never push fast
        minSpeechRate:        0.7,
        maxSoundscapeVolume:  0.65,   // softer ambient
        maxSessionMinutes:    30,     // short by default
      },
    },
  ];

  /** Apply a session mode by id. Replaces runtimeRules + runtimeTriggers + merges
   *  safetyOverrides into safetyConfig. Idempotent. Persists. */
  function applySessionMode(modeId) {
    const mode = SESSION_MODES.find(m => m.id === modeId);
    if (!mode) { notify.warn(`Unknown session mode: ${modeId}`); return; }

    state.activeSessionMode = mode.id;

    // Rules: null → defaults, [] → empty list (deep sleep wants no rules), array → normalize each
    if (mode.rules === null) {
      state.runtimeRules = null; // null causes _activeRuntimeRules() to fall back to DEFAULT_RUNTIME_RULES
    } else {
      state.runtimeRules = mode.rules.map(r => normalizeRule(r));
    }
    if (mode.triggers === null) {
      state.runtimeTriggers = null;
    } else {
      state.runtimeTriggers = mode.triggers.map(t => normalizeTrigger(t));
    }

    // Safety overrides: merge into config, clamp via field-by-field rules.
    // null overrides means "leave safetyConfig alone" (mode doesn't tweak safety).
    if (mode.safetyOverrides) {
      const cur = state.safetyConfig || { ...SAFETY_DEFAULTS };
      const ov = mode.safetyOverrides;
      state.safetyConfig = {
        ...cur,
        ...(Number.isFinite(ov.maxSpeechRate)        && { maxSpeechRate:        Math.max(0.5, Math.min(2.0, ov.maxSpeechRate)) }),
        ...(Number.isFinite(ov.minSpeechRate)        && { minSpeechRate:        Math.max(0.5, Math.min(2.0, ov.minSpeechRate)) }),
        ...(Number.isFinite(ov.maxSoundscapeVolume)  && { maxSoundscapeVolume:  Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, ov.maxSoundscapeVolume)) }),
        ...(Number.isFinite(ov.emergencyCooldownSec) && { emergencyCooldownSec: Math.max(0, Math.min(300, ov.emergencyCooldownSec)) }),
