  }

  async function loadProfile() {
    try {
      let p = null;
      if (_kv) { try { p = await _kv.settings.get(PROFILE_KEY); } catch {} }
      if (!p) { const raw = localStorage.getItem(PROFILE_KEY); if (raw) p = JSON.parse(raw); }
      if (!p) return;
      // Additive migration — seed changeLog for old profiles missing the field
      _profileChangeLog = Array.isArray(p.changeLog) ? p.changeLog : [];
      applyProfileToForm(p, { save: false });
    } catch {}
  }

  /** Tracked fields for DiffBouncer coverage.
   *  type: 'text' for prose-ish fields (pct-of-chars threshold)
   *        'csv'  for list-ish fields (entry-count threshold) */
  const TRACKED_FIELDS = [
    { id: 'pfGoals',          type: 'csv'  }, // "Goals" textarea
    { id: 'pfAbout',          type: 'text' }, // "About You" freeform
    { id: 'intentionInput',   type: 'text' }, // per-session intention
    { id: 'userAffirmations', type: 'csv'  }, // newline-delimited affirmations
    { id: 'bgPromptInput',    type: 'csv'  }, // image-gen prompt tags
  ];

  function initDiffBouncers() {
    // Text/CSV field bouncers — one per TRACKED_FIELD
    TRACKED_FIELDS.forEach(({ id, type }) => {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (!el) return; // defensive — missing field means no coverage, no crash
      const bouncer = new DiffBouncer({
        source: id,
        type,
        getState: () => el.value || '',
        onCommit: (diff, _current, meta) => commitChangeLogEntry(id, type, diff, meta),
      });
      // Seed baseline from current value — hardCommit is a no-op here
      // because lastSnapshot is null and the impl returns without committing.
      bouncer.lastSnapshot = el.value || '';
      diffBouncers[id] = bouncer;
      el.addEventListener('input', () => bouncer.ping());
    });

    // Image generation — single bouncer for all image-gen events.
    // State shape is set by the bgEngine hook (Task 6).
    diffBouncers.bgImage = new DiffBouncer({
      source: 'bgImage',
      type: 'image',
      getState: () => diffBouncers.bgImage._latestState || null,
      onCommit: (diff, _current, meta) => commitChangeLogEntry('bgImage', 'image', diff, meta),
    });

    // Timeline UI — render when the Session History section opens.
    // Changelog content lives inside Session History (moved 2026-04-25);
    // listening on the parent details ensures lazy render still happens.
    document.getElementById('sessionHistoryDetails')?.addEventListener('toggle', e => {
      if (e.target.open) renderChangeLog();
    });

    console.log('[DB] diff bouncers initialized:', Object.keys(diffBouncers).length);
  }

  // HTML escape for user-generated content shown in the changelog view
  function _escDB(s) { return String(s).replace(/[<>&"']/g, c => ({ '<':'&lt;', '>':'&gt;', '&':'&amp;', '"':'&quot;', "'":'&#39;' }[c])); }

  function _relTimeDB(ts) {
    const now = Date.now();
    const d = Math.floor((now - ts) / 1000);
    if (d < 60) return 'just now';
    if (d < 3600) return Math.floor(d / 60) + 'm ago';
    if (d < 86400) return Math.floor(d / 3600) + 'h ago';
    if (d < 86400 * 2) return 'yesterday';
    if (d < 86400 * 7) return Math.floor(d / 86400) + 'd ago';
    return new Date(ts).toISOString().slice(0, 10);
  }

  function renderChangeLog() {
    const list = document.getElementById('pfChangeLogList');
    const count = document.getElementById('pfChangeLogCount');
    if (!list) return;
    const entries = _profileChangeLog || [];
    if (count) count.textContent = entries.length ? `(${entries.length})` : '';
    if (!entries.length) {
      list.innerHTML = '<div class="sublabel" style="padding:8px 4px;">no changes logged yet — edit a tracked field or generate an image.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const srcLabel = id => ({
      pfGoals: 'goals',
      pfAbout: 'about',
      intentionInput: 'intention',
      userAffirmations: 'affirmations',
      bgPromptInput: 'bg prompt',
      bgImage: 'image',
    }[id] || id);
    const html = entries.slice(0, DIFF_BOUNCE_THRESHOLDS.logCap).map(e => {
      const ts = _relTimeDB(e.ts);
      const src = srcLabel(e.source);
      let body = '';
      if (e.type === 'csv' && e.diff) {
        const addHtml = (e.diff.added || []).map(a => `<span class="cl-chip cl-add">+${_escDB(a)}</span>`).join('');
        const remHtml = (e.diff.removed || []).map(r => `<span class="cl-chip cl-rem">−${_escDB(r)}</span>`).join('');
        body = addHtml + remHtml || '<em>no entries shifted</em>';
      } else if (e.type === 'text' && e.diff) {
        const pct = Math.round((e.diff.changePct || 0) * 100);
        body = `<span class="sublabel">${pct}% changed</span> — <em>${_escDB(e.diff.preview || '')}…</em>`;
      } else if (e.type === 'image' && e.diff) {
        const tags = (e.diff.tags || []).map(t => `<span class="cl-chip">${_escDB(t)}</span>`).join('');
        body = `<div>${_escDB(e.diff.summary || '')}</div><div style="margin-top:3px;">${tags}</div>`;
      } else {
        body = '<em>(unknown entry type)</em>';
      }
      return `<div class="pf-changelog-entry"><div class="cl-head"><span class="cl-ts">${_escDB(ts)}</span> · <span class="cl-src">${_escDB(src)}</span></div><div class="cl-body">${body}</div></div>`;
    }).join('');
    list.innerHTML = html;
  }

  /** Build an AI context string from the user's profile for prompt injection */
  // ====================================================================
  // PHASE 4 SIGNALS — time-of-day picks + modality inference
  // ====================================================================
  // Two lightweight derived signals from the existing analytics store. Both
  // are read-only — they don't add new persistence, just compute over `hr`
  // (hourly distribution) + frequency maps + current settings.

  /** What persona/method does this user most often pick at the given hour?
   *  Returns null if there's not enough signal (fewer than 3 sessions in this
   *  hour bucket OR no clear winner). Cheap — runs in-memory after analytics
   *  load. Used to surface a "matches your usual hour" hint on Step 1.
   *
   *  Note: The current analytics store keeps a single hourly counter (`hr`),
   *  not a per-(hour × persona) cross-tab. So this function approximates by
   *  combining global persona popularity with the user's typical hour. If
   *  the user has substantial activity at the requested hour AND has a clear
   *  top persona, return that persona — it's the best available signal
   *  without expanding the schema.
   *
   *  @returns {Promise<{personaId?:string, methodId?:string} | null>} */
  async function getTimeOfDayPick(hour) {
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();
      if (!a) return null;
      const hourCount = (a.hr && a.hr[hour]) || 0;
      // Need a meaningful baseline — ignore single-session noise.
      if (hourCount < 3) return null;
      // Pick the user's globally most-used persona/method as the recommendation
      // for this hour. (A future schema upgrade could store hourly cross-tabs;
      // for now this is the highest-signal field.)
      const topKey = (map) => {
        let best = null, bestN = 0;
        for (const k of Object.keys(map || {})) {
          if (map[k] > bestN) { best = k; bestN = map[k]; }
        }
        return bestN >= 3 ? best : null;
      };
      const personaId = topKey(a.p);
      const methodId  = topKey(a.m);
      if (!personaId && !methodId) return null;
      return { personaId, methodId, hourCount };
    } catch (e) { return null; }
  }

  /** Conservative inference of the user's preferred sensory modality from
   *  current settings + recent usage. Returns 'visual'|'auditory'|'kinesthetic'
   *  ONLY when the signal is strong. Otherwise returns null and we say nothing.
   *
   *  Used to lightly steer AI generation: a kinesthetic user gets more body
   *  references; an auditory user gets sound-rich descriptions. Wrong
   *  inference is worse than no inference, so the bar is high.
   *
   *  Signals (each 0 or 1):
   *    visual:       text-display ON, viz-override is intense (not none/candle/colorwash),
   *                  recent methods include visual fixation patterns
   *    auditory:     text-display ON, soundscape on, audio-reactive on, voice volume high
   *    kinesthetic:  somatic-category methods dominate, breath/body-scan in usage,
   *                  webcam/biofeedback features used
   *
   *  Requires score >= 2 in a single modality AND that modality must be the
   *  clear leader (margin >= 1) to return non-null. */
  async function inferModality() {
    try {
      const scores = { visual: 0, auditory: 0, kinesthetic: 0 };
      // Visual signals
      if (state.vizOverride && !['none', 'candle', 'colorwash'].includes(state.vizOverride)) scores.visual++;
      if (state.hud?.fixationDot !== false) scores.visual++;
      // Auditory signals
      if (state.cfgTextDisplay !== false) scores.auditory++; // narration-text on suggests they want spoken reinforcement
      if (state.soundscape && state.soundscape !== 'none') scores.auditory++;
      if ((state.audioReactiveMode || 'subtle') !== 'off') scores.auditory++;
      // Kinesthetic signals — read from analytics method usage
      const a = await getAnalytics();
      if (a && a.m) {
        const SOMATIC_METHODS = new Set(['hand-heaviness', 'arm-catalepsy', 'progressive', 'body-awareness',
          'floating-body', 'glove-anesthesia', 'heartbeat-sync', 'breath-478', 'pain-dial', 'arm-drop']);
        let somaticPlays = 0, totalPlays = 0;
        for (const k of Object.keys(a.m)) {
          totalPlays += a.m[k];
          if (SOMATIC_METHODS.has(k)) somaticPlays += a.m[k];
        }
        if (totalPlays >= 5 && (somaticPlays / totalPlays) > 0.4) scores.kinesthetic += 2;
      }
      // Pick the leader if it's clear
      const entries = Object.entries(scores).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
      const [winner, wScore] = entries[0];
      const [, runner] = entries[1];
      if (wScore < 2 || (wScore - runner) < 1) return null;
      return winner;
    } catch (e) { return null; }
  }

  /** Cached inference — refreshed asynchronously after each session and at
   *  init. `getProfileContext` is sync (called during prompt assembly), so
   *  it reads from this cache rather than awaiting. Stale by at most one
   *  session, which is fine. */
  state._inferredModality = state._inferredModality || null;
  async function refreshInferredModality() {
    try { state._inferredModality = await inferModality(); }
    catch { state._inferredModality = null; }
  }
  // Refresh once at module load so first session has signal if usage is heavy
  setTimeout(() => { refreshInferredModality().catch(() => {}); }, 1500);

  function getProfileContext() {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('getProfileContext returning empty — Smart Director off');
      return '';
    }
    const p = getProfile();
    const parts = [];
    // Only pass the subject's name to the AI when the user has opted in.
    if (p.name && p.useFirstName) parts.push(`The subject's name is ${p.name}. You may address them by name occasionally; do not overuse it.`);
    if (p.pronouns) parts.push(`Pronouns: ${p.pronouns}.`);
    if (p.age) parts.push(`Age range: ${p.age}.`);
    if (p.experience) parts.push(`Experience: ${p.experience}.`);
    if (p.about) parts.push(`About the subject: ${p.about}.`);
    if (p.appearance) parts.push(`Appearance: ${p.appearance}.`);
    if (p.goals) parts.push(`Goals: ${p.goals}.`);

    // Phase 4: inferred sensory modality. Only surfaced when inference is
    // confident (see inferModality). Wrong guidance is worse than silence.
    if (state._inferredModality) {
      const guidance = {
        visual:       'Lean into visual descriptions (light, color, distance, scenes the user can see in their mind).',
        auditory:     'Lean into auditory descriptions (sounds, rhythms, the texture of the voice itself, named sounds).',
        kinesthetic:  'Lean into bodily sensation (weight, warmth, breath, where in the body the experience lands).',
      }[state._inferredModality];
      if (guidance) parts.push(`Inferred preferred modality: ${state._inferredModality}. ${guidance}`);
    }

    // Recent change signals from the diff-bounce log — gives the director
    // a time-aware view of what the user's been exploring lately.
    const srcLabel = id => ({ pfGoals:'goals', pfAbout:'about', intentionInput:'intention', userAffirmations:'affirmations', bgPromptInput:'bg-prompt', bgImage:'image-gen' }[id] || id);
    try {
      const recent = (_profileChangeLog || []).slice(0, 10);
      if (recent.length) {
        const lines = recent.map(e => {
          const rel = _relTimeDB(e.ts);
          if (e.type === 'csv' && e.diff) {
            const add = (e.diff.added || []).slice(0, 3).join(',');
            const rem = (e.diff.removed || []).slice(0, 3).join(',');
            const bits = [];
            if (add) bits.push('+' + add);
            if (rem) bits.push('-' + rem);
            return `${rel} · ${srcLabel(e.source)}: ${bits.join(' ')}`.trim();
          } else if (e.type === 'text' && e.diff) {
            return `${rel} · ${srcLabel(e.source)}: ${Math.round((e.diff.changePct || 0) * 100)}% text change`;
          } else if (e.type === 'image' && e.diff) {
            const tags = (e.diff.tags || []).slice(0, 4).join(',');
            const sum = e.diff.summary || (tags ? `[${tags}]` : '');
            return `${rel} · image: ${sum}`;
          }
          return `${rel} · ${srcLabel(e.source)}`;
        }).filter(Boolean);
        if (lines.length) parts.push('Recent changes: ' + lines.join(' | '));
      }
    } catch (e) { /* never break context assembly */ }

    const result = parts.length > 0 ? '\nSUBJECT PROFILE: ' + parts.join(' ') : '';
    sdLog('getProfileContext built', { fieldCount: parts.length, charCount: result.length });
    return result;
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // FRESHNESS INJECTION — combinatorial anchor phrases via Perchance DSL
  // ====================================================================
  // Breaks AI mode-collapse by injecting a small set of profile-filtered
  // sensory anchors into sharedContext on each script generation. The DSL
  // picker is stateless; rotation memory (last-used phrases) lives here.
  // ====================================================================
  const FRESHNESS_COUNT = 4;              // phrases per script generation
  const FRESHNESS_MIN_TAGS = 0;           // min profile tags required (0 = always)
  const FRESHNESS_ROTATION_CAP = 30;      // max "recent" entries remembered
  let _recentAnchors = [];                // FIFO buffer of recently-picked phrases

  function deriveProfileTags() {
    const tags = new Set();
    const p = getProfile();
    // Experience → pacing tag
    if (p.experience === 'beginner') tags.add('slow');
    if (p.experience === 'advanced') tags.add('dense');
    // Goals text → simple keyword map (deliberately broad)
    const goals = (p.goals || '').toLowerCase();
    if (/(sleep|insomnia|bedtime)/.test(goals)) tags.add('sleep');
    if (/(calm|relax|anxiety|stress)/.test(goals)) tags.add('calm');
    if (/(focus|concentration|productivity)/.test(goals)) tags.add('focus');
    if (/(creative|art|write)/.test(goals)) tags.add('creative');
    if (/(confidence|self)/.test(goals)) tags.add('confidence');
    // Intention → imagery tag (intention text comes from the intention input)
    const intention = ($('intentionInput')?.value || '').toLowerCase();
    if (/(water|ocean|river|rain)/.test(intention)) tags.add('water');
    if (/(warm|sun|fire|glow)/.test(intention)) tags.add('warm');
    if (/(cool|cold|ice|winter)/.test(intention)) tags.add('cool');
    // Aesthetic preferences from the diff-bounce image log, if populated
    try {
      const imgEntries = (_profileChangeLog || []).filter(e => e.source === 'bgImage').slice(0, 5);
      imgEntries.forEach(e => (e.diff?.tags || []).forEach(t => tags.add(t)));
    } catch {}
    return [...tags];
  }

  function buildFreshnessBlock() {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) return '';
    if (typeof root === 'undefined' || !root.freshSeeds || typeof root.freshSeeds.pick !== 'function') return '';
    try {
      const tags = deriveProfileTags();
      if (tags.length < FRESHNESS_MIN_TAGS) return '';
      const phrases = root.freshSeeds.pick({
        profileTags: tags,
        n: FRESHNESS_COUNT,
        excludeSet: _recentAnchors,
      });
      if (!phrases || !phrases.length) return '';
      // Update rotation state (FIFO cap)
      _recentAnchors.push(...phrases);
      if (_recentAnchors.length > FRESHNESS_ROTATION_CAP) {
        _recentAnchors = _recentAnchors.slice(-FRESHNESS_ROTATION_CAP);
      }
      sdLog('freshness block built', { count: phrases.length, tags });
      return `\nOPTIONAL ANCHORS (use only if they fit the moment — ignore otherwise):\n${phrases.map(p => '  • ' + p).join('\n')}`;
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[freshSeeds] pick failed:', e);
      return '';
    }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // LIVING PROFILE + DIRECTOR BRIEF
  // ====================================================================
  // Merges profile + memory + adaptive + history into one on-demand view, then
  // runs rule-based logic over it to produce a session brief. No new persistence
  // layer — source stores own their data.
  //
  // IMPORTANT: director logic stays RULE-BASED. AI-inferred clinical judgment is
  // a slippery slope this app should not take.

  /**
   * Build a unified "living profile" by merging user-edited profile + AI-observed
   * memory summaries + adaptive signals + recent session snapshot.
   *
   * Pure read — does not write anywhere. Returns `null` when Smart Director is
   * off OR when any underlying read fails.
   *
   * @returns {Promise<object|null>}
   */
  async function buildLivingProfile() {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('buildLivingProfile skipped — Smart Director off');
      return null;
    }
    try {
      const stated = getProfile();
      const memory = await getMemory();
      const adaptive = await getAdaptive();
      const history = ((await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || []).map(normalizeHistoryEntry);
      const analytics = await getAnalytics();

      // Recent mood trajectory — last 5 completed sessions with both pre+post scores.
      // Index 0 = most recent. A negative value = user felt worse after the session.
      const moodSessions = history.filter(s => s.completed && s.preMood != null && s.postMood != null).slice(0, 5);
      const recentMoodDeltas = moodSessions.map(s => s.postMood - s.preMood);
      const avgRecentMoodDelta = recentMoodDeltas.length > 0
        ? recentMoodDeltas.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / recentMoodDeltas.length
        : null;

      // Completion rate over last 10 — captures "bailing" patterns earlier than
      // the lifetime rate from analytics.comp which dilutes with history.
      const recent10 = history.slice(0, 10);
      const completionRate = recent10.length > 0
        ? recent10.filter(s => s.completed).length / recent10.length
        : null;

      // Average self-rated depth in recent sessions — helps calibrate next session.
      const recentDepths = history.slice(0, 5).map(s => s.depth).filter(d => d != null);
      const avgRecentDepth = recentDepths.length > 0
        ? recentDepths.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / recentDepths.length
        : null;

      // Top preference signals from analytics (what the user reaches for most).
      const topKey = (map) => {
        const entries = Object.entries(map || {});
        if (!entries.length) return null;
        return entries.sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0][0];
      };

      const living = {
        version: 1,
        updatedAt: Date.now(),
        stated: {
          name: stated.name,
          useFirstName: stated.useFirstName,
          pronouns: stated.pronouns,
          age: stated.age,
          experience: stated.experience,
          about: stated.about,
          appearance: stated.appearance,
          goals: stated.goals,
        },
        observed: {
          longTermProfile: memory.longTermProfile || '',
          rollingPatterns: memory.rollingWindow || '',
          digestCount: memory.sessionDigests?.length || 0,
        },
        adaptive: {
          traits: adaptive.traits || {},
          difficulty: adaptive.difficulty || {},
          memorySummary: adaptive.memorySummary || '',
          topPersona: topKey(analytics.p),
          topMethod: topKey(analytics.m),
          topIntention: topKey(analytics.i),
        },
        snapshot: {
          sessionCount: history.length,
          completedCount: history.filter(s => s.completed).length,
          emergencyExitCount: analytics.comp?.emergency || 0,
          completionRate,
          recentMoodDeltas,
          avgRecentMoodDelta,
          avgRecentDepth,
          lastSessionAt: history[0]?.date || null,
          daysSinceLast: history[0]?.date
            ? Math.floor((Date.now() - history[0].date) / 86400000)
            : null,
        },
      };

      sdLog('buildLivingProfile', living);
      return living;
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('buildLivingProfile failed:', e);
      return null;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Compute a structured Director Brief from the living profile. Rule-based —
   * every recommendation includes a plain-English reason that can be surfaced
   * to the user (Pass 3).
   *
   * Cold-start (fewer than 3 completed sessions): returns a brief with
   * `coldStart: true` and no active recommendations, so the AI falls back to
   * defaults rather than pretending expertise the app hasn't earned.
   *
   * @param [object|null] living     output of buildLivingProfile()
   * @param [object]       session   { persona, method, intention, length }
   * @returns [object|null]
   */
  function computeDirectorBrief(living, session = {}) {
    if (!living) return null;
    const snap = living.snapshot;
    // User-adjustable bias, -3..+3. Negative = lean cautious (easier triggers,
    // stricter caps); positive = lean forward (harder triggers, looser caps).
    // Clamped defensively in case the setting is stale or out of range.
    const bias = Math.max(-3, Math.min(3, Math.round(Number(state.directorBias) || 0)));
    const brief = {
      generatedAt: Date.now(),
      bias,
      forSession: {
        persona: session.persona || null,
        method: session.method || null,
        intention: session.intention || null,
        length: session.length || null,
      },
      coldStart: false,
      recoveryMode: false,
      recommendations: {}, // { suggestedDepth, suggestedLength, skipIntensification, maxDepth, preferBreath }
      warnings: [],        // user-facing flags
      reasoning: [],       // plain-English rationale (one entry per rule that fired)
    };

    // Bias-adjusted thresholds. The math is deliberately simple — each step
    // moves the threshold by a human-meaningful unit, so moving one notch
    // produces an observable shift without flipping the app's personality.
    const coldStartLimit     = Math.max(0, 3 - bias);           // B=-3: 6, 0: 3, +3: 0 (no cold start)
    const recoveryMoodLimit  = -2 - bias * 0.5;                  // B=-3: -0.5 (easy), 0: -2, +3: -3.5 (hard)
    const completionFloor    = 0.5 - bias * 0.05;                // B=-3: 0.65, 0: 0.5, +3: 0.35
    const daysSinceRentry    = 14 + bias * 3;                    // B=-3: 5, 0: 14, +3: 23
    const positivePacingFloor = 1.5 - bias * 0.3;                // B=-3: 2.4 (harder to praise), +3: 0.6 (easier)
    sdLog('computeDirectorBrief thresholds', { bias, coldStartLimit, recoveryMoodLimit, completionFloor, daysSinceRentry, positivePacingFloor });

    // --- Cold start -----------------------------------------------------
    if (snap.completedCount < coldStartLimit) {
      brief.coldStart = true;
      brief.reasoning.push(
        snap.completedCount === 0
          ? 'No completed sessions yet — using defaults and keeping things grounded.'
          : `Only ${snap.completedCount} completed session${snap.completedCount === 1 ? '' : 's'} so far — still calibrating.`
      );
      sdLog('computeDirectorBrief: cold start', brief);
      return brief;
    }

    // --- Recovery mode: 3+ consecutive strongly negative mood deltas -----
    // A "strongly negative" delta is ≤ recoveryMoodLimit on the 1–10 mood scale.
    const lastThree = snap.recentMoodDeltas.slice(0, 3);
    if (lastThree.length === 3 && lastThree.every(d => d <= recoveryMoodLimit)) {
      brief.recoveryMode = true;
      brief.recommendations.suggestedDepth = 'light';
      brief.recommendations.suggestedLength = 'short';
      brief.recommendations.skipIntensification = true;
      brief.warnings.push('Last 3 sessions ended with notable mood decline.');
      brief.reasoning.push(`Recovery mode triggered — recent sessions trended mood-negative (threshold ≤ ${recoveryMoodLimit}). Recommending a gentler, shorter session and skipping intensification.`);
      sdLog('computeDirectorBrief: recovery mode', brief);
      return brief;
    }

    // --- Low completion rate → shorter sessions -------------------------
    if (snap.completionRate != null && snap.completionRate < completionFloor) {
      brief.recommendations.suggestedLength = 'short';
      brief.warnings.push(`Recent completion rate is ${Math.round(snap.completionRate * 100)}%.`);
      brief.reasoning.push(`Recent completion rate is low (${Math.round(snap.completionRate * 100)}% < ${Math.round(completionFloor * 100)}%) — suggest a shorter session to rebuild the habit.`);
    }

    // --- Emergency-exit history → cap depth -----------------------------
    // Capped in both directions — emergency exits are a hard safety signal that
    // bias shouldn't fully suppress. At bias +3, still cap if 3+ exits on short history.
    const emergencyCap = bias >= 3 ? 3 : 2;
    if (snap.emergencyExitCount >= emergencyCap && snap.completedCount < 10) {
      brief.recommendations.maxDepth = 'medium';
      brief.reasoning.push(`${snap.emergencyExitCount} emergency exits on record with limited completed history — capping suggested depth at medium.`);
    }

    // --- Beginner cap ---------------------------------------------------
    // Beginner cap is a safety feature; bias can soften it but not skip entirely.
    if (living.stated.experience === 'beginner' && bias < 3) {
      brief.recommendations.maxDepth = brief.recommendations.maxDepth || 'medium';
      brief.reasoning.push('Self-identifies as beginner — capping suggested depth at medium.');
    }

    // --- Positive reinforcement — current pacing works ------------------
    if (snap.avgRecentMoodDelta != null && snap.avgRecentMoodDelta >= positivePacingFloor) {
      brief.reasoning.push(`Average mood delta is +${snap.avgRecentMoodDelta.toFixed(1)} — current pacing is working; stay the course.`);
    }

    // --- Long gap since last session ------------------------------------
    if (snap.daysSinceLast != null && snap.daysSinceLast >= daysSinceRentry) {
      brief.recommendations.suggestedDepth = brief.recommendations.suggestedDepth || 'light';
      brief.reasoning.push(`${snap.daysSinceLast} days since last session (≥ ${daysSinceRentry}) — treat as a re-entry and keep this one gentle.`);
    }

    sdLog('computeDirectorBrief', brief);
    return brief;
  }

  /**
   * Turn a Director Brief into a short prompt block for AI injection. Stays
   * under ~300 characters so it rarely gets dropped by trimToTokenBudget.
   *
   * Appends a tone directive derived from the Director calibration bias so
   * the AI's language leans cautious or forward in sympathy with the user's
   * manual correction — even when no rule fires.
   */
  function formatDirectorBriefForPrompt(brief) {
    if (!brief) return '';
    const parts = [];
    const bias = brief.bias || 0;

    if (brief.coldStart) {
      const coldBase = 'Early practitioner — follow defaults and keep the session welcoming and grounded.';
      const toneNote = _toneDirectiveFromBias(bias);
      return '\nDIRECTOR BRIEF: ' + coldBase + (toneNote ? ' ' + toneNote : '');
    }

    if (brief.recoveryMode) {
      parts.push('Recovery mode — keep this session lighter and shorter than usual. No intensification, no peak-state work. Gentle, supportive, reassuring tone.');
    }

    const r = brief.recommendations;
    const directives = [];
    if (r.suggestedDepth) directives.push(`aim for ${r.suggestedDepth} depth`);
    if (r.maxDepth)       directives.push(`do not exceed ${r.maxDepth} depth`);
    if (r.suggestedLength)directives.push(`favor a ${r.suggestedLength}-length pacing`);
    if (r.skipIntensification && !brief.recoveryMode) directives.push('skip intensification language');
    if (directives.length) parts.push('Adjustments: ' + directives.join('; ') + '.');

    const toneNote = _toneDirectiveFromBias(bias);
    if (toneNote) parts.push(toneNote);

    if (parts.length === 0) return '';
    return '\nDIRECTOR BRIEF: ' + parts.join(' ');
  }

  /** Bias → plain-English tone directive for the AI. Empty at bias=0. */
  function _toneDirectiveFromBias(bias) {
    if (bias <= -2) return 'Tone calibration: favor grounded, careful, gently reassuring language. Avoid pushing intensity or urgency.';
    if (bias === -1) return 'Tone calibration: lean slightly cautious and unhurried.';
    if (bias === 1)  return 'Tone calibration: lean slightly forward with warm momentum.';
    if (bias >= 2)  return 'Tone calibration: favor forward-momentum, energizing language. Trust the practitioner to engage fully with deeper work.';
    return '';
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // TOKEN SUBSTITUTION — Perchance-chat-style \{\{placeholder\}\} system
  // ====================================================================
  /**
   * Replaces double-curly-brace tokens in text with real values. Inspired by
   * Perchance AI Character Chat's \{\{user\}\} / \{\{char\}\} convention so users
   * writing or editing hypnosis scripts have a familiar substitution syntax.
   *
   * Supported tokens:
   *   \{\{user\}\}        -> the listener's first name (if checkbox on) or "you" (generic)
   *   \{\{nar\}\} / \{\{guide\}\} / \{\{persona\}\}
   *                   -> the active persona's name ("Aria", "Dr. Vale", etc.)
   *   \{\{intention\}\}   -> the short intention phrase from the intention step
   *   \{\{affirmation\}\} -> one of the user's affirmations (picked for variety —
   *                     multiple \{\{affirmation\}\} tokens rotate through the list)
   *
   * Unresolved tokens are left alone so a downstream pass (or the AI itself)
   * can handle them. Called both pre-prompt (so AI sees resolved values in
   * the generation context) and pre-TTS (so user edits with live tokens work).
   *
   * @param [string] text   Source text possibly containing \{\{...\}\} tokens.
   * @param [object] [opts] Overrides: { user, persona, intention, affirmations[] }.
   * @returns [string]
   */
  function resolveTokens(text, opts = {}) {
    if (!text || typeof text !== 'string') return text || '';
    if (text.indexOf('\u007B\u007B') === -1) return text; // fast path — no tokens present

    // Profile → \{\{user\}\}
    const profile = opts.profile || getProfile();
    const useName = !!profile.useFirstName && !!profile.name;
    const userValue = opts.user != null ? String(opts.user) : (useName ? profile.name : 'you');

    // Persona → \{\{nar\}\} \{\{guide\}\} \{\{persona\}\}
    let narValue = opts.persona;
    if (narValue == null) {
      try { narValue = getPersona()?.name || ''; } catch { narValue = ''; }
    }
    narValue = narValue || 'the narrator';

    // Intention → \{\{intention\}\}
    let intentionValue = opts.intention;
    if (intentionValue == null) {
      intentionValue = ($('intentionInput')?.value || '').trim();
    }

    // Affirmations → \{\{affirmation\}\} (rotates through list)
    let affirmArr = opts.affirmations;
    if (!Array.isArray(affirmArr)) {
      const raw = ($('userAffirmations')?.value || '').trim();
      affirmArr = raw ? raw.split(/\r?\n/).map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];
    }
    let affirmIdx = 0;
    const nextAffirm = () => {
      if (!affirmArr.length) return '';
      const v = affirmArr[affirmIdx % affirmArr.length];
      affirmIdx++;
      return v;
    };

    // Replace using a single-pass regex. Token names are case-insensitive and
    // tolerate surrounding whitespace: \{\{ user \}\} works the same as \{\{user\}\}.
    return text.replace(/\{\{\s*([a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)\s*\}\}/g, (match, rawName) => {
      const name = rawName.toLowerCase();
      switch (name) {
        case 'user':        return userValue;
        case 'nar':
        case 'guide':
        case 'persona':     return narValue;
        case 'intention':   return intentionValue || match; // leave if empty
        case 'affirmation': return nextAffirm() || match;
        default:            return match; // unknown token — pass through for upstream handling
      }
    });
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // USAGE ANALYTICS — compact incremental aggregation (O(1) storage)
  // ====================================================================
  const ANALYTICS_KEY = 'stillness_analytics_v3';

  /** Get or initialize the analytics store */
  async function getAnalytics() {
    try {
      const data = await idbGet(ANALYTICS_KEY) || await idbGet('stillness_analytics_v2');
      if (data) return normalizeAnalyticsData(data);
    } catch {}
    return {
      v: 3,
      // Frequency maps: { id: count }
      p: {},   // persona usage
      m: {},   // method usage
      i: {},   // intention type usage
      s: {},   // soundscape usage
      z: {},   // visual effect usage
      ln: {},  // session length usage
      am: {},  // affirmation mode usage
      vc: {},  // narrator voice usage
      // Time patterns
      hr: new Array(24).fill(0),  // hourly distribution (0-23)
      dw: new Array(7).fill(0),   // day-of-week (0=Sun..6=Sat)
      // Mood & completion
      mood: { preSum: 0, postSum: 0, deltaSum: 0, n: 0, postN: 0 },
      comp: { total: 0, finished: 0, emergency: 0 },
      dur: { sum: 0, n: 0 },
      shape: { phaseSum: 0, workSum: 0, affirmSum: 0, n: 0 },
      // Settings usage (running sums for averages)
      cfg: { rateSum: 0, pitchSum: 0, volSum: 0, droneSum: 0, n: 0 },
      // Feature flags: which features the user has tried
      feat: 0, // bitmask: 1=affirmations 2=programs 4=custom-persona 8=skip-to-script 16=timing-fixer 32=share 64=backup 128=double-induction
      // Timestamp
      ts: Date.now(),
    };
  }

  /** Record a completed session into the analytics store */
  async function recordAnalytics(record, wasEmergency) {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('recordAnalytics skipped — Smart Director off');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();

      // Frequency tallies (increment counters)
      const inc = (map, key) => { if (key) map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + 1; };
      inc(a.p, record.personaId);
      inc(a.m, record.methodId);
      inc(a.i, record.intention);
      inc(a.s, record.soundscape);
      inc(a.z, record.vizOverride || state.vizOverride || 'auto');
      inc(a.ln, record.length);
      inc(a.am, record.affirmationMode || 'woven');
      inc(a.vc, record.voiceName || 'default');

      // Time patterns
      const d = new Date(record.date);
      a.hr[d.getHours()] = (a.hr[d.getHours()] || 0) + 1;
      a.dw[d.getDay()] = (a.dw[d.getDay()] || 0) + 1;

      // Mood tracking
      if (record.preMood != null) {
        a.mood.preSum += record.preMood;
        a.mood.n++;
      }

      // Completion
      a.comp.total++;
      if (wasEmergency) a.comp.emergency++;
      else if (record.completed) a.comp.finished++;

      // Duration
      if (record.durationSec > 0) {
        a.dur.sum += record.durationSec;
        a.dur.n++;
      }

      // Settings averages
      a.cfg.rateSum += (record.speechRate || 0.65);
      a.cfg.pitchSum += (record.voicePitch || 0.85);
      a.cfg.volSum += (record.voiceVolume ?? 1.0);
      a.cfg.droneSum += (record.droneVolume ?? 0.35);
      a.cfg.n++;

      const metrics = record.metrics || {};
      a.shape.phaseSum += metrics.phaseCount || (Array.isArray(record.phaseOrder) ? record.phaseOrder.length : 0);
      a.shape.workSum += record.workBlockCount || metrics.workBlocks || 0;
      a.shape.affirmSum += metrics.affirmBlocks || 0;
      a.shape.n++;

      a.ts = Date.now();
      await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
      // Phase 4: refresh inferred modality so the next session's prompt has
      // an updated read. Fire-and-forget — never block the analytics write.
      refreshInferredModality().catch(() => {});
    } catch(e) { console.error('Analytics write failed:', e); }
  }

  /** Update post-session mood in analytics */
  async function recordPostMood(postVal) {
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();
      a.mood.postSum += postVal;
      a.mood.deltaSum += postVal - (state._preMood ?? 5);
      a.mood.postN = (a.mood.postN || 0) + 1; // separate counter — not every session fills post-mood
      await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
    } catch {}
  }

  /** Set a feature-used flag (bitmask) */
  async function markFeatureUsed(bit) {
    try {
      const a = await getAnalytics();
      if (!(a.feat & bit)) {
        a.feat |= bit;
        await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
      }
    } catch {}
  }

  // Feature bit constants
  const FEAT = { AFFIRMATIONS: 1, PROGRAMS: 2, CUSTOM_PERSONA: 4, SKIP_SCRIPT: 8, TIMING_FIX: 16, SHARE: 32, BACKUP: 64, DOUBLE_INDUCT: 128 };

  /** Rebuild analytics from remaining history — called after deletes to keep data consistent */
  async function rebuildAnalytics(historyArr) {
    try {
      const existing = await getAnalytics();
      const feat = existing.feat || 0; // preserve feature flags
      const a = { v: 3, p: {}, m: {}, i: {}, s: {}, z: {}, ln: {}, am: {}, vc: {},
        hr: new Array(24).fill(0), dw: new Array(7).fill(0),
        mood: { preSum: 0, postSum: 0, deltaSum: 0, n: 0, postN: 0 },
        comp: { total: 0, finished: 0, emergency: 0 },
        dur: { sum: 0, n: 0 }, shape: { phaseSum: 0, workSum: 0, affirmSum: 0, n: 0 }, cfg: { rateSum: 0, pitchSum: 0, volSum: 0, droneSum: 0, n: 0 },
        feat, ts: Date.now() };
      const inc = (map, key) => { if (key) map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + 1; };
      for (const r of historyArr) {
        inc(a.p, r.personaId); inc(a.m, r.methodId); inc(a.i, r.intention);
        inc(a.s, r.soundscape); inc(a.z, r.vizOverride || 'auto'); inc(a.ln, r.length); inc(a.am, r.affirmationMode || 'woven'); inc(a.vc, r.voiceName || 'default');
        const d = new Date(r.date); a.hr[d.getHours()]++; a.dw[d.getDay()]++;
        if (r.preMood != null) { a.mood.preSum += r.preMood; a.mood.n++; }
        if (r.postMood != null) { a.mood.postSum += r.postMood; a.mood.deltaSum += (r.postMood - (r.preMood ?? 5)); a.mood.postN = (a.mood.postN || 0) + 1; }
        a.comp.total++;
        if (r.completed) a.comp.finished++;
        else a.comp.emergency++; // history entries without completed=true were emergency-ended
        if (r.durationSec > 0) { a.dur.sum += r.durationSec; a.dur.n++; }
        a.cfg.rateSum += (r.speechRate || 0.65); a.cfg.pitchSum += (r.voicePitch || 0.85);
        a.cfg.volSum += (r.voiceVolume ?? 1.0); a.cfg.droneSum += (r.droneVolume ?? 0.35); a.cfg.n++;
        const metrics = r.metrics || {};
        a.shape.phaseSum += metrics.phaseCount || (Array.isArray(r.phaseOrder) ? r.phaseOrder.length : 0);
        a.shape.workSum += r.workBlockCount || metrics.workBlocks || 0;
        a.shape.affirmSum += metrics.affirmBlocks || 0;
        a.shape.n++;
      }
      await idbSet(ANALYTICS_KEY, a);
    } catch(e) { console.error('Analytics rebuild failed:', e); }
  }

  /** Derive insights from analytics — top preferences, patterns */
  function deriveInsights(a) {
    const topKey = obj => Object.entries(obj).sort((a,b) => b[1] - a[1])[0]?.[0] || null;
    const topN = (obj, n) => Object.entries(obj).sort((a,b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, n).map(e => e[0]);
    const avgMood = a.mood.n > 0 ? (a.mood.preSum / a.mood.n).toFixed(1) : null;
    // avgPost and avgDelta use postN (count of sessions where post-mood was filled).
    // a.mood.n tracks pre-mood fills, which can be much higher — using it here would under-estimate.
    const postN = a.mood.postN || 0;
    const avgPost = postN > 0 && a.mood.postSum > 0 ? (a.mood.postSum / postN).toFixed(1) : null;
    const avgDelta = postN > 0 ? (a.mood.deltaSum / postN).toFixed(1) : null;
    const avgDur = a.dur.n > 0 ? Math.round(a.dur.sum / a.dur.n) : 0;
    const peakHour = a.hr.indexOf(Math.max(...a.hr));
    const peakDay = a.dw.indexOf(Math.max(...a.dw));
    const dayNames = ['Sunday','Monday','Tuesday','Wednesday','Thursday','Friday','Saturday'];
    return {
      favPersona: topKey(a.p), favMethod: topKey(a.m), favSoundscape: topKey(a.s),
      favIntention: topKey(a.i), favViz: topKey(a.z), favLength: topKey(a.ln),
      topPersonas: topN(a.p, 3), topMethods: topN(a.m, 3),
      avgPreMood: avgMood, avgPostMood: avgPost, avgImprovement: avgDelta,
      avgDurationSec: avgDur, completionRate: a.comp.total > 0 ? Math.round(a.comp.finished / a.comp.total * 100) : 0,
      peakHour, peakDayName: dayNames[peakDay] || '—',
      totalSessions: a.comp.total,
      avgSpeechRate: a.cfg.n > 0 ? (a.cfg.rateSum / a.cfg.n).toFixed(2) : null,
      avgPhaseCount: a.shape?.n > 0 ? (a.shape.phaseSum / a.shape.n).toFixed(1) : null,
      avgWorkBlocks: a.shape?.n > 0 ? (a.shape.workSum / a.shape.n).toFixed(1) : null,
      favAffirmationMode: topKey(a.am || {}),
      favVoice: topKey(a.vc || {}),
      featuresUsed: Object.entries(FEAT).filter(([,bit]) => a.feat & bit).map(([name]) => name.toLowerCase().replace('_',' ')),
    };
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // ADAPTIVE INTELLIGENCE SYSTEM — Phases 1–9
  // Observe → Infer → Adapt → Reinforce → Evolve
  // ====================================================================
  const ADAPTIVE_KEY = 'stillness_adaptive_v1';

  /** Default adaptive profile (~300 bytes in IDB) */
  function defaultAdaptive() {
    return {
      v: 1,
      // Phase 2 — hidden profile traits (0–1 normalized)
      traits: {
        compliance: 0.5,      // finishes sessions?
        sensitivity: 0.5,     // mood responds to sessions?
        stability: 0.5,       // consistent improvement?
        noveltySeeking: 0.5,  // explores vs repeats?
        depthTolerance: 0.5,  // handles long/deep?
        controlPref: 0.5,     // authoritative (1) vs gentle (0)
        sensoryAudio: 0.5,    // uses soundscapes?
        sensoryVisual: 0.5,   // uses visuals?
      },
      // Phase 3 — reward-weighted preferences { id: weight }
      w: { p: {}, m: {}, s: {}, ln: {} },
      // Phase 4 — AI memory summary (updated every 5 sessions)
      memorySummary: '',
      memorySessCount: 0,  // sessions since last summary
      // Phase 6 — difficulty ramp
      difficulty: 0.3,  // 0=gentle 1=deep
      // Phase 7 — equilibrium
      recoveryMode: false,
      // Timestamp
      ts: 0,
    };
  }

  async function getAdaptive() {
    try { const d = await idbGet(ADAPTIVE_KEY); if (d?.v === 1) return d; } catch {}
    return defaultAdaptive();
  }

  // ── Phase 1: Derived signals ──
  function deriveSignals(analytics, history) {
    const a = analytics, h = history || [];
    const clamp = (v, lo = 0, hi = 1) => Math.max(lo, Math.min(hi, v));
    const compRate = a.comp.total > 0 ? a.comp.finished / a.comp.total : 0.5;
    const postN = a.mood.postN || 0; // only sessions where user filled post-mood
    const avgDelta = postN > 0 ? a.mood.deltaSum / postN : 0;
    const emergRate = a.comp.total > 0 ? a.comp.emergency / a.comp.total : 0;
    // Mood variance from last 10 sessions
    const recent = h.filter(s => s.preMood != null && s.postMood != null).slice(0, 10);
    const deltas = recent.map(s => s.postMood - s.preMood);
    const deltaVar = deltas.length > 1 ? deltas.reduce((s, d) => s + Math.pow(d - avgDelta, 2), 0) / deltas.length : 1;
    // Entropy of method usage (variety)
    const mEntries = Object.values(a.m || {});
    const mTotal = mEntries.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) || 1;
    const mEntropy = -mEntries.reduce((s, v) => { const p = v / mTotal; return s + (p > 0 ? p * Math.log2(p) : 0); }, 0);
    const maxEntropy = Math.log2(Math.max(mEntries.length, 1)) || 1;
    // Average session length normalized (0=micro, 1=marathon)
    const lenMap = { micro: 0, quick: 0.15, short: 0.3, medium: 0.45, long: 0.6, extended: 0.75, deep: 0.88, marathon: 1 };
    const lenEntries = Object.entries(a.ln || {});
    const lenTotal = lenEntries.reduce((s, [, v]) => s + v, 0) || 1;
    const avgLen = lenEntries.reduce((s, [k, v]) => s + (lenMap[k] ?? 0.5) * v, 0) / lenTotal;
    // Control preference — ratio of authoritarian persona usage
    // IDs must match BUILTIN_PERSONAS entries with category 'authoritarian'
    const authPersonas = ['commander','headmistress','interrogator','drill-instructor','dominatrix','surgeon'];
    const authCount = authPersonas.reduce((s, id) => s + (a.p[id] || 0), 0);
    const totalPersona = Object.values(a.p || {}).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) || 1;
    // Soundscape & visual usage rates
    const soundNone = (a.s?.none || 0) / (a.comp.total || 1);
    const vizAuto = (a.z?.auto || 0) / (a.comp.total || 1);
    return {
      completionRate: compRate,
      avgImprovement: clamp(avgDelta / 5 + 0.5),
      moodVariance: clamp(1 - deltaVar / 10),
      noveltyEntropy: clamp(mEntropy / maxEntropy),
      depthNorm: clamp(avgLen),
      controlRatio: clamp(authCount / totalPersona),
      emergencyRate: emergRate,
      audioUsage: clamp(1 - soundNone),
      visualUsage: clamp(1 - vizAuto),
    };
  }

  // ── Phase 2: Update hidden profile traits ──
  function updateTraits(traits, sig) {
    const lerp = (old, target, rate = 0.15) => old + (target - old) * rate;
    return {
      compliance:     lerp(traits.compliance, sig.completionRate),
      sensitivity:    lerp(traits.sensitivity, sig.avgImprovement),
      stability:      lerp(traits.stability, sig.moodVariance),
      noveltySeeking: lerp(traits.noveltySeeking, sig.noveltyEntropy),
      depthTolerance: lerp(traits.depthTolerance, sig.depthNorm),
      controlPref:    lerp(traits.controlPref, sig.controlRatio),
      sensoryAudio:   lerp(traits.sensoryAudio, sig.audioUsage),
      sensoryVisual:  lerp(traits.sensoryVisual, sig.visualUsage),
    };
  }

  // ── Phase 3: Reward function + weight update ──
  function computeReward(record, wasEmergency) {
    const delta = (record.postMood ?? 5) - (record.preMood ?? 5);
    return delta + (record.completed ? 1 : -1) - (wasEmergency ? 2 : 0);
  }

  function updateWeights(w, record, reward) {
    const decay = 0.98;
    const apply = (map, key) => { if (!key) return; for (const k in map) map[k] *= decay; map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + reward; };
    apply(w.p, record.personaId);
    apply(w.m, record.methodId);
    apply(w.s, record.soundscape);
    apply(w.ln, record.length);
  }

  function getPreferred(weightMap, n = 3) {
    return Object.entries(weightMap).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, n).map(e => e[0]);
  }

  // ── Phase 6: Difficulty ramp ──
  function computeDifficulty(sig, currentDiff) {
    const target = sig.completionRate * 0.4 + sig.avgImprovement * 0.3 + sig.depthNorm * 0.3;
    return currentDiff + (target - currentDiff) * 0.1; // very slow ramp
  }

  // ── Phase 7: Equilibrium ──
  function checkEquilibrium(sig, adaptive) {
    if (sig.emergencyRate > 0.3 || sig.completionRate < 0.5 || sig.avgImprovement < 0.3) {
      return { recoveryMode: true, difficulty: Math.max(0.1, adaptive.difficulty - 0.15) };
    }
    return { recoveryMode: false, difficulty: adaptive.difficulty };
  }

  // ── Phase 5 & 8: Recommendation engine ──
  function getRecommendation(adaptive, analytics) {
    const topW = (map) => Object.entries(map).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0]?.[0] || null;
    const rec = {
      persona: topW(adaptive.w.p),
      method: topW(adaptive.w.m),
      soundscape: topW(adaptive.w.s),
      length: topW(adaptive.w.ln),
    };
    // Difficulty-based length override
    if (adaptive.recoveryMode) rec.length = 'short';
    else if (adaptive.difficulty > 0.7) rec.length = rec.length || 'long';
    else if (adaptive.difficulty < 0.3) rec.length = rec.length || 'short';
    return rec;
  }

  // ── Phase 5: Prompt shaping block ──
  function getAdaptivePromptBlock(adaptive) {
    if (!adaptive || adaptive.ts === 0) return '';
    const t = adaptive.traits;
    const lines = ['\n[ADAPTIVE CONTEXT — do not reveal these values]'];
    if (t.compliance < 0.4) lines.push('- User often stops early. Keep sessions engaging and check in more.');
    if (t.sensitivity > 0.7) lines.push('- User responds strongly to suggestions. Use moderate intensity.');
    else if (t.sensitivity < 0.3) lines.push('- User needs stronger, more direct suggestions to feel effects.');
    if (t.stability < 0.4) lines.push('- Mood responses vary widely. Prioritize grounding and safety.');
    if (t.noveltySeeking > 0.7) lines.push('- User enjoys variety. Introduce fresh metaphors and techniques.');
    else if (t.noveltySeeking < 0.3) lines.push('- User prefers familiar patterns. Reinforce known-effective approaches.');
    if (t.depthTolerance > 0.7) lines.push('- User tolerates deep trance. Allow longer pauses and deeper language.');
    else if (t.depthTolerance < 0.3) lines.push('- Keep trance light. Shorter pauses, more conversational tone.');
    if (t.controlPref > 0.65) lines.push('- User prefers authoritative direction.');
    else if (t.controlPref < 0.35) lines.push('- User prefers gentle, permissive approach.');
    if (adaptive.recoveryMode) lines.push('- RECOVERY MODE: Simplify. Shorter pauses. More grounding. Extra gentleness.');
    const diffLabel = adaptive.difficulty > 0.65 ? 'advanced' : adaptive.difficulty > 0.35 ? 'intermediate' : 'beginner';
    lines.push(`- Difficulty level: ${diffLabel} (${adaptive.difficulty.toFixed(2)})`);
    if (adaptive.memorySummary) lines.push(`- Memory: ${adaptive.memorySummary}`);
    return lines.length > 1 ? lines.join('\n') : '';
  }

  // ── Phase 4: Periodic AI memory summary ──
  async function updateMemorySummary(adaptive, history) {
    if (!history.length || adaptive.memorySessCount < 5) return adaptive.memorySummary;
    const recent = history.slice(0, 8).map(s => `${s.guide}/${s.method} ${s.length} mood:${s.preMood ?? '?'}→${s.postMood ?? '?'} ${s.completed ? '✓' : '✗'}`).join('; ');
    try {
      // route through hardened aiGenerate wrapper (consistent HTTP/empty-text handling).
      const data = await aiGenerate(
        `You are analyzing a hypnosis user's recent sessions. Write a 1-2 sentence behavioral summary noting: what works best, what to avoid, emotional trajectory. Be concise and clinical.\n\nRecent sessions: ${recent}\n\nPrevious summary: ${adaptive.memorySummary || 'none'}\n\nNew summary:`,
        { stopSequences: ['\n\n'] }
      );
      if (!data || data.stopReason === 'error') return adaptive.memorySummary;
      const text = (data.generatedText || '').trim().slice(0, 250);
      return text || adaptive.memorySummary;
    } catch { return adaptive.memorySummary; }
  }

  // Master update — called after each completed session
  async function updateAdaptiveProfile(sessionRecord, wasEmergency) {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('updateAdaptiveProfile skipped — Smart Director off');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const adaptive = await getAdaptive();
      const analytics = await getAnalytics();
      const history = ((await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || []).map(normalizeHistoryEntry);
      // Phase 1: signals
      const sig = deriveSignals(analytics, history);
      // Phase 2: update traits
      adaptive.traits = updateTraits(adaptive.traits, sig);
      // Phase 3: reward + weights
      const reward = computeReward(sessionRecord, wasEmergency);
      updateWeights(adaptive.w, sessionRecord, reward);
      // Phase 6: difficulty
      adaptive.difficulty = computeDifficulty(sig, adaptive.difficulty);
      // Phase 7: equilibrium
      const eq = checkEquilibrium(sig, adaptive);
      adaptive.recoveryMode = eq.recoveryMode;
      adaptive.difficulty = eq.difficulty;
      // Phase 4: memory (every 5 sessions)
      adaptive.memorySessCount = (adaptive.memorySessCount || 0) + 1;
      if (adaptive.memorySessCount >= 5) {
        adaptive.memorySummary = await updateMemorySummary(adaptive, history);
        adaptive.memorySessCount = 0;
      }
      adaptive.ts = Date.now();
      await idbSet(ADAPTIVE_KEY, adaptive);
    } catch(e) { console.error('Adaptive update failed:', e); }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // STEP MANAGEMENT
  // ====================================================================
  function validateStep(n) {
    if (n === 1) return !!getPersona();
    if (n === 2) return !!getMethod();
    if (n === 3) {
      const skipCraft = ['trance', 'sleep'].includes(state.intentionType);
      return !!state.craftedSuggestion || skipCraft;
    }
    if (n === 4) return true;
    if (n === 5) return true;
    if (n === 6) return !!state.fullScript;
    return true;
  }

  function clearGeneratedScriptUi() {
    state.fullScript = null;
    state.parsedScript = null;
    state.generatedPhaseOrder = [];
    state.scriptSections = [];
    if (typeof _scriptEditedSinceGen !== 'undefined') _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;
    if ($('scriptText')) $('scriptText').value = '';
    if ($('scriptStats')) $('scriptStats').innerHTML = '';
    if ($('scriptPreview')) $('scriptPreview').classList.remove('visible');
    if ($('phaseEditorPanel')) $('phaseEditorPanel').style.display = 'none';
    if ($('genProgress')) $('genProgress').style.display = 'none';
    if ($('scriptBuildProgress')) $('scriptBuildProgress').style.display = 'none';
    if ($('generateScriptBtn')) showEl('generateScriptBtn', true);
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // EXTERNAL AI ROUTER — wraps Perchance AI, Anthropic, OpenAI
  // ====================================================================
  async function aiGenerate(instruction, opts = {}) {
    const provider = state.extAiProvider || 'perchance';
    // Helper — ensure a returned object always has a usable shape and
    // surfaces empty/failed generations as errors rather than silent empty
    // strings that propagate into scripts.
    const asResult = (text, stopReason, note) => {
      const t = (text || '').trim();
      if (!t || stopReason === 'error') return { generatedText: '', stopReason: 'error', _note: note || 'empty or errored' };
      return { generatedText: t, stopReason: stopReason || 'stop' };
    };
    if (provider === 'anthropic' && state._extAiKey) {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'x-api-key': state._extAiKey, 'anthropic-version': '2023-06-01', 'anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access': 'true' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ model: opts.model || 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514', max_tokens: opts.maxTokens || 2048, messages: [{ role: 'user', content: instruction }] }),
        });
        if (!res.ok) {
          console.warn(`Anthropic API HTTP ${res.status}, falling back to Perchance`);
          // fall through to Perchance below
        } else {
          const data = await res.json();
          if (data.error) {
            console.warn('Anthropic API returned error:', data.error);
          } else {
            const text = data.content?.[0]?.text || '';
            const stop = data.stop_reason === 'end_turn' || data.stop_reason === 'stop_sequence' ? 'stop'
              : data.stop_reason === 'max_tokens' ? 'max_tokens' : 'stop';
            const result = asResult(text, stop, 'anthropic empty');
            if (result.stopReason !== 'error') return result;
          }
        }
      } catch (e) { console.warn('Anthropic API failed, falling back to Perchance:', e); }
    }
    if (provider === 'openai' && state._extAiKey) {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${state._extAiKey}` },
          body: JSON.stringify({ model: opts.model || 'gpt-4o-mini', messages: [{ role: 'user', content: instruction }], max_tokens: opts.maxTokens || 2048 }),
        });
        if (!res.ok) {
          console.warn(`OpenAI API HTTP ${res.status}, falling back to Perchance`);
        } else {
          const data = await res.json();
          if (data.error) {
            console.warn('OpenAI API returned error:', data.error);
          } else {
            const text = data.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || '';
            const finish = data.choices?.[0]?.finish_reason;
            const stop = finish === 'stop' ? 'stop' : finish === 'length' ? 'max_tokens' : 'stop';
            const result = asResult(text, stop, 'openai empty');
            if (result.stopReason !== 'error') return result;
          }
        }
      } catch (e) { console.warn('OpenAI API failed, falling back to Perchance:', e); }
    }
    // Default: Perchance AI
    if (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.aiTextPlugin) {
      try {
        // Merge defensive chat-format guards ('\n\n[[' and '\n[[') into whatever
        // stop sequences the caller passed. Some models occasionally emit the
        // [[Speaker]]: chat format even when not requested — this catches that.
        // Per perchance-api §14 checklist. Set-dedupe so we don't pass duplicates.
        const userStops = opts.stopSequences || ['\n\n\n'];
        const stopSequences = Array.from(new Set([...userStops, '\n\n[[', '\n[[']));
        const data = await root.aiTextPlugin({ ...opts, instruction, stopSequences, hideStartWith: true });
        if (!data || data.stopReason === 'error') return asResult('', 'error', 'perchance ai error');
        return asResult(data.generatedText, data.stopReason, 'perchance empty');
      } catch (e) { console.warn('Perchance AI threw:', e); return asResult('', 'error', 'perchance threw'); }
    }
    return asResult('', 'error', 'no provider available');
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // METRICS HISTORY — daily rolling aggregates
  // ====================================================================
  // Per-day session aggregates independent of the per-session log. Session
  // log holds the last 50 sessions; this holds the last 180 calendar days
  // with sessions grouped. Feeds Smart Director with time-series shape that
  // memory digests don't have.
  //
  // DayMetric shape (one entry per calendar date):
  //   {
  //     date:                 'YYYY-MM-DD',
  //     sessionCount:         n,
  //     totalRuntimeSec:      n,
  //     completedCount:       n,
  //     interruptedCount:     n,
  //     emergencyExitCount:   n,
  //     intentionMix:         { sleep: n, calm: n, focus: n, ... },
  //     methodMix:            { 'method-id': n, ... },
  //     personaMix:           { 'persona-id': n, ... },
  //     avgPostMood:          0..10 | null,
  //     avgMoodDelta:         signed | null,
  //     avgDepth:             1..10 | null,
  //     // Transient accumulators (stripped on save, rebuilt from samples on load)
  //     _moodSamples:         [n, ...],
  //     _deltaSamples:        [n, ...],
  //     _depthSamples:        [n, ...],
  //     source:               'app' | 'app+import:<n>'
  //   }
  //
  // Adapted from /mnt/user-data/uploads/Adaptive-Session-Studio — js/metrics-history.js
  // ====================================================================
  const METRICS_HISTORY_KEY     = 'hne_metrics_history_v1';
  const METRICS_RETAIN_DAYS     = 180;

  let _metricsDays = null; // DayMetric[] sorted newest-first once loaded
  const metricsHistoryReady = (async () => {
    try { _metricsDays = (await idbGet(METRICS_HISTORY_KEY)) || []; }
    catch { _metricsDays = []; }
    if (!Array.isArray(_metricsDays)) _metricsDays = [];
  })();

  function _metricsDateStr(ts) {
    const d = new Date(ts);
    return `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')}`;
  }

  function _metricsEmptyDay(date, source = 'app') {
    return {
      date, source,
      sessionCount:        0,
      totalRuntimeSec:     0,
      completedCount:      0,
      interruptedCount:    0,
      emergencyExitCount:  0,
      intentionMix:        {},
      methodMix:           {},
      personaMix:          {},
      avgPostMood:         null,
      avgMoodDelta:        null,
      avgDepth:            null,
      _moodSamples:        [],
      _deltaSamples:       [],
      _depthSamples:       [],
    };
  }

  async function _saveMetricsHistory() {
    if (!_metricsDays) return;
    // Prune entries older than retainDays from the live cache too —
    // safe because old days' transient accumulators carry no future value.
    const cutoff = new Date();
    cutoff.setDate(cutoff.getDate() - METRICS_RETAIN_DAYS);
    const cutStr = _metricsDateStr(cutoff);
    _metricsDays = _metricsDays.filter(d => d.date >= cutStr);
    // Strip transient accumulator fields for the IDB payload.
    // Keep them in-memory so further same-day sessions can extend averages
    // accurately without restarting from scratch.
    const forStorage = _metricsDays.map(({ _moodSamples, _deltaSamples, _depthSamples, ...d }) => d);
    try { await idbSet(METRICS_HISTORY_KEY, forStorage); } catch {}
  }

  /**
   * Record a finished session into the day's aggregate. Called from finishSession.
   * Idempotent on repeat calls for the same record only if id is supplied —
   * but we don't bother with dedupe since finishSession is the single caller.
   */
  async function recordSessionInMetricsHistory(record, completionState) {
    await metricsHistoryReady;
    if (!record || !_metricsDays) return;
    const date = _metricsDateStr(record.date || Date.now());
    let day = _metricsDays.find(d => d.date === date);
    if (!day) {
      day = _metricsEmptyDay(date, 'app');
      _metricsDays.unshift(day);
    }
    // Defensive: rebuild transient arrays if the day was loaded from disk
    // (where they were stripped). Future same-day sessions get accurate
    // running averages even after a page reload mid-day.
    if (!day._moodSamples)  day._moodSamples  = day.avgPostMood  != null ? [day.avgPostMood]  : [];
    if (!day._deltaSamples) day._deltaSamples = day.avgMoodDelta != null ? [day.avgMoodDelta] : [];
    if (!day._depthSamples) day._depthSamples = day.avgDepth     != null ? [day.avgDepth]     : [];

    day.sessionCount++;
    day.totalRuntimeSec += record.durationSec || 0;

    if (completionState === 'completed')           day.completedCount++;
    else if (completionState === 'emergency')      day.emergencyExitCount++;
    else                                           day.interruptedCount++;

    // Mix counters — keys come from the session record verbatim
    if (record.intention)       day.intentionMix[record.intention]   = (day.intentionMix[record.intention]   || 0) + 1;
    if (record.methodId)        day.methodMix[record.methodId]       = (day.methodMix[record.methodId]      || 0) + 1;
    if (record.personaId)       day.personaMix[record.personaId]     = (day.personaMix[record.personaId]    || 0) + 1;

    // Post-mood / depth may be null at session-end (only set after post-checkin).
    // updateMetricsHistoryWithPostCheckin() patches these later if available.
    if (Number.isFinite(record.postMood)) {
      day._moodSamples.push(record.postMood);
      day.avgPostMood = +(day._moodSamples.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / day._moodSamples.length).toFixed(2);
      if (Number.isFinite(record.preMood)) {
        const delta = record.postMood - record.preMood;
        day._deltaSamples.push(delta);
        day.avgMoodDelta = +(day._deltaSamples.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / day._deltaSamples.length).toFixed(2);
      }
    }
    if (Number.isFinite(record.depth)) {
      day._depthSamples.push(record.depth);
      day.avgDepth = +(day._depthSamples.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / day._depthSamples.length).toFixed(2);
    }

    await _saveMetricsHistory();
  }

  /**
   * Patch today's metric with post-checkin data. Called when the user submits
   * the post-screen mood + depth check-in. Adds to the day's running averages
   * (the session was already counted at finishSession time, this just enriches
   * the per-day stats with the post-checkin signals).
   */
  async function updateMetricsHistoryWithPostCheckin({ postMood, preMood, depth }) {
    await metricsHistoryReady;
    if (!_metricsDays || !_metricsDays.length) return;
    const today = _metricsDateStr(Date.now());
    const day = _metricsDays.find(d => d.date === today);
    if (!day) return;
    // Guard against the same post-checkin being submitted twice (the slider's
    // input event can fire on a draft change AND a final value). We only add
    // one sample per call — duplicates within a session will inflate the
    // running average toward the latest value, which is fine.
    if (!day._moodSamples)  day._moodSamples  = [];
    if (!day._deltaSamples) day._deltaSamples = [];
    if (!day._depthSamples) day._depthSamples = [];
    if (Number.isFinite(postMood)) {
      day._moodSamples.push(postMood);
      day.avgPostMood = +(day._moodSamples.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / day._moodSamples.length).toFixed(2);
      if (Number.isFinite(preMood)) {
        const delta = postMood - preMood;
        day._deltaSamples.push(delta);
        day.avgMoodDelta = +(day._deltaSamples.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / day._deltaSamples.length).toFixed(2);
      }
    }
    if (Number.isFinite(depth)) {
      day._depthSamples.push(depth);
      day.avgDepth = +(day._depthSamples.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / day._depthSamples.length).toFixed(2);
    }
    await _saveMetricsHistory();
  }

  /** Returns DayMetric[] newest-first, capped to maxDays days. */
  async function getDailyMetricsHistory(maxDays = METRICS_RETAIN_DAYS) {
    await metricsHistoryReady;
    return (_metricsDays || []).slice(0, maxDays);
  }

  /** Compute trend signals from recent days for the Smart Director.
   *  Returns null when there's not enough data for any signal to be meaningful. */
  async function getMetricsTrendSummary(opts = {}) {
    const windowDays = opts.windowDays || 7;
    const compareDays = opts.compareDays || 14;
    const days = await getDailyMetricsHistory(windowDays + compareDays);
    if (days.length < 3) return null;
    const recent = days.slice(0, windowDays);
    const prior  = days.slice(windowDays, windowDays + compareDays);

    const sum = (arr, key) => arr.reduce((a, d) => a + (d[key] || 0), 0);
    const avgNonNull = (arr, key) => {
      const vals = arr.map(d => d[key]).filter(v => Number.isFinite(v));
      return vals.length ? vals.reduce((a,b) => a+b, 0) / vals.length : null;
    };

    const recentSessions  = sum(recent, 'sessionCount');
    const recentCompleted = sum(recent, 'completedCount');
    const priorSessions   = sum(prior, 'sessionCount');
    const priorCompleted  = sum(prior, 'completedCount');

    if (recentSessions === 0) return null;

    const recentCompletionRate = recentSessions ? recentCompleted / recentSessions : null;
    const priorCompletionRate  = priorSessions  ? priorCompleted  / priorSessions  : null;
    const completionDelta = (recentCompletionRate != null && priorCompletionRate != null)
      ? recentCompletionRate - priorCompletionRate
      : null;

    return {
      windowDays,
      recentSessionCount:  recentSessions,
      recentCompletionRate,
      completionDelta,
      avgPostMood:    avgNonNull(recent, 'avgPostMood'),
      avgMoodDelta:   avgNonNull(recent, 'avgMoodDelta'),
      avgDepth:       avgNonNull(recent, 'avgDepth'),
      avgRuntimeSec:  recentSessions ? sum(recent, 'totalRuntimeSec') / recentSessions : null,
    };
  }

  /** Wipe metrics history (linked from the existing Profile reset path) */
  async function clearMetricsHistory() {
    _metricsDays = [];
    try { await idbDel(METRICS_HISTORY_KEY); } catch {}
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // 3-TIER HIERARCHICAL MEMORY SYSTEM
  // ====================================================================
  const MEMORY_KEY = 'stillness_memory_v1';
  async function getMemory() {
    const m = await idbGet(MEMORY_KEY);
    return m || { sessionDigests: [], rollingWindow: '', longTermProfile: '', lastRollingAt: 0, lastProfileAt: 0 };
  }
  async function saveMemory(m) { await idbSet(MEMORY_KEY, m); }

  // Tier 1: Per-session script digest (called in finishSession)
  async function digestSessionScript(script, record) {
    if (!script || script.length < 100) return null;
    const truncated = script.slice(0, 2000);
    const instruction = `Summarize this hypnosis session script in 2-3 sentences. Note: key imagery/metaphors, specific suggestions delivered, induction method, emotional tone. Be clinical and specific — this feeds a personalization system.

TIP: Ensure summaries use full, natural, readable sentences with correct grammar.
NOTE: Don't append commentary or word counts. Just do the task and end your response.

Script excerpt:
${truncated}

Session: guide=${record.guide || '?'}, method=${record.method || '?'}, mood Δ=${(record.postMood ?? 5) - (record.preMood ?? 5)}, depth=${record.depth ?? '?'}/10

Summary:`;
    try {
      const data = await aiGenerate(instruction, { stopSequences: ['\n\n', '\n---'] });
      if (data.stopReason === 'error') return null;
      return (data.generatedText || '').trim().replace(/\n+/g, ' ').replace(/---$/, '').trim().slice(0, 300);
    } catch { return null; }
  }

  // Tier 2: Rolling window summary (every 5 sessions)
  async function updateRollingMemory(memory) {
    if (memory.sessionDigests.length - memory.lastRollingAt < 5) return;
    const recent = memory.sessionDigests.slice(0, 10).map(d => d.digest).filter(Boolean).join('\n- ');
    if (!recent) return;
    const instruction = `You are analyzing a hypnosis user's recent session summaries. Write a 3-4 sentence behavioral analysis: what imagery/methods produce the best results, what to emphasize in future sessions, what to avoid. Previous analysis: "${memory.rollingWindow || 'none'}"

Recent sessions:
- ${recent}

Updated analysis (full, natural, readable sentences with correct grammar):`;
    try {
      const data = await aiGenerate(instruction, { stopSequences: ['\n\n'] });
      if (data.stopReason !== 'error') {
        memory.rollingWindow = (data.generatedText || '').trim().replace(/\n+/g, ' ').trim().slice(0, 500);
        memory.lastRollingAt = memory.sessionDigests.length;
      }
    } catch {}
  }

  // Tier 3: Long-term profile (every 15 sessions)
  async function updateLongTermProfile(memory) {
    if (memory.sessionDigests.length - memory.lastProfileAt < 15) return;
    const profile = getProfileContext();
    const instruction = `Write a ~150 word practitioner profile for a hypnosis user based on their data. Note: primary use case, best methods/guides, imagery preferences, depth patterns, session length preference, key insights about what works.

Profile data: ${profile}
Rolling analysis: ${memory.rollingWindow || 'none'}
Total sessions: ${memory.sessionDigests.length}

Practitioner profile (full, natural sentences):`;
    try {
      const data = await aiGenerate(instruction, { stopSequences: ['\n\n\n'] });
      if (data.stopReason !== 'error') {
        memory.longTermProfile = (data.generatedText || '').trim().slice(0, 600);
        memory.lastProfileAt = memory.sessionDigests.length;
      }
    } catch {}
  }

  // Master memory update — called after each completed session
  async function updateSessionMemory(script, record) {
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      sdLog('updateSessionMemory skipped — Smart Director off');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const memory = await getMemory();
      const digest = await digestSessionScript(script, record);
      if (digest) {
        const entry = { sessionId: record.date, date: record.date, digest, depth: record.depth, moodDelta: (record.postMood ?? 5) - (record.preMood ?? 5) };
        memory.sessionDigests.unshift(entry);
        while (memory.sessionDigests.length > 30) memory.sessionDigests.pop();
        // also persist an embedding vector so future sessions can
        // retrieve semantically relevant digests (not just recent ones).
        // Guarded — silent no-op if embedTexts isn't available in this browser.
        embedAndStoreDigest(entry.sessionId, digest).catch(() => {});
      }
      await updateRollingMemory(memory);
      await updateLongTermProfile(memory);
      await saveMemory(memory);
    } catch (e) { console.error('Memory update failed:', e); }
  }

  function resetWizardForNewSession(opts = {}) {
    const preserveSelections = opts.preserveSelections !== false;
    state.currentStep = 1;
    state.stepsCompleted = { 1: false, 2: false, 3: false, 4: false, 5: false, 6: false };
    state._skippedToScript = false;
    state.abortFlag = false;
    state.paused = false;
    state.craftedSuggestion = null;
    // Reset pre-session check-in so prior session's values don't leak forward
    state._preMood = 5;
    state._preTension = 5;
    state._preEnergy = 5;
    document.querySelectorAll('.mood-emoji.selected').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('selected'));
    const tEl = $('preTensionSlider'); if (tEl) tEl.value = 5;
    const tVal = $('preTensionVal'); if (tVal) tVal.textContent = '5';
    const eEl = $('preEnergySlider'); if (eEl) eEl.value = 5;
    const eVal = $('preEnergyVal'); if (eVal) eVal.textContent = '5';
    if (!preserveSelections) {
      state.selectedPersonaId = 'driver';
      state.selectedMethodId = 'highway';
      state.intentionType = 'trigger';
      state.length = 'medium';
      $('intentionInput').value = '';
      // Apply adaptive recommendations if available
      applyAdaptiveRecommendations();
    }
    clearGeneratedScriptUi();
    switchScreen('setup-wizard');
    goToStep(1);
    updateStepUI();
  }

  async function applyAdaptiveRecommendations() {
    try {
      const adaptive = await getAdaptive();
      const analytics = await getAnalytics();
      // Need at least 3 completed sessions for recommendations to be meaningful.
      // (Previously compared adaptive.ts — a Date.now() timestamp — against the literal 3,
      // which was always false after any session.)
      if (!adaptive || !analytics || (analytics.comp?.total || 0) < 3) return;
      const rec = getRecommendation(adaptive, analytics);
      if (rec.persona && state.personas.find(p => p.id === rec.persona)) state.selectedPersonaId = rec.persona;
      if (rec.method && METHODS.find(m => m.id === rec.method)) state.selectedMethodId = rec.method;
      if (rec.length) { state.length = rec.length; const el = $('lengthSelect'); if (el) el.value = rec.length; }
      if (rec.soundscape) { state.soundscape = rec.soundscape; state.droneEnabled = rec.soundscape !== 'none'; const el = $('soundscapeSelect'); if (el) el.value = rec.soundscape; }
      renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); renderMethodGrid(); renderMethodDetail();
    } catch(e) { console.debug('Adaptive recommendations skipped:', e); }
  }

  function goToStep(n) {
    if (n < 1 || n > TOTAL_STEPS) return;
    // Forward direction: validate current step
    if (n > state.currentStep) {
      for (let i = state.currentStep; i < n; i++) {
        if (!validateStep(i)) { return; }
        state.stepsCompleted[i] = true;
      }
    }
    // Going backward from a skip clears the skipped state
    if (n < state.currentStep && state._skippedToScript) {
      state._skippedToScript = false;
    }
    // Leaving Step 1 → clear the ephemeral persona chat history (Phase 3).
    // Chat is preview-only by design; users coming back to Step 1 start fresh.
    if (state.currentStep === 1 && n !== 1 && typeof clearAllPersonaChats === 'function') {
      clearAllPersonaChats();
    }
    state.currentStep = n;
    // Stop all previews when leaving the Configure step
    if (typeof _stopAllPreviews === 'function') _stopAllPreviews();
    updateStepUI();
    if (n === 5) { renderConfigSummary(); }
    if (n === 6) { refreshSummary(); showEl('generateScriptBtn', true); }
    window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });

    // Accessibility: announce step change and move focus
    const stepNames = { 1: 'Choose Your Guide', 2: 'Choose Your Method', 3: 'Set Your Intention', 4: 'Add Your Own Affirmations', 5: 'Configure the Session', 6: 'Generate Your Session' };
    const announce = $('ariaStepAnnounce');
    if (announce) announce.textContent = `Step ${n} of ${TOTAL_STEPS}: ${stepNames[n] || ''}`;
    // Move focus to step heading
    const heading = document.querySelector(`.step-content[data-step="${n}"] .step-title`);
    if (heading) { heading.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1'); heading.focus(); }
  }

  function updateStepUI() {
    // Content
    document.querySelectorAll('.step-content').forEach(el => {
      el.classList.toggle('active', parseInt(el.dataset.step) === state.currentStep);
    });
    // Stepper circles
    document.querySelectorAll('.step-item').forEach(el => {
      const n = parseInt(el.dataset.step);
      const isSkipped = state._skippedToScript && n < state.currentStep && !state.stepsCompleted[n];
      el.classList.toggle('current', n === state.currentStep);
      el.classList.toggle('completed', n < state.currentStep && !isSkipped);
      el.classList.toggle('skipped', isSkipped);
      el.classList.toggle('clickable', n < state.currentStep && !isSkipped);
    });
    // Step values under circles — show "Skipped" for bypassed steps
    if (state._skippedToScript) {
      for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
        const el = $('stepValue' + i);
        if (el && !state.stepsCompleted[i]) el.textContent = 'skipped';
      }
    } else {
      $('stepValue1').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[1] ? getPersona().name : '';
      $('stepValue2').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[2] ? getMethod().name : '';
      let s3 = '';
      if (state.stepsCompleted[3]) {
        if (state.craftedSuggestion) s3 = 'crafted ✓';
        else if (state.intentionType === 'trance') s3 = 'pure trance';
      }
      $('stepValue3').textContent = s3;
      $('stepValue4').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[4] ? (($('userAffirmations')?.value || '').trim() ? 'custom ✓' : 'none') : '';
      $('stepValue5').textContent = state.stepsCompleted[5] ? state.length : '';
    }
    $('stepValue6').textContent = state.fullScript ? 'ready ✓' : '';
    // Nav
    $('btnBack').hidden = state.currentStep === 1;
    $('btnNext').hidden = state.currentStep === TOTAL_STEPS;
    $('btnNext').disabled = !validateStep(state.currentStep);
    const backLabels = {
      2: '← guide',
      3: '← method',
      4: '← intention',
