    // unless the user has provided BOTH custom prefix and suffix (in which case
    // they've taken explicit control and the category default is omitted).
    const prefix = (persona.imagePromptPrefix || '').trim();
    const suffix = (persona.imagePromptSuffix || '').trim();
    const useCategoryHint = !(prefix && suffix); // skip if user has overridden both ends
    const parts = [
      'stylized minimal half-body portrait illustration',
      prefix,
      tagline,
      useCategoryHint ? styleHint : '',
      'soft glowing background, looking ahead with serene focus, ethereal mood, fine art illustration',
      suffix,
      'no background text, no signature',
    ].filter(Boolean);
    return parts.join(', ');
  }

  /** Get cached portrait URL for a persona, or null if not cached.
   *  Returns objectURL — caller is responsible for revoking when done. */
  async function personaPortraitGet(personaId) {
    try {
      const blob = await idbGet(PORTRAIT_KEY(personaId));
      return blob ? URL.createObjectURL(blob) : null;
    } catch { return null; }
  }

  /** Cache a portrait blob for a persona. Overwrites any existing portrait. */
  async function personaPortraitSet(personaId, blob) {
    await idbSet(PORTRAIT_KEY(personaId), blob);
  }

  /** Delete a cached portrait. Called when a persona is deleted. */
  async function personaPortraitDelete(personaId) {
    await idbDel(PORTRAIT_KEY(personaId));
  }

  /** Generate a portrait for a persona. Async — caller awaits the objectURL.
   *  Returns null if the plugin is unavailable, opt-in is off, or generation
   *  fails. Notifies the user on each outcome so they understand what happened.
   *  Per-persona dedup: if a generation is already running for this persona,
   *  returns the existing promise rather than starting a second call. */
  const _portraitInflight = new Map(); // personaId → Promise<URL|null>
  async function generatePersonaPortrait(persona) {
    if (!persona || !persona.id) return null;
    // Dedup: in-flight call for the same persona returns the existing promise
    if (_portraitInflight.has(persona.id)) return _portraitInflight.get(persona.id);

    if (typeof root === 'undefined' || !root.textToImagePlugin) {
      notify.warn('Image plugin unavailable — portraits require Perchance hosting.');
      return null;
    }
    if (!state.remoteProcessingOptIn) {
      notify.warn('Portraits require remote processing opt-in (in Options).');
      return null;
    }

    const promise = (async () => {
      try {
        const prompt = _buildPortraitPrompt(persona);
        const result = await root.textToImagePlugin({
          prompt,
          negativePrompt: PORTRAIT_NEGATIVE,
          negative:       PORTRAIT_NEGATIVE,
          guidanceScale:  7.5,
          numInferenceSteps: 25,
          steps:             25,
          seed: Math.floor(Math.random() * 2147483647), // fresh seed each generation
        });
        const dataUrl = result?.dataUrl || String(result || '');
        if (!dataUrl || !dataUrl.startsWith('data:')) {
          notify.warn(`Portrait generation returned no image for ${persona.name}.`);
          return null;
        }
        const blob = await fetch(dataUrl).then(r => r.blob());
        await personaPortraitSet(persona.id, blob);
        notify.success(`Portrait generated for ${persona.name}.`);
        return URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn('[persona portrait] generation failed:', e);
        notify.error('Portrait generation failed — see console.');
        return null;
      } finally {
        _portraitInflight.delete(persona.id);
      }
    })();
    _portraitInflight.set(persona.id, promise);
    return promise;
  }

  async function renderBgGallery() {
    const grid = $('bgGalleryGrid');
    const info = $('bgGalleryInfo');
    const countEl = $('bgCacheCount');
    if (!grid) return;
    const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
    if (countEl) countEl.textContent = manifest.length;
    if (info) info.textContent = `${manifest.length} image${manifest.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} · stored as binary blobs (no base64 overhead)`;
    if (!manifest.length) { grid.innerHTML = '<div class="sublabel" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;">No cached images yet. Generate some with the preview button or during a session.</div>'; return; }
    // Build grid with placeholder thumbnails, load blobs lazily
    grid.innerHTML = manifest.map(c => `
      <div class="bg-gallery-item" data-id="${c.id}">
        <img alt="" loading="lazy" style="background:#111;">
        <button class="bg-del" data-id="${c.id}" title="delete">✕</button>
        <button class="bg-dl" data-id="${c.id}" title="download">⬇</button>
      </div>`).join('');
    // Load thumbnails lazily
    for (const entry of manifest) {
      const url = await bgCacheGetUrl(entry.id);
      const img = grid.querySelector(`.bg-gallery-item[data-id="${entry.id}"] img`);
      if (img && url) img.src = url;
    }
    grid.querySelectorAll('.bg-del').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', async (e) => {
        e.stopPropagation();
        await bgCacheDelete(btn.dataset.id);
        renderBgGallery();
      });
    });
    grid.querySelectorAll('.bg-dl').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.stopPropagation();
        bgCacheDownload(btn.dataset.id);
      });
    });
  }

  let highwayRAF = null;
  let vizRAF = null;
  let stageResizeObs = null;

  // ── Canvas Visual Renderers (ported from Adaptive Session Studio — MIT) ──
  function hexToRgb(hex) {
    let h = hex.replace('#','');
    if (h.length === 3) h = h[0]+h[0]+h[1]+h[1]+h[2]+h[2];
    const r = parseInt(h.slice(0,2),16), g = parseInt(h.slice(2,4),16), b = parseInt(h.slice(4,6),16);
    return `${Number.isFinite(r)?r:128},${Number.isFinite(g)?g:128},${Number.isFinite(b)?b:128}`;
  }

  function renderTunnel(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rgb = hexToRgb(color), maxR = Math.hypot(cx,cy)*1.1, RINGS = 18;
    const mod = getAudioMod();
    // Bass adds forward velocity (rings rush toward viewer faster on bass hits)
    const velMul = 1 + mod.bass * 1.2;
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (let i = RINGS; i >= 0; i--) {
      const frac = ((i/RINGS) + (t*0.18*velMul)) % 1, r = frac*maxR, alpha = (1-frac)*0.65+0.05;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,r,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${alpha})`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5+(1-frac)*3; ctx.stroke();
    }
    // Voice-pulse light rings — fresh ring spawned on each voicePulse (3Hz cap)
    // Stored on the function itself to persist across frames
    if (!renderTunnel._voiceRings) { renderTunnel._voiceRings = []; renderTunnel._lastSpawn = 0; }
    const now = performance.now();
    if (mod.pulse > 0.6 && now - renderTunnel._lastSpawn > 333) {
      renderTunnel._lastSpawn = now;
      renderTunnel._voiceRings.push({ t: now });
      if (renderTunnel._voiceRings.length > 8) renderTunnel._voiceRings.shift();
    }
    for (const ring of renderTunnel._voiceRings) {
      const age = (now - ring.t) / 1000; // 0..2s lifetime
      if (age > 2) continue;
      const prog = age / 2; // 0..1
      const rr = prog * maxR;
      const ra = (1 - prog) * 0.7 * mod.pulse + (1 - prog) * 0.3;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, rr, 0, Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255,215,140,${ra})`;
      ctx.lineWidth = 2 + (1-prog) * 2;
      ctx.stroke();
    }
    const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx,cy,0,cx,cy,maxR*0.15);
    g.addColorStop(0,`rgba(${rgb},0.7)`); g.addColorStop(1,`rgba(${rgb},0)`);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,maxR*0.15,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle = g; ctx.fill();
  }

  function renderPendulumViz(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rx = W*0.38, ry = H*0.38, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.beginPath();
    for (let i = 0; i <= 2400; i++) {
      const frac = i/2400, s = (t - frac*4);
      const x = cx + rx*Math.sin(s*1.23+0.4)*Math.cos(s*0.71);
      const y = cy + ry*Math.sin(s*0.97+1.1)*Math.cos(s*1.03);
      i===0 ? ctx.moveTo(x,y) : ctx.lineTo(x,y);
    }
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.6)`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.2; ctx.stroke();
  }

  function renderVortex(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rgb = hexToRgb(color), maxR = Math.min(W,H)*0.44, ARMS = 6;
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (let arm = 0; arm < ARMS; arm++) {
      const baseAngle = (arm/ARMS)*Math.PI*2 + t*0.6;
      ctx.beginPath();
      for (let i = 0; i <= 300; i++) {
        const frac = i/300, angle = baseAngle + frac*Math.PI*3;
        const r = frac * maxR * (0.8 + 0.2*Math.sin(t*1.5+arm));
        const x = cx + r*Math.cos(angle), y = cy + r*Math.sin(angle);
        i===0 ? ctx.moveTo(x,y) : ctx.lineTo(x,y);
      }
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${0.35+0.25*Math.sin(t+arm)})`; ctx.lineWidth = 1; ctx.stroke();
    }
  }

  function renderMandala(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, petals = 8, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    const mod = getAudioMod();
    // Rotation speed × (1 + overall), arm brightness on voice pulse, petal scale on bass
    const speedMul = 1 + mod.overall;
    const armBright = 0.7 + mod.pulse * 0.3;
    const petalScale = 1 + mod.bass * 0.35;
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${armBright})`; ctx.shadowColor = color; ctx.shadowBlur = 12 + mod.pulse * 18;
    for (let layer = 0; layer < 4; layer++) {
      const R = (layer+1)*Math.min(W,H)*0.1 * petalScale;
      const spin = t*(layer%2===0 ? 0.2 : -0.15)*speedMul + layer*0.4;
      ctx.globalAlpha = (0.6-layer*0.1); ctx.lineWidth = 1.8-layer*0.3;
      for (let p = 0; p < petals; p++) {
        const base = (p/petals)*Math.PI*2 + spin, tip = base + Math.PI/petals;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx,cy);
        ctx.quadraticCurveTo(cx+R*1.5*Math.cos(base+0.3),cy+R*1.5*Math.sin(base+0.3),cx+R*Math.cos(tip),cy+R*Math.sin(tip));
        ctx.stroke();
      }
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,R*0.4,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();
    }
    ctx.globalAlpha = 1; ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
  }

  function renderLissajous(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, R = Math.min(W,H)*0.42, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.85)`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.8;
    ctx.shadowColor = color; ctx.shadowBlur = 10;
    const a = 3, b = 2, delta = t*0.4;
    ctx.beginPath();
    for (let i = 0; i <= 600; i++) {
      const th = (i/600)*Math.PI*2;
      const x = cx + R*Math.sin(a*th+delta), y = cy + R*Math.sin(b*th);
      i===0 ? ctx.moveTo(x,y) : ctx.lineTo(x,y);
    }
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.globalAlpha = 0.08; ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.globalAlpha = 1; ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
  }

  function renderColorWash(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const hue = (t*12 + parseInt(color.replace('#',''),16)%360) % 360, hue2 = (hue+40)%360;
    const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.4,H*0.4,0,W/2,H/2,Math.max(W,H)*0.7);
    grad.addColorStop(0,`hsla(${hue},70%,35%,1)`);
    grad.addColorStop(0.5,`hsla(${hue2},60%,20%,1)`);
    grad.addColorStop(1,`hsla(${(hue+180)%360},50%,8%,1)`);
    ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2,H/2,H*0.2,W/2,H/2,H*0.75);
    vig.addColorStop(0,'transparent'); vig.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)');
    ctx.fillStyle = vig; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  }

  function renderCanvasPulse(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, rgb = hexToRgb(color), maxR = Math.min(W,H)*0.46;
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
      const phase = (t*0.45 + i/6) % 1, r = phase*maxR, alpha = (1-phase)*0.7;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,r,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${alpha})`; ctx.lineWidth = 2+(1-phase)*5; ctx.stroke();
    }
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy,10+4*Math.sin(t*3),0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.85)`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // Breathing circle — the single most evidence-based hypnotic visual
  function renderBreathingCircle(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, maxR = Math.min(W,H)*0.38, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    // 4-7-8 cycle: 4s inhale, 7s hold, 8s exhale = 19s total
    // TEMPO IS LOCKED — audio reactivity ONLY modulates color warmth + halo alpha.
    // Do not introduce any audio-derived multiplier into phase/cycle/frac.
    const cycle = 19, phase = t % cycle;
    // Haptic at cycle start (once per 19s)
    if (phase < 0.05 && t > 0.1) vibrateBreath();
    let frac; // 0-1 breath position
    if (phase < 4) frac = phase / 4; // inhale: expand
    else if (phase < 11) frac = 1; // hold: full
    else frac = 1 - (phase - 11) / 8; // exhale: contract
    frac = frac * frac * (3 - 2 * frac); // smoothstep ease

    // Audio reactivity — color/halo only
    const mod = getAudioMod();
    const warmthShift = mod.envelope * 25; // pulls hue toward warm amber (lower) on voice
    const haloBoost = mod.bass * 0.35;      // outer halo gains alpha on bass

    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const r = maxR * 0.3 + maxR * 0.7 * frac;

    // Concentric rings at phase offsets
    for (let ring = 4; ring >= 0; ring--) {
      const ringFrac = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, frac - ring * 0.04));
      const rr = maxR * 0.3 + maxR * 0.7 * ringFrac * (3 - 2 * ringFrac);
      const alpha = 0.08 + ring * 0.04;
      // Color shift: cool blue inhale → warm amber exhale (+ warmth from voice envelope)
      const hue = 210 - frac * 30 - warmthShift; // 210 (blue) → 180 (teal) + voice warmth
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, rr, 0, Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `hsla(${hue}, 50%, 60%, ${alpha})`; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5; ctx.stroke();
    }

    // Outer halo ring — reacts to bass, sits outside maxR. Does NOT change breath tempo.
    if (haloBoost > 0.02) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, maxR * (1.05 + haloBoost * 0.25), 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.strokeStyle = `hsla(${210 - warmthShift}, 55%, 62%, ${haloBoost * 0.8})`;
      ctx.lineWidth = 3 + haloBoost * 4;
      ctx.stroke();
    }

    // Main circle
    const mainHue = 210 - frac * 40 - warmthShift;
    const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, cy, r * 0.3, cx, cy, r);
    grad.addColorStop(0, `hsla(${mainHue}, 55%, 55%, 0.35)`);
    grad.addColorStop(1, `hsla(${mainHue}, 45%, 40%, 0.08)`);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, 0, Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fill();
    ctx.strokeStyle = `hsla(${mainHue}, 50%, 60%, 0.5)`; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();

    // Label
    let label = '';
    if (phase < 4) label = 'breathe in';
    else if (phase < 11) label = 'hold';
    else label = 'breathe out';
    ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${mainHue}, 40%, 70%, 0.6)`;
    ctx.font = '0.8rem -apple-system, sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.fillText(label, cx, cy + r + 24);

    // Center dot
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, 4 + 2 * frac, 0, Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle = `hsla(${mainHue}, 50%, 70%, 0.8)`; ctx.fill();
  }

  // Moiré — historically the most potent trance device (per ROADMAP)
  // Two concentric-ring patterns with one center slowly orbiting the other
  function renderMoire(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, maxR = Math.max(W, H) * 0.8;
    ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(136,136,136,0.45)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    // First grating: centered
    for (let r = 6; r < maxR; r += 12) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.stroke();
    }
    // Second grating: orbiting offset
    const ox = cx + Math.cos(t * 0.15) * 18;
    const oy = cy + Math.sin(t * 0.12) * 14;
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(136,136,136,0.4)';
    for (let r = 6; r < maxR; r += 12) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(ox, oy, r, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.stroke();
    }
    // Soft vignette
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, cy, maxR * 0.2, cx, cy, maxR * 0.6);
    vig.addColorStop(0, 'transparent'); vig.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)');
    ctx.fillStyle = vig; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
  }

  // Starfield warp tunnel — 3D stars projected to 2D with streak lines
  function renderStarfield(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H/2, STARS = 200, focal = 180, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    if (!renderStarfield._pool) {
      renderStarfield._pool = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < STARS; i++) renderStarfield._pool.push({
        x: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 600, y: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 600,
        z: Math.random() * 600, psx: 0, psy: 0
      });
    }
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    const speed = 1.5 + Math.sin(t * 0.3) * 0.5;
    for (const s of renderStarfield._pool) {
      const psx = s.psx, psy = s.psy;
      s.z -= speed;
      if (s.z < 1) { s.x = (Math.random()-0.5)*600; s.y = (Math.random()-0.5)*600; s.z = 600; s.psx = cx; s.psy = cy; continue; }
      const sx = s.x / s.z * focal + cx;
      const sy = s.y / s.z * focal + cy;
      s.psx = sx; s.psy = sy;
      if (sx < 0 || sx > W || sy < 0 || sy > H) continue;
      const brightness = Math.min(1, (600 - s.z) / 400);
      const size = Math.max(0.5, (1 - s.z / 600) * 3);
      ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${brightness})`;
      // Streak line from previous position
      if (psx > 0 && Math.abs(sx - psx) < 40) {
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(psx, psy); ctx.lineTo(sx, sy);
        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${brightness * 0.5})`; ctx.lineWidth = size * 0.5; ctx.stroke();
      }
      ctx.fillRect(sx - size/2, sy - size/2, size, size);
    }
  }

  // Candle focal — soft radial glow with position jitter (classic Mesmerist's candle)
  function renderCandle(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const cx = W/2, cy = H * 0.4, rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.08)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    // Flame jitter
    const jx = cx + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 4;
    const jy = cy + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 3;
    const baseR = 30 + Math.sin(t * 2.5) * 5 + Math.sin(t * 4.1) * 3;
    // Outer glow
    const outer = ctx.createRadialGradient(jx, jy, 0, jx, jy, baseR * 3);
    outer.addColorStop(0, `rgba(${rgb},0.15)`);
    outer.addColorStop(0.4, `rgba(${rgb},0.05)`);
    outer.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
    ctx.fillStyle = outer; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    // Inner flame
    const inner = ctx.createRadialGradient(jx, jy - 4, 0, jx, jy, baseR);
    inner.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255,240,200,0.7)');
    inner.addColorStop(0.3, `rgba(${rgb},0.4)`);
    inner.addColorStop(0.7, `rgba(${rgb},0.08)`);
    inner.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(jx, jy, baseR, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fillStyle = inner; ctx.fill();
    // Bright core
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(jx, jy - 2, 4, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,240,0.9)'; ctx.fill();
  }

  // Flow-field particles — simplex noise driven, additive glow
  // Uses a simplified 2D noise (value noise with smoothstep) since we can't import simplex
  function renderFlowField(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    const N = W < 500 ? 250 : 600; // Mobile vs desktop
    if (!renderFlowField._p) {
      renderFlowField._p = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < N; i++) renderFlowField._p.push({ x: Math.random()*W, y: Math.random()*H, px: 0, py: 0 });
    }
    const ps = renderFlowField._p;
    // Resize pool if canvas changed
    if (ps.length < N) while (ps.length < N) ps.push({ x: Math.random()*W, y: Math.random()*H, px: 0, py: 0 });

    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)'; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'lighter';

    const scale = 0.003, speed = 0.5;
    for (const p of ps) {
      p.px = p.x; p.py = p.y;
      // Simple hash-based noise field
      const nx = p.x * scale, ny = p.y * scale, nt = t * 0.08;
      const angle = (Math.sin(nx * 3.1 + nt) + Math.cos(ny * 2.7 - nt * 0.7) + Math.sin((nx + ny) * 1.4 + nt * 0.3)) * Math.PI;
      p.x += Math.cos(angle) * speed;
      p.y += Math.sin(angle) * speed;
      // Wrap around
      if (p.x < 0) p.x += W; if (p.x > W) p.x -= W;
      if (p.y < 0) p.y += H; if (p.y > H) p.y -= H;
      // Draw streak
      const dx = p.x - p.px, dy = p.y - p.py;
      if (Math.abs(dx) < 20 && Math.abs(dy) < 20) {
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(p.px, p.py); ctx.lineTo(p.x, p.y);
        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.3)`; ctx.lineWidth = 0.8; ctx.stroke();
      }
    }
    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
    // Vignette
    const vig = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2, H/2, Math.min(W,H)*0.2, W/2, H/2, Math.min(W,H)*0.6);
    vig.addColorStop(0, 'transparent'); vig.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.4)');
    ctx.fillStyle = vig; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
  }

  // Classic plasma — sum of sines mapped through HSV palette
  function renderPlasma(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    // Render at reduced resolution for performance
    const rW = 192, rH = Math.round(rW * H / W);
    if (!renderPlasma._img || renderPlasma._img.width !== rW) {
      renderPlasma._off = (typeof OffscreenCanvas !== 'undefined') ? new OffscreenCanvas(rW, rH) : document.createElement('canvas');
      renderPlasma._off.width = rW; renderPlasma._off.height = rH;
      renderPlasma._img = renderPlasma._off.getContext('2d').createImageData(rW, rH);
      // Precompute sine LUT
      renderPlasma._sin = new Float32Array(1024);
      for (let i = 0; i < 1024; i++) renderPlasma._sin[i] = Math.sin(i * Math.PI * 2 / 1024);
    }
    const data = renderPlasma._img.data, sinLut = renderPlasma._sin;
    const S = v => sinLut[((v % 1024) + 1024) % 1024 | 0];

    for (let y = 0; y < rH; y++) {
      for (let x = 0; x < rW; x++) {
        const v = S(x * 3 + t * 40) + S(y * 4 - t * 30) + S((x + y) * 2 + t * 20) + S(Math.sqrt(x*x + y*y) * 2 - t * 50);
        const hue = ((v + 4) / 8 * 360 + t * 15) % 360;
        // HSV to RGB (S=0.7, V=0.6)
        const c = 0.42, x2 = c * (1 - Math.abs((hue / 60) % 2 - 1));
        let r1=0,g1=0,b1=0;
        const h = Math.floor(hue / 60) % 6;
        if (h===0){r1=c;g1=x2;}else if(h===1){r1=x2;g1=c;}else if(h===2){g1=c;b1=x2;}
        else if(h===3){g1=x2;b1=c;}else if(h===4){r1=x2;b1=c;}else{r1=c;b1=x2;}
        const m = 0.18;
        const idx = (y * rW + x) * 4;
        data[idx] = (r1+m)*255; data[idx+1] = (g1+m)*255; data[idx+2] = (b1+m)*255; data[idx+3] = 255;
      }
    }
    const offCtx = renderPlasma._off.getContext('2d');
    offCtx.putImageData(renderPlasma._img, 0, 0);
    ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
    ctx.drawImage(renderPlasma._off, 0, 0, W, H);
  }

  // Kaleidoscope — wraps any sub-renderer with N-fold mirror symmetry
  function makeKaleidoscope(subRenderer, folds = 6) {
    return function(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
      const cx = W/2, cy = H/2;
      // Render sub-effect to an offscreen canvas
      if (!makeKaleidoscope._off || makeKaleidoscope._off.width !== W) {
        makeKaleidoscope._off = document.createElement('canvas');
        makeKaleidoscope._off.width = W; makeKaleidoscope._off.height = H;
      }
      const offCtx = makeKaleidoscope._off.getContext('2d');
      subRenderer(offCtx, W, H, t, color);
      // Draw N wedges with alternating mirrors
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);
      const wedgeAngle = Math.PI * 2 / folds;
      for (let i = 0; i < folds; i++) {
        ctx.save();
        ctx.translate(cx, cy);
        ctx.rotate(wedgeAngle * i);
        if (i % 2 === 1) ctx.scale(-1, 1); // Mirror alternate wedges
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, 0);
        ctx.lineTo(Math.max(W, H), 0);
        ctx.arc(0, 0, Math.max(W, H), 0, wedgeAngle);
        ctx.closePath();
        ctx.clip();
        ctx.translate(-cx, -cy);
        ctx.drawImage(makeKaleidoscope._off, 0, 0);
        ctx.restore();
      }
    };
  }

  // Aurora borealis — undulating gradient curtains
  function renderAurora(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    const mod = getAudioMod();
    // Wave crest height on voice envelope; color-band vertical shift on bass; opacity waves on treble
    const crestMul = 1 + mod.envelope * 1.8;      // 1× base → 2.8× on full envelope
    const bandShift = mod.bass * 60;              // pixel shift upward
    const opacityBoost = mod.treble * 0.4;        // additive alpha boost
    for (let b = 0; b < 4; b++) {
      const ph = b * 1.7 + t * 0.0004;
      const baseY = H * 0.25 - bandShift
        + Math.sin(ph) * H * 0.12 * crestMul
        + Math.sin(ph * 0.7 + b) * H * 0.06 * crestMul;
      const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, baseY - 100, 0, baseY + 140);
      grad.addColorStop(0, 'transparent');
      grad.addColorStop(0.3, `rgba(${rgb},${(0.035 + b * 0.008 + opacityBoost).toFixed(3)})`);
      grad.addColorStop(0.7, `rgba(${rgb},${(0.05 - b * 0.008 + opacityBoost).toFixed(3)})`);
      grad.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
      ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
    }
  }

  // Rain drops — falling streaks with splash
  function renderRain(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    if (!renderRain._drops) { renderRain._drops = []; for (let i = 0; i < 120; i++) renderRain._drops.push({ x: Math.random() * W, y: Math.random() * H, len: 8 + Math.random() * 18, speed: 4 + Math.random() * 6 }); }
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.15)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},0.25)`; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    for (const d of renderRain._drops) {
      d.y += d.speed; if (d.y > H) { d.y = -d.len; d.x = Math.random() * W; }
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(d.x, d.y); ctx.lineTo(d.x - 0.5, d.y + d.len); ctx.stroke();
    }
  }

  // Sacred geometry — Flower of Life
  function renderSacredGeo(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color), cx = W/2, cy = H/2, R = Math.min(W,H) * 0.18;
    const rot = t * 0.00015;
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${0.15 + Math.sin(t * 0.001) * 0.05})`; ctx.lineWidth = 0.8;
    const pts = [[0,0]]; for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) pts.push([Math.cos(i * Math.PI/3) * R, Math.sin(i * Math.PI/3) * R]);
    for (let ring = 0; ring < 2; ring++) for (const [px,py] of pts) {
      const r = R * (ring === 0 ? 1 : 1.73);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx + px * (ring+1) * Math.cos(rot) - py * Math.sin(rot), cy + px * (ring+1) * Math.sin(rot) + py * Math.cos(rot), r, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.stroke();
    }
  }

  // Waveform — phase-aware frequency shift (beta→theta)
  function renderWaveform(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color), cy = H/2;
    const mod = getAudioMod();
    const a = state.audioReactive;
    const haveAudio = a && a.active && a._fftBuffer && mod.overall > 0.01;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, cy);
    if (haveAudio) {
      // Real FFT — sampled evenly across the width
      const buf = a._fftBuffer;
      const step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(buf.length / Math.min(W, 128)));
      const ampScale = H * 0.35 * (0.6 + mod.overall);
      for (let x = 0; x < W; x++) {
        const idx = Math.floor((x / W) * buf.length / step) * step;
        const v = (buf[idx] / 255) - 0.5; // -0.5..0.5
        const y = cy + v * ampScale * Math.sin(x / W * Math.PI); // window envelope
        ctx.lineTo(x, y);
      }
    } else {
      // Idle sine — unchanged legacy behavior
      const freq = 0.02 + Math.sin(t * 0.0003) * 0.015;
      for (let x = 0; x < W; x++) {
        const amp = H * 0.15 * (1 + Math.sin(t * 0.0005) * 0.3);
        ctx.lineTo(x, cy + Math.sin(x * freq + t * 0.002) * amp * Math.sin(x / W * Math.PI));
      }
    }
    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${rgb},${0.4 + mod.envelope * 0.4})`;
    ctx.lineWidth = 2 + mod.bass * 1.2;
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  // Smoke / fog — drifting translucent circles
  function renderSmoke(ctx, W, H, t, color) {
    const rgb = hexToRgb(color);
    const mod = getAudioMod();
    if (!renderSmoke._puffs) { renderSmoke._puffs = []; for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) renderSmoke._puffs.push({ x: Math.random() * W, y: Math.random() * H, r: 60 + Math.random() * 120, vx: (Math.random()-0.5)*0.3, vy: (Math.random()-0.5)*0.2 }); }
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.02)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    // Turbulence strength on overall — jitters velocities; density increases with envelope
    const turbMul = 1 + mod.overall * 1.5;
    const densityBoost = 1 + mod.envelope * 0.6; // brighter puffs when narrator speaks
    for (const p of renderSmoke._puffs) {
      // Apply turbulence to velocity each frame
      p.vx += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.015 * turbMul;
      p.vy += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.012 * turbMul;
      // Mild damping so velocities don't explode
      p.vx *= 0.985; p.vy *= 0.985;
      p.x += p.vx; p.y += p.vy;
      if (p.x < -p.r) p.x = W + p.r; if (p.x > W + p.r) p.x = -p.r;
      if (p.y < -p.r) p.y = H + p.r; if (p.y > H + p.r) p.y = -p.r;
      const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(p.x, p.y, 0, p.x, p.y, p.r);
      grad.addColorStop(0, `rgba(${rgb},${(0.025 * densityBoost).toFixed(4)})`); grad.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
      ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fillRect(p.x - p.r, p.y - p.r, p.r * 2, p.r * 2);
    }
  }

  const VIZ_RENDERERS = {
    tunnel: renderTunnel,
    'pendulum-viz': renderPendulumViz,
    vortex: renderVortex,
    mandala: renderMandala,
    lissajous: renderLissajous,
    colorwash: renderColorWash,
    'canvas-pulse': renderCanvasPulse,
    breathing: renderBreathingCircle,
    moire: renderMoire,
    starfield: renderStarfield,
    candle: renderCandle,
    flowfield: renderFlowField,
    plasma: renderPlasma,
    'kaleidoscope-flow': makeKaleidoscope(renderFlowField, 6),
    'kaleidoscope-plasma': makeKaleidoscope(renderPlasma, 8),
    aurora: renderAurora,
    rain: renderRain,
    'sacred-geo': renderSacredGeo,
    waveform: renderWaveform,
    smoke: renderSmoke,
  };

  // Phase-based speed multipliers for visuals
  const PHASE_VIZ_SPEED = { settling: 0.5, induction: 1.0, deepener: 0.7, work: 0.9, lightener: 0.75, wake: 0.95, reintroduction: 0.8, emergence: 0.95 };

  // ====================================================================
  // PREVIEW ENGINES (Configure tab — separate from session playback)
  // ====================================================================

  // Soundscape preview — uses a separate SoundscapeEngine instance
  const _previewDrone = new SoundscapeEngine();
  let _previewDroneTimeout = null;

  async function previewSoundscape() {
    const type = $('soundscapeSelect')?.value;
    if (!type || type === 'none') { notify.info('Select a soundscape first.'); return; }
    await stopSoundscapePreview();
    try {
      await _previewDrone.start(state.droneVolume, type);
      togglePreviewBtns('sound', true);

      $('soundPreviewHint').textContent = 'playing ' + type + '...';
      // Auto-stop after 10 seconds
      _previewDroneTimeout = setTimeout(() => stopSoundscapePreview(), 10000);
    } catch(e) { notify.warn('Could not start audio preview.'); }
  }

  async function stopSoundscapePreview() {
    clearTimeout(_previewDroneTimeout);
    await _previewDrone.stop();
    togglePreviewBtns('sound', false);

    $('soundPreviewHint').textContent = 'Listen to a 10-second preview.';
  }

  // Viz preview — renders to the mini canvas with its own rAF loop
  let _vizPreviewRaf = null;
  let _vizPreviewStart = 0;

  function startVizPreview() {
    stopVizPreview();
    const sel = $('vizSelect')?.value;
    const vizKey = sel === 'auto' ? (getMethod().visual) : sel;
    const renderer = VIZ_RENDERERS[vizKey];
    if (!renderer) {
      // Non-canvas types (highway, spiral, pulse, none) — show a label instead
      const wrap = $('vizPreviewWrap');
      if (wrap) { wrap.style.display = 'block'; }
      const canvas = $('vizPreviewCanvas');
      if (canvas) { const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); ctx.fillStyle = '#000'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height); ctx.fillStyle = '#4a6a84'; ctx.font = '13px -apple-system, sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center'; ctx.fillText(vizKey === 'none' ? 'Black screen — no visual' : vizKey + ' (non-canvas preview)', canvas.width/2, canvas.height/2); }
      $('vizPreviewLabel').textContent = vizKey;
      togglePreviewBtns('viz', true);

      return;
    }

    const wrap = $('vizPreviewWrap');
    const canvas = $('vizPreviewCanvas');
    if (!wrap || !canvas) return;
    wrap.style.display = 'block';
    canvas.width = canvas.offsetWidth || 300;
    canvas.height = 120;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { alpha: false });
    const color = '#6b94b8';
    _vizPreviewStart = performance.now();
    $('vizPreviewLabel').textContent = vizKey;
    togglePreviewBtns('viz', true);

    function frame() {
      const t = ((performance.now() - _vizPreviewStart) / 1000) * (state.vizSettings.speed || 1.0);
      try { renderer(ctx, canvas.width, canvas.height, t, color); } catch(e) {}
      _vizPreviewRaf = requestAnimationFrame(frame);
    }
    _vizPreviewRaf = requestAnimationFrame(frame);
  }

  function stopVizPreview() {
    if (_vizPreviewRaf) { cancelAnimationFrame(_vizPreviewRaf); _vizPreviewRaf = null; }
    const wrap = $('vizPreviewWrap');
    if (wrap) wrap.style.display = 'none';
    togglePreviewBtns('viz', false);

  }

  // Voice preview state
  let _voicePreviewing = false;

  // ====================================================================
  // NEURAL BLOOM — flagship audio-reactive visualizer (spec §4)
  // ====================================================================
  // WebGL2-first, WebGL1 fallback, canvas 2D last-resort. All three share
  // the same JS per-frame tick with getAudioMod()/state._currentPhase
  // inputs; only the draw details differ.
  //
  // Visual composition (back → front):
  //   1. Background shader     — fBM gradient, phase-colored, near-static
  //   2. Central breathing orb — size modulated by overall + voiceEnvelope
  //   3. Radial particle ring  — 300 orbiting points, radius on bass
  //   4. Bloom bursts          — 20 petals per voicePulse, 3Hz rate cap
  //
  // Safety: bloom bursts throttled to ≥333ms spacing; orb radius smoothed
  // so it cannot complete a cycle faster than ~500ms; burst fade is
  // asymmetric (150ms in, 850ms out) so no strobe-like flashes.
  // ====================================================================

  const NB_PHASE_PALETTES = {
    settling:        { a: [0.10, 0.15, 0.35], b: [0.15, 0.40, 0.45] },
    induction:       { a: [0.15, 0.40, 0.45], b: [0.30, 0.15, 0.45] },
    deepener:        { a: [0.30, 0.15, 0.45], b: [0.50, 0.10, 0.40] },
    work:            { a: [0.50, 0.10, 0.40], b: [0.80, 0.60, 0.20] },
    affirmation:     { a: [0.50, 0.10, 0.40], b: [0.80, 0.60, 0.20] },
    affirm:          { a: [0.50, 0.10, 0.40], b: [0.80, 0.60, 0.20] },
    lightener:       { a: [0.80, 0.60, 0.20], b: [0.85, 0.55, 0.25] },
    wake:            { a: [0.85, 0.55, 0.25], b: [0.30, 0.70, 0.85] },
    reintroduction:  { a: [0.30, 0.70, 0.85], b: [0.90, 0.95, 1.00] },
    _default:        { a: [0.10, 0.20, 0.40], b: [0.30, 0.10, 0.50] },
  };

  // Shader sources — WebGL2 (GLSL ES 3.0). GL1 variants derived at load time.
  const NB_VS_BG = `#version 300 es
    in vec2 aPos;
    out vec2 vUv;
    void main() { vUv = aPos * 0.5 + 0.5; gl_Position = vec4(aPos, 0.0, 1.0); }
  `;
  const NB_FS_BG = `#version 300 es
    precision highp float;
    in vec2 vUv;
    uniform float uTime;
    uniform vec3  uColorA;
    uniform vec3  uColorB;
    out vec4 fragColor;
    float hash(vec2 p){ return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(127.1, 311.7))) * 43758.5453); }
    float noise(vec2 p){
      vec2 i = floor(p), f = fract(p);
      float a = hash(i), b = hash(i+vec2(1,0)), c = hash(i+vec2(0,1)), d = hash(i+vec2(1,1));
      vec2 u = f*f*(3.0-2.0*f);
      return mix(a,b,u.x) + (c-a)*u.y*(1.0-u.x) + (d-b)*u.x*u.y;
    }
    float fbm(vec2 p){ float v=0.0, a=0.5; for(int i=0;i<4;i++){ v+=a*noise(p); p*=2.0; a*=0.5; } return v; }
    void main() {
      vec2 p = vUv * 3.0;
      float n = fbm(p + uTime*0.05);
      vec3 c = mix(uColorA, uColorB, smoothstep(0.3, 0.7, n));
      fragColor = vec4(c, 1.0);
    }
  `;
  const NB_VS_ORB = `#version 300 es
    in vec2 aPos;
    uniform vec2  uResolution;
    uniform vec2  uCenter;       // pixel offset from canvas center
    uniform float uRadius;
    out vec2 vPos;
    void main() {
      vec2 scaled = aPos * uRadius;
      vec2 pixel = scaled + uCenter;
      vec2 ndc = pixel / uResolution * 2.0;
      gl_Position = vec4(ndc.x, -ndc.y, 0.0, 1.0);
      vPos = aPos;
    }
  `;
  const NB_FS_ORB = `#version 300 es
    precision highp float;
    in vec2 vPos;
    uniform vec3  uColor;
    uniform float uGlow;
    out vec4 fragColor;
    void main() {
      float r = length(vPos);
      if (r > 1.0) discard;
      float core = smoothstep(0.6, 0.0, r);
      float halo = smoothstep(1.0, 0.5, r) * uGlow;
      vec3 c = uColor * (core + halo * 0.6);
      fragColor = vec4(c, core + halo * 0.4);
    }
  `;
  const NB_VS_PARTICLE = `#version 300 es
    in float aPhase;
    uniform float uTime;
    uniform float uRadius;
    uniform float uPtSize;
    uniform vec2  uResolution;
    uniform float uSpin;
    out float vFade;
    void main() {
      float angle = aPhase * 6.2831853 + uTime * uSpin;
      vec2 pos = vec2(cos(angle), sin(angle)) * uRadius;
      vec2 ndc = pos / uResolution * 2.0;
      gl_Position = vec4(ndc.x, -ndc.y, 0.0, 1.0);
      gl_PointSize = uPtSize;
      vFade = 0.5 + 0.5 * sin(aPhase * 30.0 + uTime * 0.7);
    }
  `;
  const NB_FS_PARTICLE = `#version 300 es
    precision highp float;
    in float vFade;
    uniform vec3 uColor;
    out vec4 fragColor;
    void main() {
      vec2 c = gl_PointCoord * 2.0 - 1.0;
      float r = length(c);
      if (r > 1.0) discard;
      float glow = smoothstep(1.0, 0.2, r);
      fragColor = vec4(uColor * glow * vFade, glow * vFade);
    }
  `;

  // WebGL1 shader variants — strip #version, convert in/out, gl_FragColor
  function _nbToGL1(src, isFrag) {
    let s = src.replace(/#version 300 es\s*\n?/, '').replace(/in /g, isFrag ? 'varying ' : 'attribute ');
    if (isFrag) {
      s = s.replace(/out vec4 fragColor;/, '').replace(/fragColor/g, 'gl_FragColor');
    } else {
      s = s.replace(/out /g, 'varying ');
    }
    return s;
  }

  function _nbCompile(gl, vsSrc, fsSrc, isGL2) {
    const vs = gl.createShader(gl.VERTEX_SHADER);
    gl.shaderSource(vs, isGL2 ? vsSrc : _nbToGL1(vsSrc, false));
    gl.compileShader(vs);
    if (!gl.getShaderParameter(vs, gl.COMPILE_STATUS)) { console.error('[NB] vs compile:', gl.getShaderInfoLog(vs)); return null; }
    const fs = gl.createShader(gl.FRAGMENT_SHADER);
    gl.shaderSource(fs, isGL2 ? fsSrc : _nbToGL1(fsSrc, true));
    gl.compileShader(fs);
    if (!gl.getShaderParameter(fs, gl.COMPILE_STATUS)) { console.error('[NB] fs compile:', gl.getShaderInfoLog(fs)); return null; }
    const p = gl.createProgram();
    gl.attachShader(p, vs); gl.attachShader(p, fs); gl.linkProgram(p);
    if (!gl.getProgramParameter(p, gl.LINK_STATUS)) { console.error('[NB] link:', gl.getProgramInfoLog(p)); return null; }
    return p;
  }

  const neuralBloomRenderer = {
    canvas: null,
    gl: null,
    ctx2d: null,
    mode: null, // 'webgl2' | 'webgl1' | 'canvas2d' | null
    _rafHandle: null,
    _ro: null,
    _smoothRadius: null,
    _frameTimes: [],
    _degraded: false,
    _particleCount: 300,
    _lastPhase: null,
    _targetColorA: null,
    _targetColorB: null,
    colorA: null,
    colorB: null,
    bursts: null,
    burstCursor: 0,
    startMs: 0,
    _lastFrameAt: 0,

    start(stage) {
      this.canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      this.canvas.className = 'neural-bloom-canvas';
      this.canvas.style.cssText = 'position:absolute; inset:0; width:100%; height:100%; pointer-events:none; background:#000;';
      this.canvas.width = stage.clientWidth;
      this.canvas.height = stage.clientHeight;
      stage.insertBefore(this.canvas, stage.firstChild);

      // Context acquisition chain: WebGL2 → WebGL1 → canvas2d
      this.gl = this.canvas.getContext('webgl2');
      if (this.gl) { this.mode = 'webgl2'; this._initGL(); }
      else {
        this.gl = this.canvas.getContext('webgl') || this.canvas.getContext('experimental-webgl');
        if (this.gl) {
          this.mode = 'webgl1';
          // WebGL1 needs OES_point_size for custom gl_PointSize — try to enable
          try { this.gl.getExtension('OES_standard_derivatives'); } catch {}
          this._initGL();
        } else {
          this.ctx2d = this.canvas.getContext('2d');
          this.mode = 'canvas2d';
          this._initCanvas2D();
        }
      }
      console.log('[NB] renderer mode:', this.mode);

      // Shared state for all modes
      this._smoothRadius = null;
      this._frameTimes = [];
      this._degraded = false;
      this._particleCount = 300;
      this.bursts = Array.from({ length: 5 }, () => ({ spawnTime: -1, angleBase: 0 }));
      this.burstCursor = 0;
      this._lastPhase = null;
      this._targetColorA = null;
      this._targetColorB = null;
      this.startMs = performance.now();
      this._lastFrameAt = this.startMs;

      this._ro = new ResizeObserver(() => {
        this.canvas.width = stage.clientWidth;
        this.canvas.height = stage.clientHeight;
        if (this.gl) this.gl.viewport(0, 0, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);
      });
      this._ro.observe(stage);

      this._startLoop();
    },

    _initGL() {
      const gl = this.gl;
      const isGL2 = this.mode === 'webgl2';
      gl.viewport(0, 0, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);
      this.bgProg       = _nbCompile(gl, NB_VS_BG,       NB_FS_BG,       isGL2);
      this.orbProg      = _nbCompile(gl, NB_VS_ORB,      NB_FS_ORB,      isGL2);
      this.particleProg = _nbCompile(gl, NB_VS_PARTICLE, NB_FS_PARTICLE, isGL2);
      if (!this.bgProg || !this.orbProg || !this.particleProg) {
        // Shader compilation failed — fall back to canvas2d on the same element
        console.warn('[NB] GL shader compile failed — falling back to canvas2d');
        this.gl = null;
        this.mode = 'canvas2d';
        this.ctx2d = this.canvas.getContext('2d');
        this._initCanvas2D();
        return;
      }
      this.bgUniforms = {
        uTime:   gl.getUniformLocation(this.bgProg, 'uTime'),
        uColorA: gl.getUniformLocation(this.bgProg, 'uColorA'),
        uColorB: gl.getUniformLocation(this.bgProg, 'uColorB'),
      };
      this.orbUniforms = {
        uResolution: gl.getUniformLocation(this.orbProg, 'uResolution'),
        uCenter:     gl.getUniformLocation(this.orbProg, 'uCenter'),
        uRadius:     gl.getUniformLocation(this.orbProg, 'uRadius'),
        uColor:      gl.getUniformLocation(this.orbProg, 'uColor'),
        uGlow:       gl.getUniformLocation(this.orbProg, 'uGlow'),
      };
      this.particleUniforms = {
        uTime:       gl.getUniformLocation(this.particleProg, 'uTime'),
        uRadius:     gl.getUniformLocation(this.particleProg, 'uRadius'),
        uPtSize:     gl.getUniformLocation(this.particleProg, 'uPtSize'),
        uResolution: gl.getUniformLocation(this.particleProg, 'uResolution'),
        uSpin:       gl.getUniformLocation(this.particleProg, 'uSpin'),
        uColor:      gl.getUniformLocation(this.particleProg, 'uColor'),
      };
      // Fullscreen quad (bg + orb both use it)
      this.quad = gl.createBuffer();
      gl.bindBuffer(gl.ARRAY_BUFFER, this.quad);
      gl.bufferData(gl.ARRAY_BUFFER, new Float32Array([-1,-1, 1,-1, -1,1, 1,1]), gl.STATIC_DRAW);
      // Particle phases (static; orbit math is in shader)
      const phases = new Float32Array(300);
      for (let i = 0; i < 300; i++) phases[i] = i / 300;
      this.particleBuf = gl.createBuffer();
      gl.bindBuffer(gl.ARRAY_BUFFER, this.particleBuf);
      gl.bufferData(gl.ARRAY_BUFFER, phases, gl.STATIC_DRAW);

      // Default palette (overridden on first frame by phase logic)
      this.colorA = [0.10, 0.20, 0.40];
      this.colorB = [0.30, 0.10, 0.50];
    },

    _initCanvas2D() {
      this.ctx2d.fillStyle = '#0a0a0c';
      this.ctx2d.fillRect(0, 0, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);
      this.colorA = [0.10, 0.20, 0.40];
      this.colorB = [0.30, 0.10, 0.50];
    },

    _startLoop() {
      const tick = () => {
        if (state.abortFlag) { this.stop(); return; }
        if (!this._rafHandle) return; // stopped externally
        this._renderFrame();
        this._rafHandle = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      };
      this._rafHandle = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    },

    // Phase → palette smooth crossfade; per-frame, nudges colorA/B toward the
    // target palette (3s full transition). Shared by GL and canvas2d modes.
    _updatePalette() {
      const target = NB_PHASE_PALETTES[state._currentPhase] || NB_PHASE_PALETTES._default;
      if (!this._targetColorA) {
        this._targetColorA = target.a.slice(); this._targetColorB = target.b.slice();
        this.colorA = target.a.slice(); this.colorB = target.b.slice();
      }
      if (this._lastPhase !== state._currentPhase) {
        this._lastPhase = state._currentPhase;
        this._targetColorA = target.a.slice(); this._targetColorB = target.b.slice();
      }
      // Lerp at ~60fps for a 3s full transition — k ≈ 1/(180 frames)
      const k = 0.0055;
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        this.colorA[i] += (this._targetColorA[i] - this.colorA[i]) * k;
        this.colorB[i] += (this._targetColorB[i] - this.colorB[i]) * k;
      }
    },

    // Shared: spawn/track bloom bursts (3Hz-capped)
    _updateBursts(mod) {
      if (mod.pulse > 0.6) {
        const a = state.audioReactive;
        if (performance.now() - a._lastBurstAt >= 333) {
          a._lastBurstAt = performance.now();
          this.bursts[this.burstCursor] = { spawnTime: performance.now(), angleBase: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2 };
          this.burstCursor = (this.burstCursor + 1) % 5;
        }
      }
    },

    // Shared: frame-time watchdog (auto-degrade under 30fps sustained)
    _tickFrameGuard() {
      const now = performance.now();
      const dt = now - this._lastFrameAt;
      this._lastFrameAt = now;
      this._frameTimes.push(dt);
      if (this._frameTimes.length > 30) this._frameTimes.shift();
      if (!this._degraded && this._frameTimes.length === 30) {
        const avg = this._frameTimes.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / 30;
        if (avg > 33) {
          console.log('[NB] frame time degraded (avg ' + avg.toFixed(1) + 'ms) — reducing particles');
          this._degraded = true;
          this._particleCount = 150;
        }
      }
    },

    _renderFrame() {
      this._tickFrameGuard();
      this._updatePalette();
      const mod = getAudioMod();
      this._updateBursts(mod);

      if (this.mode === 'webgl2' || this.mode === 'webgl1') this._renderGL(mod);
      else if (this.mode === 'canvas2d') this._renderCanvas2D(mod);
    },

    _renderGL(mod) {
      const gl = this.gl;
      gl.viewport(0, 0, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);
      gl.clearColor(0, 0, 0, 1);
      gl.clear(gl.COLOR_BUFFER_BIT);

      // ── Background gradient ──
      gl.useProgram(this.bgProg);
      gl.bindBuffer(gl.ARRAY_BUFFER, this.quad);
      const bgAPos = gl.getAttribLocation(this.bgProg, 'aPos');
      gl.enableVertexAttribArray(bgAPos);
      gl.vertexAttribPointer(bgAPos, 2, gl.FLOAT, false, 0, 0);
      gl.uniform1f(this.bgUniforms.uTime, (performance.now() - this.startMs) / 1000);
      gl.uniform3fv(this.bgUniforms.uColorA, this.colorA);
      gl.uniform3fv(this.bgUniforms.uColorB, this.colorB);
      gl.drawArrays(gl.TRIANGLE_STRIP, 0, 4);

      // ── Blended layers (orb + particles + bursts) ──
      gl.enable(gl.BLEND);
      gl.blendFunc(gl.SRC_ALPHA, gl.ONE);

      // Orb (size-smoothed so breathe cycle can't exceed 2Hz)
      const targetRadius = Math.min(this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height) * 0.12
        * (1 + mod.overall * 0.5 + mod.envelope * 0.3);
      this._smoothRadius = this._smoothRadius == null
        ? targetRadius
        : this._smoothRadius + (targetRadius - this._smoothRadius) * 0.08;
      gl.useProgram(this.orbProg);
      gl.bindBuffer(gl.ARRAY_BUFFER, this.quad);
      const orbAPos = gl.getAttribLocation(this.orbProg, 'aPos');
      gl.enableVertexAttribArray(orbAPos);
      gl.vertexAttribPointer(orbAPos, 2, gl.FLOAT, false, 0, 0);
      gl.uniform2f(this.orbUniforms.uResolution, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);
      gl.uniform2f(this.orbUniforms.uCenter, 0, 0);
      gl.uniform1f(this.orbUniforms.uRadius, this._smoothRadius);
      gl.uniform3f(this.orbUniforms.uColor, 0.6 + mod.bass * 0.4, 0.8, Math.max(0, 1.0 - mod.bass * 0.3));
      gl.uniform1f(this.orbUniforms.uGlow, 0.4 + mod.envelope * 0.6);
      gl.drawArrays(gl.TRIANGLE_STRIP, 0, 4);

      // Particle ring
      gl.useProgram(this.particleProg);
      gl.bindBuffer(gl.ARRAY_BUFFER, this.particleBuf);
      const partAPhase = gl.getAttribLocation(this.particleProg, 'aPhase');
      gl.enableVertexAttribArray(partAPhase);
      gl.vertexAttribPointer(partAPhase, 1, gl.FLOAT, false, 0, 0);
      gl.uniform1f(this.particleUniforms.uTime, (performance.now() - this.startMs) / 1000);
      gl.uniform1f(this.particleUniforms.uRadius, Math.min(this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height) * 0.28 + mod.bass * 80);
      gl.uniform1f(this.particleUniforms.uPtSize, 4);
      gl.uniform2f(this.particleUniforms.uResolution, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);
      gl.uniform1f(this.particleUniforms.uSpin, 0.1 + mod.overall * 0.8);
      gl.uniform3f(this.particleUniforms.uColor, 0.8, 0.9, 1.0);
      gl.drawArrays(gl.POINTS, 0, this._particleCount);

      // Bloom bursts — reuse orb shader for each petal
      gl.useProgram(this.orbProg);
      gl.bindBuffer(gl.ARRAY_BUFFER, this.quad);
      gl.enableVertexAttribArray(orbAPos);
      gl.vertexAttribPointer(orbAPos, 2, gl.FLOAT, false, 0, 0);
      for (const burst of this.bursts) {
        if (burst.spawnTime < 0) continue;
        const age = (performance.now() - burst.spawnTime) / 1000;
        if (age >= 1.0) { burst.spawnTime = -1; continue; }
        // Asymmetric fade — 150ms in, 850ms out (strobe-safe per spec §7)
        const alpha = age < 0.15 ? age / 0.15 : (1 - (age - 0.15) / 0.85);
        const dist = age * Math.min(this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height) * 0.45;
        for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
          const theta = burst.angleBase + (i / 20) * Math.PI * 2;
          gl.uniform2f(this.orbUniforms.uCenter, Math.cos(theta) * dist, Math.sin(theta) * dist);
          gl.uniform1f(this.orbUniforms.uRadius, 8);
          gl.uniform3f(this.orbUniforms.uColor, 1.0, 0.85, 0.6);
          gl.uniform1f(this.orbUniforms.uGlow, alpha * 1.5);
          gl.drawArrays(gl.TRIANGLE_STRIP, 0, 4);
        }
      }
      gl.uniform2f(this.orbUniforms.uCenter, 0, 0); // reset for next frame

      gl.disable(gl.BLEND);
    },

    _renderCanvas2D(mod) {
      const ctx = this.ctx2d;
      const W = this.canvas.width, H = this.canvas.height;
      // Soft trail
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(10,10,12,0.15)';
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
      // Background radial gradient
      const rgb = (c) => `rgb(${Math.round(c[0]*255)},${Math.round(c[1]*255)},${Math.round(c[2]*255)})`;
      const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2, H/2, 0, W/2, H/2, Math.max(W, H) * 0.7);
      grad.addColorStop(0, rgb(this.colorA));
      grad.addColorStop(1, rgb(this.colorB));
      ctx.fillStyle = grad;
      ctx.globalAlpha = 0.12;
      ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
      ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
      // Central orb
      const targetR = Math.min(W, H) * 0.12 * (1 + mod.overall * 0.5 + mod.envelope * 0.3);
      this._smoothRadius = this._smoothRadius == null ? targetR : this._smoothRadius + (targetR - this._smoothRadius) * 0.08;
      const orbR = this._smoothRadius;
      const orbGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2, H/2, 0, W/2, H/2, orbR);
      orbGrad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(220,240,255,0.9)');
      orbGrad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(120,180,240,0)');
      ctx.fillStyle = orbGrad;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(W/2, H/2, orbR, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.fill();
      // Orbiting particles (50, half the WebGL count — perf parity)
      const t = (performance.now() - this.startMs) / 1000;
      const spin = 0.1 + mod.overall * 0.8;
      const particleR = Math.min(W, H) * 0.28 + mod.bass * 60;
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(200,230,255,0.7)';
      const count = Math.min(50, this._particleCount);
      for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        const angle = (i / count) * Math.PI * 2 + t * spin;
        const x = W/2 + Math.cos(angle) * particleR;
        const y = H/2 + Math.sin(angle) * particleR;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x, y, 2, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.fill();
      }
      // Bursts
      for (const burst of this.bursts) {
        if (burst.spawnTime < 0) continue;
        const age = (performance.now() - burst.spawnTime) / 1000;
        if (age >= 1.0) { burst.spawnTime = -1; continue; }
        const alpha = age < 0.15 ? age / 0.15 : (1 - (age - 0.15) / 0.85);
        const dist = age * Math.min(W, H) * 0.45;
        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255,210,140,${alpha})`;
        ctx.lineWidth = 2;
        for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
          const theta = burst.angleBase + (i / 20) * Math.PI * 2;
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(W/2 + Math.cos(theta) * 40, H/2 + Math.sin(theta) * 40);
          ctx.lineTo(W/2 + Math.cos(theta) * (40 + dist), H/2 + Math.sin(theta) * (40 + dist));
          ctx.stroke();
        }
      }
    },

    stop() {
      if (this._rafHandle) { cancelAnimationFrame(this._rafHandle); this._rafHandle = null; }
      if (this._ro) { this._ro.disconnect(); this._ro = null; }
      if (this.canvas && this.canvas.parentNode) this.canvas.parentNode.removeChild(this.canvas);
      this.canvas = this.gl = this.ctx2d = null;
      this.mode = null;
    },
  };

  function setupVisual(visualType) {
    const stage = $('stage');
    // Clean up previous visuals
    if (vizRAF) { cancelAnimationFrame(vizRAF); vizRAF = null; }
    if (highwayRAF) { cancelAnimationFrame(highwayRAF); highwayRAF = null; }
    if (stageResizeObs) { stageResizeObs.disconnect(); stageResizeObs = null; }
    if (neuralBloomRenderer && neuralBloomRenderer.mode) neuralBloomRenderer.stop();
    Array.from(stage.children).forEach(c => {
      if (!c.classList.contains('fixation-dot') && !c.classList.contains('audio-indicator')
        && !c.classList.contains('persona-indicator') && !c.classList.contains('method-indicator')
        && !c.classList.contains('session-progress-wrap')) c.remove();
    });

    // Neural Bloom — WebGL flagship (spec §4)
    if (visualType === 'neural-bloom') {
      neuralBloomRenderer.start(stage);
      return;
    }

    // Canvas-based renderer (new visual types)
    const renderer = VIZ_RENDERERS[visualType];
    if (renderer) {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas'); canvas.className = 'highway-canvas';
      canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight;
      stage.insertBefore(canvas, stage.firstChild);
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      const color = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue('--accent').trim() || '#6b94b8';
      // Resize observer
      stageResizeObs = new ResizeObserver(() => { canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight; });
      stageResizeObs.observe(stage);
      (function draw(ts) {
        if (state.abortFlag) return;
        const speed = (PHASE_VIZ_SPEED[state._currentPhase] || 1.0) * (state.vizSettings.speed || 1.0);
        renderer(ctx, canvas.width, canvas.height, (ts/1000)*speed, color);
        vizRAF = requestAnimationFrame(draw);
      })(0);
      return;
    }

    if (visualType === 'highway') {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas'); canvas.className = 'highway-canvas';
      canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight;
      stage.insertBefore(canvas, stage.firstChild);
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      // Resize observer
      stageResizeObs = new ResizeObserver(() => { canvas.width = stage.clientWidth; canvas.height = stage.clientHeight; });
      stageResizeObs.observe(stage);
      const lines = []; for (let i = 0; i < 8; i++) lines.push({ y: (canvas.height / 8) * i, speed: 1.2 + Math.random() * 0.4 });
      (function draw() {
        if (state.abortFlag) return;
        const mod = getAudioMod();
        const W = canvas.width, H = canvas.height;
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        // Line width pulses with bass (base 4, max +2.4 with full bass)
        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(212,220,232,0.55)'; ctx.lineWidth = 4 + mod.bass * 2.4;
        // Line speed × (1 + overall * 0.6)
        const speedMul = 1 + mod.overall * 0.6;
        lines.forEach(l => { l.y += l.speed * speedMul; if (l.y > H + 40) l.y = -40; ctx.globalAlpha = Math.min(1,(l.y/H)*1.2)*0.7; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(W/2, l.y); ctx.lineTo(W/2, l.y+28); ctx.stroke(); });
        ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
        const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2, H*0.38, 20, W/2, H*0.38, H*0.5); g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(0,0,0,0)'); g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)');
        ctx.fillStyle = g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        highwayRAF = requestAnimationFrame(draw);
      })();
    } else if (visualType === 'spiral') {
      const svg = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg','svg');
      svg.setAttribute('class','spiral-svg'); svg.setAttribute('viewBox','0 0 100 100');
      let d = 'M 50 50 ';
      for (let t=0;t<30;t+=0.1) { const r=0.5*t; d += `L ${(50+r*Math.cos(t)).toFixed(2)} ${(50+r*Math.sin(t)).toFixed(2)} `; }
      const p = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg','path');
      p.setAttribute('d',d); p.setAttribute('stroke','rgba(107,148,184,0.4)'); p.setAttribute('stroke-width','0.4'); p.setAttribute('fill','none');
      svg.appendChild(p); stage.insertBefore(svg, stage.firstChild);
    } else {
      // Default: CSS pulse rings
      const wrap = document.createElement('div'); wrap.className = 'pulse-rings';
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) { const r = document.createElement('div'); r.className = 'pulse-ring'; wrap.appendChild(r); }
      stage.insertBefore(wrap, stage.firstChild);
    }
  }
  const stopVisuals = () => {
    if (highwayRAF) cancelAnimationFrame(highwayRAF); highwayRAF = null;
    if (vizRAF) cancelAnimationFrame(vizRAF); vizRAF = null;
    if (stageResizeObs) { stageResizeObs.disconnect(); stageResizeObs = null; }
    if (neuralBloomRenderer && neuralBloomRenderer.mode) neuralBloomRenderer.stop();
  };

  // ====================================================================
  // PERSONA EDITOR
  // ====================================================================
  function openPersonaEditor(id) {
    state.editingPersonaId = id;
    $('personaModalTitle').textContent = id ? 'edit persona' : 'create custom persona';
    if (id) {
      const p = state.personas.find(x => x.id === id);
      $('personaFormName').value = p.name;
      $('personaFormTagline').value = p.tagline;
      $('personaFormPrompt').value = getPersonaRole(p);
      $('personaFormCategory').value = p.category || 'contemplative';
      // v2 advanced fields
      $('personaFormReminder').value         = p.reminderMessage   || '';
      $('personaFormImagePrefix').value      = p.imagePromptPrefix || '';
      $('personaFormImageSuffix').value      = p.imagePromptSuffix || '';
      $('personaFormMetaTitle').value        = p.metaTitle         || '';
      $('personaFormMetaDescription').value  = p.metaDescription   || '';
      $('personaFormRecommendedRate').value  = p.recommendedSpeechRate ?? '';
      $('personaFormRecommendedVisual').value = p.recommendedVisual    || '';
      $('personaFormRecommendedSound').value  = p.recommendedSoundscape || '';
    } else {
      $('personaFormName').value = '';
      $('personaFormTagline').value = '';
      $('personaFormPrompt').value = '';
      $('personaFormCategory').value = 'contemplative';
      // Clear v2 advanced fields too
      ['personaFormReminder','personaFormImagePrefix','personaFormImageSuffix',
       'personaFormMetaTitle','personaFormMetaDescription','personaFormRecommendedRate',
       'personaFormRecommendedVisual','personaFormRecommendedSound'].forEach(id => {
        const el = $(id); if (el) el.value = '';
      });
    }
    $('personaModal').classList.add('visible');
  }
  const closePersonaEditor = () => { $('personaModal').classList.remove('visible'); state.editingPersonaId = null; };
  function savePersonaFromForm() {
    const name = $('personaFormName').value.trim();
    const tagline = $('personaFormTagline').value.trim();
    const role = $('personaFormPrompt').value.trim();
    const category = $('personaFormCategory').value || 'contemplative';
    if (!name || !role) { notify.warn('Name and voice instruction required.'); return; }

    // Collect v2 advanced fields. Empty strings → null/empty so normalizePersona's
    // defaults apply on next read. Number field guarded with NaN-check.
    const rateRaw = parseFloat($('personaFormRecommendedRate').value);
    const v2Fields = {
      reminderMessage:       ($('personaFormReminder').value          || '').trim().slice(0, 500),
      imagePromptPrefix:     ($('personaFormImagePrefix').value       || '').trim().slice(0, 200),
      imagePromptSuffix:     ($('personaFormImageSuffix').value       || '').trim().slice(0, 200),
      metaTitle:             ($('personaFormMetaTitle').value         || '').trim().slice(0, 100),
      metaDescription:       ($('personaFormMetaDescription').value   || '').trim().slice(0, 200),
      recommendedSpeechRate: Number.isFinite(rateRaw) ? Math.max(0.5, Math.min(2.0, rateRaw)) : null,
      recommendedVisual:     ($('personaFormRecommendedVisual').value || '').trim().slice(0, 40) || null,
      recommendedSoundscape: ($('personaFormRecommendedSound').value  || '').trim().slice(0, 40) || null,
    };

    let custom = loadCustomPersonas();
    if (state.editingPersonaId) {
      // Edit existing — preserve uuid, creationTime, customData; merge new values
      custom = custom.map(p => p.id === state.editingPersonaId
        ? normalizePersona({ ...p, name, tagline, roleInstruction: role, category, ...v2Fields })
        : p);
    } else {
      // New persona — normalizePersona auto-assigns uuid + creationTime
      const id = 'custom_' + Date.now();
      custom.push(normalizePersona({ id, name, tagline: tagline || '(custom)', roleInstruction: role, category, ...v2Fields }));
      state.selectedPersonaId = id;
      markFeatureUsed(FEAT.CUSTOM_PERSONA); // mark feature only when a NEW custom persona is created
    }
    if (!saveCustomPersonas(custom)) { notify.error('Could not save: browser storage may be full.'); return; }
    refreshPersonas(); renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail(); closePersonaEditor();
  }
  async function deletePersona(id) {
    if (!await confirmAsync('Delete this persona?')) return;
    saveCustomPersonas(loadCustomPersonas().filter(p => p.id !== id));
    if (state.selectedPersonaId === id) state.selectedPersonaId = 'driver';
    // Drop the cached portrait too — orphan blobs would just bloat IDB
    personaPortraitDelete(id).catch(() => {});
    refreshPersonas(); renderPersonaGrid(); renderPersonaDetail();
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // CRAFTER
  // ====================================================================
  let _aiInProgress = false; // Prevents double-click firing two concurrent AI calls

  async function craftSuggestion() {
    if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('An AI call is already in progress.'); return; }
    // Resolve \{\{...\}\} tokens before feeding the AI so the model sees concrete text.
    const rough = resolveTokens($('intentionInput').value.trim());
    const skipTypes = ['trance', 'sleep'];
    if (!rough && !skipTypes.includes(state.intentionType)) { notify.warn('Describe what you want first.'); return; }
    const type = INTENTION_TYPES[state.intentionType];
    if (!type) { notify.warn('Select an intention type first.'); return; }
    _aiInProgress = true;
    const progressLabel = $('craftProgressLabel');
    setLoading('craftBtn', true);
    setLoading('recraftBtn', true);
    $('craftProgress').classList.add('visible');
    progressLabel.textContent = 'crafting your suggestion — about 2–3 minutes...';
    const stopTimer = makeElapsedTimer(s => { progressLabel.textContent = `crafting... ${s}s elapsed`; });

    // Token-budgeted prompt assembly. The JSON-output schema and
    // universal rules are priority-5 (never trimmed); profile context trims
    // first if we're near the context limit.
    const headerBlock = `You are a master hypnotherapist converting a user's rough intention into a technically-precise hypnotic suggestion.

TYPE: ${type.label}
USER'S ROUGH DESCRIPTION: "${rough}"

UNIVERSAL RULES:
• Second person ("you")
• Presupposition ("you'll notice" not "you will feel") [For convincer/novelty: direct present-tense fine]
• Somatic anchoring (tie states to physical sensations)
• Automaticity ("automatically", "without effort")
• Progressive intensification
• Future-pacing ("from now on")
• Positive construction only
• Specificity

TYPE-SPECIFIC GUIDANCE:
${type.guidance}`;
    const profileBlock = getProfileContext();
    const schemaBlock = `
Output EXACTLY this JSON, no other text, no markdown fences:
{
  "craftedSuggestion": "Complete hypnotic suggestion, 3-5 sentences, ready to deliver verbatim. Second person.",
  "trigger": "Specific trigger phrase, or 'ongoing state'",
  "coreResponse": "Specific response/effect, 3-7 words",
  "reinforcementPhrases": ["Three or four short variants (5-10 words)"],
  "explanation": "ONE sentence on the technique used"
}`;
    const instruction = trimToTokenBudget([
      { name: 'header',   text: headerBlock,  priority: 5 },
      { name: 'profile',  text: profileBlock, priority: 2 },
      { name: 'schema',   text: schemaBlock,  priority: 5 },
    ], 600);

    try {
      const data = await root.aiTextPlugin({ instruction, startWith: '{', stopSequences: ['\n\n\n'], hideStartWith: true });
      // guard against error status AND empty output
      if (!data || data.stopReason === 'error') throw new Error('AI generation encountered an error.');
      let text = (data.generatedText || '').trim();
      if (!text) throw new Error('AI returned empty text — please try again.');
      if (!text.startsWith('{')) text = '{' + text;
      const lb = text.lastIndexOf('}'); if (lb > -1) text = text.substring(0, lb + 1);
      state.craftedSuggestion = JSON.parse(text);
      showCrafted();
      updateStepUI();
      notify.success('Suggestion crafted successfully.');
    } catch (e) { console.error(e); notify.warn('Crafting failed: ' + e.message + '. Try again.'); }
    finally {
      _aiInProgress = false;
      stopTimer();
      setLoading('craftBtn', false, 'craft hypnotic suggestion →');
      setLoading('recraftBtn', false);
      $('craftProgress').classList.remove('visible');
    }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // AFFIRMATION AUTO-FILL — Smart Director drafts from profile + intention
  // ====================================================================
  // When the user's affirmation textarea is empty (Step 4) and Smart Director
  // is enabled, the user can click "✨ generate from profile" to have the AI
  // draft 3-5 affirmations tailored to their profile, current intention, and
  // selected persona/method. The textarea remains editable — generation just
  // gives the user a starting point.
  //
  // Design choices:
  //   • Manual trigger (button click) — never auto-fires on step entry, so
  //     the user is always in control of when API calls happen.
  //   • Confirms before overwrite if the textarea has content.
  //   • Uses the same _aiInProgress single-flight gate as craftSuggestion to
  //     prevent overlapping AI calls.
  //   • If Smart Director is off, the button is disabled (not hidden) with a
  //     tooltip pointing the user to the toggle.
  //   • Output respects the 500-char input limit and is shaped as one
  //     affirmation per line (matching the textarea's expected format).
  // ====================================================================
  async function generateAffirmationsFromProfile() {
    if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('An AI call is already in progress.'); return; }
    if (state.smartDirectorEnabled === false) {
      notify.warn('Enable Smart Director (Settings) to use profile-driven generation.');
      return;
    }
    const textarea = $('userAffirmations');
    if (!textarea) return;
    const existing = textarea.value.trim();
    if (existing) {
      const ok = await confirmAsync('Replace your existing affirmations with AI-drafted ones?');
      if (!ok) return;
    }

    _aiInProgress = true;
    const btn = $('generateAffirmationsBtn');
    const label = $('generateAffirmationsBtnLabel');
    const hint = $('generateAffirmationsHint');
    if (btn) btn.disabled = true;
    if (label) label.textContent = '⏳ drafting…';
    if (hint) hint.textContent = '';
    const stopTimer = makeElapsedTimer(s => { if (label) label.textContent = `⏳ drafting… ${s}s`; });

    try {
      // Build the prompt. Profile context provides about/goals/experience,
      // intention type provides the directional purpose, persona provides voice.
      const persona = getPersona();
      const method = getMethod();
      const intention = resolveTokens($('intentionInput')?.value?.trim() || '');
      const intentionType = INTENTION_TYPES[state.intentionType] || INTENTION_TYPES.emotional;
      const profileBlock = getProfileContext(); // already gated on Smart Director

      // Phase 5: pull the persona's full role text (with signature phrases and
      // vocabulary) into the prompt so the affirmations come out IN VOICE.
      // Previously we used only persona.tagline, which produced voice-neutral
      // affirmations regardless of who the guide was.
      const personaRole = getPersonaRole(persona);
      const voiceBlock = personaRole
        ? `\n\nPERSONA VOICE — match this completely:\n${personaRole}\n\nThe affirmations MUST sound like ${persona.name} wrote them. Pull from the vocabulary, cadence, and signature phrasing above.`
        : '';

      const headerBlock = `You are ${persona.name}, drafting personal affirmations for the listener's hypnosis session.

The listener did not write their own affirmations and asked you to draft some. Generate 3-5 affirmations they will hear during the session, in your voice.

INTENTION TYPE: ${intentionType.label}
USER'S INTENTION: "${intention || '(none specified — use the profile and intention type as guidance)'}"
METHOD: ${method.name}`;

      const rulesBlock = `
AFFIRMATION RULES:
• First person, present tense ("I am…", "I notice…", "I allow…")
• Short — 4 to 12 words each
• Positively framed (state what IS, not what isn't)
• Specific to the user's profile and intention — not generic platitudes
• Each line should stand alone as a complete suggestion
• Use the user's pronouns and any specific details from their profile
• Avoid clichés like "I am enough" — be specific to what the user is working on
• CRITICAL: Match the persona voice above. A Commander's affirmations sound like commands. The Inner Voice's affirmations sound like a thought just below words. The Old Master's are short and elemental. Don't write generic affirmations.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
One affirmation per line. No numbering, no bullets, no quotes around lines, no preamble, no commentary. Just the affirmations themselves, separated by newlines. 3-5 lines total.`;

      const instruction = trimToTokenBudget([
        { name: 'header',   text: headerBlock,  priority: 5 },
        { name: 'voice',    text: voiceBlock,   priority: 5 }, // voice is non-negotiable
        { name: 'profile',  text: profileBlock, priority: 3 },
        { name: 'rules',    text: rulesBlock,   priority: 5 },
      ], 600); // bumped from 400 to make room for the voice block

      const result = await aiGenerate(instruction, { stopSequences: ['\n\n', '\n---'] });
      // aiGenerate returns { generatedText, stopReason } — was checking result.text (always undefined)
      if (!result || !result.generatedText) throw new Error(result?._note || 'no text returned');

      // Parse: split on newlines, drop empties, drop any quoted/numbered/bulleted prefixes
      // the model adds despite the format instruction. Keep at most 5 lines.
      const lines = result.generatedText.split('\n')
        .map(l => l.trim())
        .filter(Boolean)
        // Strip leading bullets, numbers, dashes, quotes that the model may add
        .map(l => l.replace(/^[-•*\d.)\s]+/, '').replace(/^["'""'']\s*/, '').replace(/\s*["'""'']\s*$/, '').trim())
        .filter(l => l.length >= 3 && l.length <= 200) // sanity bounds
        .slice(0, 5);

      if (lines.length === 0) throw new Error('AI output had no usable affirmations');

      const joined = lines.join('\n');
      // Respect the 500-char input cap (used downstream by buildSettingsObj URL encoder)
      textarea.value = joined.slice(0, 500);
      // Programmatic value change does NOT fire input event — manually ping the DiffBouncer
      // so this counts as a tracked change in the profile changeLog.
      diffBouncers.userAffirmations?.ping();
      // Trigger updateStepUI so the step indicator reflects the now-filled state
      if (typeof updateStepUI === 'function') updateStepUI();
      // Persist to settings so a reload preserves the generated affirmations
      saveUserSettings();

      notify.success(`Drafted ${lines.length} affirmation${lines.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} from your profile.`);
      if (hint) hint.textContent = 'You can edit these freely — they\'re just a starting point.';
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('[affirmations] generation failed:', e);
      notify.warn('Could not draft affirmations: ' + (e.message || 'unknown error'));
    } finally {
      _aiInProgress = false;
      stopTimer();
      _refreshAffirmationsBtnState();
    }
  }

  /** Update the affirmation generator button label + enabled state based on
   *  current textarea content + Smart Director state. Called after typing,
   *  after generation, after Smart Director toggle. Idempotent. */
  function _refreshAffirmationsBtnState() {
    const btn = $('generateAffirmationsBtn');
    const label = $('generateAffirmationsBtnLabel');
    const hint = $('generateAffirmationsHint');
    if (!btn || !label) return;
    const sdOn = state.smartDirectorEnabled !== false;
    const hasContent = !!($('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim());
    btn.disabled = !sdOn || _aiInProgress;
    if (!sdOn) {
      label.textContent = '✨ generate from profile';
      btn.title = 'Smart Director must be enabled (in Settings) to use profile-driven generation';
      if (hint) hint.textContent = 'Smart Director is off — enable it in Settings to use this.';
    } else if (_aiInProgress) {
      btn.title = 'Another AI call is in progress';
    } else {
      label.textContent = hasContent ? '✨ regenerate' : '✨ generate from profile';
      btn.title = hasContent
        ? 'Replace your affirmations with newly drafted ones'
        : 'Drafts a few affirmations from your profile and intention';
      if (hint && hint.textContent.startsWith('Smart Director is off')) hint.textContent = '';
    }
  }

  function showCrafted() {
    const c = state.craftedSuggestion;
    $('craftedText').textContent = c.craftedSuggestion;
    $('craftedText').style.display = 'block';
    $('craftedEditable').style.display = 'none';
    $('saveEditBtn').style.display = 'none';
    $('craftedMeta').innerHTML = `<strong>trigger:</strong> ${escapeHtml(c.trigger||'—')}  ·  <strong>effect:</strong> ${escapeHtml(c.coreResponse||'—')}<br><strong>technique:</strong> ${escapeHtml(c.explanation||'—')}`;
    $('craftedPreview').classList.add('visible');
  }
  function hideCrafted() { state.craftedSuggestion = null; $('craftedPreview').classList.remove('visible'); hideScript(); }
  function toggleEditCrafted() {
    const t = $('craftedText'), e = $('craftedEditable'), s = $('saveEditBtn');
    e.value = state.craftedSuggestion.craftedSuggestion;
    t.style.display = 'none'; e.style.display = 'block'; s.style.display = 'inline-block';
  }
  function saveEditCrafted() {
    state.craftedSuggestion.craftedSuggestion = $('craftedEditable').value.trim();
    showCrafted(); hideScript();
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SCRIPT GEN — per-phase generation with live progress
  // ====================================================================

  /** Session work block count by selected length */
  function getWorkBlockCount() {
    if (state.length === 'marathon') return 8;
    if (state.length === 'deep')     return 7;
    if (state.length === 'extended') return 6;
    if (state.length === 'long')     return 5;
    if (state.length === 'medium')   return 2;
    return 1;
  }

  function getPhaseLabel(phaseId) {
    if (!phaseId) return 'Phase';
    const base = phaseId.replace(/-\d+$/, '');
    const idx = phaseId.includes('-') ? phaseId.split('-').pop() : '';
    const labels = {
      settling: 'Settling',
      induction: 'Induction',
      deepener: idx ? `Deepener ${idx}` : 'Deepener',
      lightener: idx ? `Lightener ${idx}` : 'Lightener',
      wake: 'Wake',
      reintroduction: 'Reintroduction',
      emergence: 'Emergence',
      work: idx ? `Work ${idx}` : 'Work',
      affirm: idx ? `Affirmation ${idx}` : 'Affirmation',
      sounding: idx ? `Sounding ${idx}` : 'Sounding',
      custom: idx ? `Custom ${idx}` : 'Custom',
    };
    return labels[base] || phaseId;
  }

  function phaseIdToMarker(phaseId) {
    return String(phaseId || 'work').toUpperCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
  }

  function markerToPhaseId(marker) {
    return String(marker || '').toLowerCase();
  }

  const PHASE_MARKER_CAPTURE_RX = /===\s*([A-Z0-9-]+)\s*===/gi;
  const PHASE_MARKER_SPLIT_RX = /(===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===)/gi;
  const PHASE_MARKER_STRIP_RX = /===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===/gi;

  function stripLeadingPhaseHeader(text, phaseId = '') {
    let out = String(text || '').replace(/^﻿/, '').trimStart();
    // Canonical marker line, including numbered phases like WORK-1 / AFFIRM-2
    out = out.replace(/^===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===\s*(?:\r?\n)?/i, '');
    // Markdown / label-only heading lines at the top of a generated phase
    const base = String(phaseId || '').replace(/-\d+$/, '');
    const num = (String(phaseId || '').match(/-(\d+)$/) || [])[1];
    const labelMap = {
      settling: 'settling',
      induction: 'induction',
      deepener: 'deepener',
      lightener: 'lightener',
      wake: 'wake',
      reintroduction: 'reintroduction',
      emergence: 'emergence',
      work: num ? `work(?:\s*[-:]?\s*${num})?` : 'work(?:\s*[-:]?\s*\d+)?',
      affirm: num ? `affirm(?:ation)?(?:\s*[-:]?\s*${num})?` : 'affirm(?:ation)?(?:\s*[-:]?\s*\d+)?',
    };
    const phaseRx = labelMap[base];
    if (phaseRx) {
      const headingOnly = new RegExp(`^(?:[#>*-]+\s*)?(?:phase\s*[:\-]\s*)?(?:${phaseRx})\s*:?(?:\r?\n)+`, 'i');
      out = out.replace(headingOnly, '');
      const bareLine = new RegExp(`^(?:phase\s*[:\-]\s*)?(?:${phaseRx})\s*:?\s*(?:\r?\n)+`, 'i');
      out = out.replace(bareLine, '');
    }
    return out.trim();
  }
