  function stripAllPhaseMarkers(text) {
    return String(text || '').replace(/===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===/gi, ' ');
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // PHASE PAIRS — Induction↔Emergence, Deepener↔Lightener (nestable)
  // ====================================================================
  /**
   * "Trance entry" pair: an Induction must be matched by wake + reintroduction
   * (the two phases that together form Emergence).
   * "Depth" pair: every Deepener must be matched by a Lightener. Multiple
   * Deepeners can be nested; their Lighteners unwind in reverse (LIFO).
   *
   * Sleep sessions (state.intentionType === 'sleep') deliberately skip the
   * trance-entry closers — the user is meant to drift into natural sleep.
   */
  const PHASE_BASE_RX = /-\d+$/;
  const phaseBase = id => String(id || '').replace(PHASE_BASE_RX, '');

  const PHASE_PAIR_GROUP = {
    induction: 'trance',
    wake: 'trance',
    reintroduction: 'trance',
    deepener: 'depth',
    lightener: 'depth',
  };
  /** Phases that must exist at end of session for a "safe" finish. */
  const SAFE_ENDING_PHASES = ['lightener', 'wake', 'reintroduction'];

  /**
   * Default structure per spec:
   *   \{\{Settling\}\} \{\{Induction\}\} \{\{Deepener\}\} -> (\{\{Work\}\}, \{\{Affirm\}\}) x N -> \{\{Lightener\}\} \{\{Wake\}\} \{\{Reintroduction\}\}
   * Sleep intention skips the ending trio (drifts into sleep).
   */
  function getSessionPhaseBlueprint() {
    // Marathon length doubles the descent: two deepener phases on the way
    // down, two lighteners on the way back up (LIFO unwind, mirrored).
    // Other lengths use a single deepener+lightener pair.
    const deepenerCount = state.length === 'marathon' ? 2 : 1;
    const phases = ['settling', 'induction'];
    for (let d = 1; d <= deepenerCount; d++) {
      phases.push(deepenerCount > 1 ? `deepener-${d}` : 'deepener');
    }
    const workCount = getWorkBlockCount();
    const userAff = $('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim();
    const hasAff = !!userAff;
    for (let i = 1; i <= workCount; i++) {
      // (Work, Affirm) pair — affirm follows each work when user has affirmations
      phases.push(workCount > 1 ? `work-${i}` : 'work');
      if (hasAff) phases.push(workCount > 1 ? `affirm-${i}` : 'affirm');
    }
    if (state.intentionType === 'sleep') return phases;
    // Mirror the deepener depth on the way out — innermost lightener first,
    // unwinding back to surface awareness layer by layer.
    for (let l = deepenerCount; l >= 1; l--) {
      phases.push(deepenerCount > 1 ? `lightener-${l}` : 'lightener');
    }
    phases.push('wake', 'reintroduction');
    return phases;
  }

  /**
   * Count how many Deepener and Lightener phases are currently in sections,
   * used to determine nesting depth when adding another.
   */
  function countPhaseBase(sections, base) {
    return sections.filter(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === base).length;
  }

  /**
   * Find the insertion index for a new phase of a given kind, respecting the
   * canonical order: settling → induction → deepeners → (work/affirm) → lighteners → wake → reintro.
   * Returns an index into `sections` where the new phase should be spliced in.
   */
  function findPhaseInsertionIdx(sections, kind) {
    const idxOf = (pred) => sections.findIndex(pred);
    const lastIdxOf = (pred) => {
      let last = -1;
      sections.forEach((s, i) => { if (pred(s)) last = i; });
      return last;
    };
    if (kind === 'settling') {
      return 0; // always first
    }
    if (kind === 'induction') {
      // After last settling, before first deepener/work/lightener/wake/reintro
      const afterSettling = lastIdxOf(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'settling');
      const anchor = idxOf(s => ['deepener','work','affirm','lightener','wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (anchor >= 0) return anchor;
      if (afterSettling >= 0) return afterSettling + 1;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'deepener') {
      // After last existing deepener (nesting), before first work/affirm
      const lastDeepener = lastIdxOf(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'deepener');
      if (lastDeepener >= 0) return lastDeepener + 1;
      // Otherwise after induction, before work
      const afterInduction = lastIdxOf(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'induction');
      const beforeWork = idxOf(s => ['work','affirm','lightener','wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (beforeWork >= 0) return beforeWork;
      if (afterInduction >= 0) return afterInduction + 1;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'work' || kind === 'affirm') {
      // Before first lightener/wake/reintro; after last existing work/affirm
      const beforeReturn = idxOf(s => ['lightener','wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (beforeReturn >= 0) return beforeReturn;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'lightener') {
      // After last work/affirm, before wake (LIFO unwind — outermost lightener last)
      const lastWork = lastIdxOf(s => ['work','affirm'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      const firstWake = idxOf(s => ['wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (firstWake >= 0) {
        // Insert immediately before the first wake, so the newest lightener
        // sits closest to wake (LIFO: later-added deepeners get closed first).
        return firstWake;
      }
      if (lastWork >= 0) return lastWork + 1;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'wake') {
      const reintroIdx = idxOf(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'reintroduction');
      if (reintroIdx >= 0) return reintroIdx;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'reintroduction') {
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'sounding') {
      // Sounding (depth check / witness moment) — slot AFTER deepener and
      // BEFORE work so the user takes a meta-awareness pause at the bottom of
      // the descent before therapeutic work begins. Subsequent soundings
      // (multiple) stack at the same canonical position; user can move with
      // up/down arrows.
      const lastDeepener = lastIdxOf(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'deepener');
      const beforeWork = idxOf(s => ['work','affirm','lightener','wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (beforeWork >= 0) return beforeWork;
      if (lastDeepener >= 0) return lastDeepener + 1;
      return sections.length;
    }
    if (kind === 'custom') {
      // Custom (user-authored) — default to before lightener (i.e. inside the
      // trance work zone, after work blocks). User can re-arrange freely with
      // up/down arrows; this is just a sensible initial slot.
      const beforeReturn = idxOf(s => ['lightener','wake','reintroduction'].includes(phaseBase(s.phaseId)));
      if (beforeReturn >= 0) return beforeReturn;
      return sections.length;
    }
    return sections.length;
  }

  function getPhaseList() {
    return getSessionPhaseBlueprint();
  }

  function getPlaybackPhaseOrder() {
    if (state.generatedPhaseOrder?.length) return [...state.generatedPhaseOrder];
    if (state.parsedScript?.ordered?.length) return [...state.parsedScript.ordered];
    return getPhaseList();
  }

  /** Render phase progress with state: pending, streaming, done, error, warn */
  function renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, eta, retryCallback) {
    const wrap = $('genProgress');
    const container = $('genPhases');
    const etaEl = $('genEta');
    if (!wrap || !container) return;
    wrap.style.display = 'block';
    container.innerHTML = phases.map((p, i) => {
      const label = getPhaseLabel(p);
      const st = stateMask[i] || 'pending';
      return `<div class="gen-phase ${st}" data-phase-idx="${i}"><div class="gen-dot"></div><span>${label}</span></div>`;
    }).join('');
    if (etaEl) etaEl.textContent = eta || '';
    // Streaming preview box — ensure it exists under the phase list.
    if (!$('genStreamBox')) {
      const box = document.createElement('div');
      box.id = 'genStreamBox';
      box.className = 'gen-stream-box';
      box.innerHTML = `<div class="gen-stream-label" id="genStreamLabel">generating…</div><div class="gen-stream-text" id="genStreamText"></div>`;
      container.parentNode.insertBefore(box, container.nextSibling);
    }
    if (retryCallback) {
      // error/warn phases are clickable to retry; pending phases become clickable too
      // (for phases added to the list after initial generation — user can trigger them on demand)
      container.querySelectorAll('.gen-phase.error, .gen-phase.warn, .gen-phase.pending').forEach(el => {
        el.addEventListener('click', () => retryCallback(parseInt(el.dataset.phaseIdx)));
      });
    }
  }

  /** Show/update the streaming preview for the phase currently generating. */
  function setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, text, opts = {}) {
    const box = $('genStreamBox'); if (!box) return;
    if (opts.hide) { box.classList.remove('active', 'done'); return; }
    box.classList.add('active');
    if (opts.done) box.classList.add('done'); else box.classList.remove('done');
    const label = $('genStreamLabel');
    const textEl = $('genStreamText');
    if (label) label.textContent = phaseLabel ? `generating · ${phaseLabel.toLowerCase()}` : 'generating…';
    if (textEl) {
      // Truncate displayed text to keep the DOM light on very long phases —
      // tail-biased so user sees fresh content.
      const display = text.length > 1400 ? '…' + text.slice(text.length - 1400) : text;
      textEl.textContent = display;
      // Auto-scroll to bottom so streaming feels like a running transcript.
      box.scrollTop = box.scrollHeight;
    }
  }

  // Generation state held outside so retry can access it
  let _genState = null;

  /**
   * Build per-phase instruction strings from a phase list + context.
   * Pure function — same inputs produce same outputs.
   *
   * Extracted from generateFullScript so it can be called again by
   * syncGenStateWithPhases() when the user adds/removes blocks after
   * the initial generation.
   *
   * @param [string[]] phases       ordered phase IDs (e.g. ['settling','induction','deepener','work-1','affirm-1',...])
   * @param [object]   targetWords  { settling: n, induction: n, ... } word budgets
   * @param [object]   persona      current persona object
   * @param [object]   method       current method object
   * @param [string[]] affirmLines  affirmations (already token-resolved, line-per-entry)
   */
  function buildPhaseInstructions(phases, targetWords, persona, method, affirmLines) {
    const deepenerPhases = phases.filter(p => phaseBase(p) === 'deepener');
    const lightenerPhases = phases.filter(p => phaseBase(p) === 'lightener');
    const totalDepth = deepenerPhases.length;

    const phaseInstructions = {
      settling: `Write the SETTLING phase (~${targetWords.settling} words). Orient the user. Open naturally — don't say "hello". Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY the script text.`,
      induction: `Write the INDUCTION phase (~${targetWords.induction} words). Move from awareness toward trance using ${method.name}. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`,
      wake: `Write the WAKE phase (~${targetWords.wake} words). Bring the user fully awake and alert. Use a distinct upward count or direct waking sequence. Re-alert clearly. Eyes open. Fully awake. This is the actual wake-up phase and must not be replaced by reintroduction. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`,
      reintroduction: `Write the REINTRODUCTION phase (~${targetWords.reintroduction} words). This phase happens AFTER wake. The user is already awake. Include a warm welcome-back, a suggestion to slowly get up only when ready, stretch, shake it off, and continue the day. If this is a demonstration method, the test can be mentioned after wake and before the final welcome-back, but the ending must fully reintroduce the user. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`,
    };

    const deepenerWordsEach = totalDepth > 0 ? Math.round(targetWords.deepener / totalDepth) : targetWords.deepener;
    deepenerPhases.forEach((p, i) => {
      const depth = i + 1;
      let intensity;
      if (totalDepth === 1) intensity = 'light-to-medium trance';
      else if (depth === 1) intensity = 'light trance (first layer)';
      else if (depth === totalDepth) intensity = 'deep trance (innermost layer)';
      else intensity = `medium trance (layer ${depth} of ${totalDepth})`;
      phaseInstructions[p] = `Write DEEPENER phase ${depth} of ${totalDepth} (~${deepenerWordsEach} words). Target state: ${intensity}. ${depth === 1 ? 'Move from post-induction awareness into the first layer of trance.' : `The user is already at layer ${depth - 1}; take them ONE LEVEL deeper, not all the way from waking.`}${state.craftedSuggestion && depth === totalDepth ? ' Foreshadow the crafted suggestion at this innermost layer.' : ''}${affirmLines.length && depth === totalDepth ? ' Begin weaving affirmations.' : ''} Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D. Output ONLY script text.`;
    });

    const lightenerWordsEach = lightenerPhases.length > 0 ? Math.round(targetWords.lightener / lightenerPhases.length) : targetWords.lightener;
    lightenerPhases.forEach((p, i) => {
      const closesDepth = lightenerPhases.length - i;
      const fromDepth = closesDepth;
      const toDepth = closesDepth - 1;
      phaseInstructions[p] = fromDepth === 1
        ? `Write the LIGHTENER phase (~${lightenerWordsEach} words). Ease intensity down gradually from light trance toward waking awareness. Keep the same narrator voice and continuity — this phase works with the narrator rather than stopping them. Use gentle return language, body awareness, orientation, breath, movement, and upward pacing. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`
        : `Write LIGHTENER phase for level ${fromDepth} → ${toDepth} (~${lightenerWordsEach} words). The user is currently at depth ${fromDepth}; bring them up ONE LEVEL toward depth ${toDepth}, not all the way. Subsequent lighteners will continue the ascent. Gentle upward language, breath, light. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D markers. Output ONLY script text.`;
    });

    const workCount = phases.filter(p => phaseBase(p) === 'work').length;
    const workWordsEach = workCount > 0 ? Math.round(targetWords.work / workCount) : targetWords.work;
    phases.forEach(p => {
      const base = phaseBase(p);
      if (base === 'affirm') {
        phaseInstructions[p] = `Write a brief affirmation interlude (~40-60 words). Deliver these affirmations in ${persona.name}'s voice, woven into flowing, hypnotic language:\n${affirmLines.map(l => `"${l}"`).join('\n')}\nUse the user's exact words. Add \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D between each. Poetic, rhythmic, repetitive. Output ONLY script text.`;
      } else if (base === 'sounding') {
        // Sounding (a.k.a. depth check / witness moment) — a meta-awareness
        // pause where the narrator invites the user to register their CURRENT
        // internal state without changing it. Interoceptive prompt; pulled
        // from clinical mindfulness + somatic-experiencing protocols (Levine,
        // Kabat-Zinn). Should feel like coming up for a breath without
        // breaking trance.
        phaseInstructions[p] = `Write a SOUNDING phase (~80-130 words). This is a brief meta-awareness moment — a "depth check" where you invite the user to NOTICE how they feel right now WITHOUT changing it. The narrator pauses the descent or work, lets the user register their own state, then continues.

Tone: gently observing, never directive. The user is the instrument; you're helping them read it.

Touch on (pick 2-3, in ${persona.name}'s voice):
  • the body — weight, warmth, the sit of the hands, the feel of the breath at this moment
  • the mind — the speed and quality of thoughts, what's surfacing
  • the awareness itself — wide or narrow, sharp or soft, near or far
  • emotional weather — what's present, without naming it as good or bad

End with a brief acknowledgment that you're now continuing — bridging back to the surrounding phase. Use \x5BPAUSE 4-7\x5D between observations to give the user time to actually look. Output ONLY script text.`;
      } else if (base === 'custom') {
        // Custom blocks are user-authored — they pass through generation
        // verbatim. We DO NOT issue a prompt for these. The Reimagine button
        // in the editor uses a separate flow (reimagineCustomPhase).
        // Leaving phaseInstructions[p] undefined is safe: generateSinglePhase
        // checks the phaseId and skips custom blocks during generation.
      } else if (base === 'work') {
        const workIdx = p.includes('-') ? parseInt(p.split('-')[1]) : 1;
        let role;
        if (workCount === 1) role = 'single-block: deliver and consolidate.';
        else if (workIdx === 1) role = state.craftedSuggestion ? 'INTRODUCE: deliver the crafted suggestion verbatim for the first time. Plant the seed.' : method.category === 'demonstration' ? 'INTRODUCE: begin building the demonstration effect.' : 'INTRODUCE: establish the core therapeutic theme.';
        else if (workIdx === workCount) role = state.craftedSuggestion ? 'CONSOLIDATE + FUTURE-PACE: final reinforcement at peak intensity. Project the effect forward in time.' : 'CONSOLIDATE: bring the work to its peak and anchor it for the future.';
        else if (workIdx === workCount - 1) role = state.craftedSuggestion ? 'PEAK: most intense reinforcement of the crafted suggestion. Highest suggestibility.' : 'PEAK: highest intensity — the crux of the work.';
        else {
          const midRoles = ['DEVELOP: expand with a fresh metaphor you have not yet used.', 'INTENSIFY: deliver the suggestion at higher conviction and specificity.', 'REINFORCE: a different angle on the same core effect.'];
          role = midRoles[(workIdx - 2) % midRoles.length];
        }
        phaseInstructions[p] = `Write WORK phase ${workIdx} of ${workCount} (~${workWordsEach} words). ROLE: ${role}${state.craftedSuggestion ? '' : ' Therapeutic deepening tied to the intention.'} Do not repeat imagery or phrasing from earlier work blocks. Use \x5BPAUSE n\x5D. Output ONLY script text.`;
      }
    });

    return phaseInstructions;
  }

  /**
   * Reconcile _genState with the current phase list. Called after the user
   * edits the phase editor (add/remove blocks) so the status indicator row
   * and retry affordances stay in sync.
   *
   * - New phases (no existing phaseResults entry) start as 'pending'
   * - Removed phases have their state + result dropped
   * - Existing phases keep their state + result
   * - phaseInstructions are rebuilt fully (word budgets rebalance across
   *   new work/deepener counts)
   *
   * No-op if _genState is null (user hasn't generated yet) or if the phase
   * list is identical to what's already tracked.
   */
  function syncGenStateWithPhases() {
    if (!_genState) return;
    const newPhases = getPhaseList();
    const gs = _genState;
    // Cheap identity check — same order, same ids → nothing to do
    if (newPhases.length === gs.phases.length && newPhases.every((p, i) => p === gs.phases[i])) return;

    const newStateMask = newPhases.map(p => {
      const oldIdx = gs.phases.indexOf(p);
      if (oldIdx === -1) return 'pending';
      return gs.stateMask[oldIdx] || 'pending';
    });
    // Keep only phaseResults for phases that still exist
    const newPhaseResults = {};
    newPhases.forEach(p => { if (gs.phaseResults[p] != null) newPhaseResults[p] = gs.phaseResults[p]; });

    // Rebuild phaseInstructions — word budgets rebalance across new work/deepener counts.
    // Recompute targetWords since state.length might also have changed via a different path.
    const durations = PHASE_DURATIONS[state.length] || PHASE_DURATIONS.medium;
    const wpm = 50;
    const targetWords = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(durations).map(([k, v]) => [k, Math.round(v * wpm / 60)]));
    const userAffRaw = $('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim();
    const affirmLines = userAffRaw ? userAffRaw.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).map(l => resolveTokens(l.trim())) : [];

    gs.phases = newPhases;
    gs.stateMask = newStateMask;
    gs.phaseResults = newPhaseResults;
    gs.phaseInstructions = buildPhaseInstructions(newPhases, targetWords, gs.persona, gs.method, affirmLines);

    // Re-render the progress indicators; retry handler closure from the initial
    // render is re-bound here so clicks on newly-appeared phases work.
    if ($('genProgress') && $('genProgress').style.display !== 'none') {
      renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, _genStateRetryHandler);
    }
  }

  // Captured when generateFullScript sets up _genState. syncGenStateWithPhases
  // uses it to re-bind retry clicks on phases added after initial generation.
  let _genStateRetryHandler = null;

  /**
   * Step-6 "Regenerate" button (the one below the script textarea, before auto-tempo).
   *
   * Behavior — sequentially retries any chunks that failed to generate the first
   * time (stateMask is 'error' or 'warn'). The button itself is disabled while
   * running so a user can't accidentally double-trigger.
   *
   * Decision tree:
   *   • _genState is null → no prior generation; offer full regen via confirm
   *   • all phases done → no failures to retry; offer full regen via confirm
   *   • some phases failed → run retryPhase for each in order, awaiting each
   *
   * Why sequential not parallel: the retry path uses _genStateRetryHandler which
   * gates on _aiInProgress, so concurrent retries would just queue and notify.
   * Sequential matches the visual progress (one indicator turning green at a
   * time) and avoids hammering the AI endpoint with bursts.
   */
  async function regenerateFailedChunks() {
    const btn = $('regenScriptBtn');
    if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('Another generation is already in progress.'); return; }

    // No prior generation state — fall back to full regen flow with confirm.
    if (!_genState) {
      if (await confirmAsync('No previous generation in memory. Generate the full script?')) {
        return generateFullScript();
      }
      return;
    }

    // Find indices that need retry. Treat both 'error' (hard failure) and 'warn'
    // (soft issue, content present but flagged) as candidates so the user gets
    // the maximum benefit from the retry button.
    const failedIdx = [];
    _genState.stateMask.forEach((s, i) => {
      if (s === 'error' || s === 'warn') failedIdx.push(i);
    });

    // No failures — offer full regen as a fallback rather than silently no-op.
    if (failedIdx.length === 0) {
      const editedText = $('scriptText')?.value?.trim();
      const hasManualEdits = state.fullScript && editedText && editedText !== state.fullScript.trim();
      const msg = hasManualEdits
        ? 'No failed chunks to regenerate. Discard your manual edits and regenerate the full script?'
        : 'No failed chunks to regenerate. Regenerate the full script anyway?';
      if (await confirmAsync(msg)) return generateFullScript();
      return;
    }

    // Disable the button for the duration. Use setLoading so the visual matches
    // the existing generation flow. Capture the original label to restore after.
    const originalLabel = btn?.textContent || 'regenerate';
    setLoading('regenScriptBtn', true);
    if (btn) btn.disabled = true;

    let succeeded = 0;
    let failed = 0;
    const retry = _genStateRetryHandler; // snapshot — generateFullScript reassigns this

    try {
      for (const idx of failedIdx) {
        // Re-check current status — the user may have manually retried one
        // mid-loop via the indicator click. Skip if it's no longer failed.
        const cur = _genState.stateMask[idx];
        if (cur !== 'error' && cur !== 'warn') {
          succeeded++; // already fixed by user — count as a win
          continue;
        }
        if (typeof retry !== 'function') {
          notify.error('Retry handler missing — try the regenerate-everything path instead.');
          break;
        }
        // retryPhase manages _aiInProgress internally; await it directly.
        await retry(idx);
        // After awaiting, check the new state to tally success/failure.
        const after = _genState.stateMask[idx];
        if (after === 'done') succeeded++; else failed++;
      }
    } finally {
      setLoading('regenScriptBtn', false, originalLabel);
      if (btn) btn.disabled = false;
    }

    if (failed === 0) {
      notify.success(`Regenerated ${succeeded} failed chunk${succeeded === 1 ? '' : 's'}.`);
    } else if (succeeded === 0) {
      notify.warn(`Could not regenerate any of the ${failed} failed chunk${failed === 1 ? '' : 's'}. Click indicators to retry individually.`);
    } else {
      notify.warn(`Regenerated ${succeeded}, ${failed} still failing. Click red indicators to retry individually.`);
    }
  }

  async function generateFullScript() {
    if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('An AI call is already in progress.'); return; }
    const editedText = $('scriptText').value.trim();
    if (state.fullScript && editedText && editedText !== state.fullScript.trim()) {
      if (!await confirmAsync('Your manual edits to the script will be discarded. Regenerate anyway?')) return;
    }
    _aiInProgress = true;
    history.clear(); // fresh generation invalidates prior edit history
    const persona = getPersona();
    const method = getMethod();
    const durations = PHASE_DURATIONS[state.length];
    // Resolve \{\{...\}\} tokens in user-written text BEFORE feeding the AI, so
    // the model sees real values. Any token the AI later emits in its output
    // will be caught again at TTS-time by the resolver in speakScript.
    const rough = resolveTokens($('intentionInput').value.trim());
    const wpm = 50;
    const targetWords = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(durations).map(([k,v]) => [k, Math.round(v * wpm / 60)]));
    const scriptBuildProgress = $('scriptBuildProgress');
    if (scriptBuildProgress) scriptBuildProgress.style.display = 'block';

    setLoading('generateScriptBtn', true);
    setLoading('regenScriptBtn', true);

    const phases = getPhaseList();
    const stateMask = phases.map(() => 'pending');
    const phaseTimes = [];
    const phaseResults = {};

    const craftedBlock = state.craftedSuggestion ? `\nCRAFTED SUGGESTION: "${state.craftedSuggestion.craftedSuggestion}"\nTRIGGER: ${state.craftedSuggestion.trigger}\nEFFECT: ${state.craftedSuggestion.coreResponse}` : '';
    const userAffRaw = $('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim();
    // Resolve tokens in user affirmations line-by-line so \{\{user\}\} etc. in
    // affirmations become concrete text before being injected into prompts.
    const affirmLines = userAffRaw ? userAffRaw.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).map(l => resolveTokens(l.trim())) : [];
    const affirmBlock = affirmLines.length ? `\nUSER AFFIRMATIONS:\n${affirmLines.map(l => `"${l}"`).join('\n')}` : '';
    const demoNote = method.category === 'demonstration' ? '\nDEMONSTRATION METHOD: direct suggestions, build effect, include TEST.' : '';

    const profileCtx = getProfileContext();
    // Smart Director gate — when off, don't pull adaptive or memory context at all.
    // getProfileContext() already gates itself. See _debug for bypass considerations.
    const sdOn = state.smartDirectorEnabled !== false;
    let adaptiveCtx = '';
    if (sdOn) {
      try { const ap = await getAdaptive(); adaptiveCtx = getAdaptivePromptBlock(ap); } catch {}
    } else { sdLog('adaptiveCtx skipped — Smart Director off'); }

    // Director Brief — built once per session generation (not per phase)
    // so it adds ≤ 1 extra round-trip of IDB reads, no AI call. Formatted block
    // is short (≤ 300 chars) and takes priority 3 alongside profile.
    let directorBriefCtx = '';
    if (sdOn) {
      try {
        const living = await buildLivingProfile();
        const brief = computeDirectorBrief(living, {
          persona: persona.name,
          method: method.name,
          intention: rough,
          length: state.length,
        });
        directorBriefCtx = formatDirectorBriefForPrompt(brief);
        // Stash the brief on state so the session record can capture which
        // brief was active (useful for retrospective debugging in future).
        state._lastDirectorBrief = brief;
      } catch (e) { console.warn('Director brief build failed:', e); }
    } else { sdLog('directorBriefCtx skipped — Smart Director off'); }

    // Memory context — prefer semantic retrieval over pure recency.
    // Fall back to rolling window + long-term profile when embeddings aren't
    // available or no relevant matches exist.
    let memoryCtx = '';
    if (sdOn) {
      try {
        const mem = await getMemory();
        // Top-K most semantically similar past digests (embedding-based)
        const relevant = await findRelevantDigests(rough || (persona.name + ' ' + method.name), 3);
        const relevantBlock = relevant.length
          ? '\nMOST RELEVANT PAST SESSIONS (by semantic similarity to this intention):\n' +
            relevant.map(r => `- [similarity ${((1 - r.distance) * 100).toFixed(0)}%] ${r.digest.digest}`).join('\n')
          : '';
        const baseBlock = (mem.rollingWindow || mem.longTermProfile)
          ? `\nPRACTITIONER MEMORY:${mem.longTermProfile ? '\nProfile: ' + mem.longTermProfile : ''}${mem.rollingWindow ? '\nRecent patterns: ' + mem.rollingWindow : ''}`
          : '';
        memoryCtx = baseBlock + relevantBlock;
        sdLog('memoryCtx built', { relevantCount: relevant.length, hasRolling: !!mem.rollingWindow, hasLongTerm: !!mem.longTermProfile });
      } catch (e) { console.warn('Memory context build failed:', e); }
    } else { sdLog('memoryCtx skipped — Smart Director off'); }

    // Metrics trends — multi-day rolling aggregates that give the director
    // time-series shape (completion-rate trends, mood deltas) over the recent
    // 7-day window. Short block, priority 3 alongside director brief.
    let metricsTrendCtx = '';
    if (sdOn) {
      try {
        const trend = await getMetricsTrendSummary({ windowDays: 7, compareDays: 14 });
        if (trend && trend.recentSessionCount >= 2) {
          const bits = [];
          bits.push(`${trend.recentSessionCount} session${trend.recentSessionCount===1?'':'s'} in last ${trend.windowDays} days`);
          if (trend.recentCompletionRate != null) {
            bits.push(`${Math.round(trend.recentCompletionRate * 100)}% completion`);
          }
          if (Number.isFinite(trend.completionDelta) && Math.abs(trend.completionDelta) >= 0.15) {
            bits.push(trend.completionDelta > 0
              ? `up ${Math.round(trend.completionDelta * 100)}pts vs prior 14d`
              : `down ${Math.round(-trend.completionDelta * 100)}pts vs prior 14d`);
          }
          if (Number.isFinite(trend.avgMoodDelta)) {
            bits.push(`avg mood Δ ${trend.avgMoodDelta >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${trend.avgMoodDelta.toFixed(1)}`);
          }
          if (Number.isFinite(trend.avgDepth)) {
            bits.push(`avg self-reported depth ${trend.avgDepth.toFixed(1)}/10`);
          }
          metricsTrendCtx = '\nRECENT TRENDS: ' + bits.join(' · ') + '. Adjust pacing or intensity if completion or mood is trending down.';
          sdLog('metricsTrendCtx built', trend);
        }
      } catch (e) { console.warn('Metrics trend build failed:', e); }
    } else { sdLog('metricsTrendCtx skipped — Smart Director off'); }

    // Build sharedContext under a token budget — priority order
    // determines what gets dropped first if the user has a huge profile +
    // long memory + many affirmations.
    const headerBlock = `You are ${persona.name}. ${getPersonaRole(persona)}\nMETHOD: ${method.name}. ${method.detail}\nPACING: ${PACING_RULES[method.pacing]}\nTHEME: "${rough || 'general trance experience'}"`;
    // Persona reminder — short anchor (Perchance §2.1 REMINDER pattern). Helps
    // keep the AI in voice across multi-phase generation, where drift accumulates.
    // High priority (4) since it's specific behavioral guidance, but lower than
    // the role itself so it can drop if context is extremely tight.
    const reminderBlock = persona.reminderMessage
      ? `\nREMINDER for writing as ${persona.name}: "${persona.reminderMessage}"`
      : '';
    const freshBlock = buildFreshnessBlock();
    const sharedContext = trimToTokenBudget([
      { name: 'header',     text: headerBlock,       priority: 5 }, // persona + method + theme — never drop
      { name: 'reminder',   text: reminderBlock,     priority: 4 }, // persona behavioral anchor
      { name: 'crafted',    text: craftedBlock,      priority: 4 },
      { name: 'affirm',     text: affirmBlock,       priority: 4 },
      { name: 'demoNote',   text: demoNote,          priority: 4 },
      { name: 'director',   text: directorBriefCtx,  priority: 3 }, // short, actionable, high-value
      { name: 'profile',    text: profileCtx,        priority: 3 },
      { name: 'metrics',    text: metricsTrendCtx,   priority: 3 }, // recent-day trend signals
      { name: 'freshSeeds', text: freshBlock,        priority: 2 }, // optional anchors — drops before adaptive
      { name: 'adaptive',   text: adaptiveCtx,       priority: 2 },
      { name: 'memory',     text: memoryCtx,         priority: 1 }, // first to drop
    ], 1200); // leave generous headroom for per-phase task block + output

    // Count nested Deepener/Lightener pairs so we can produce depth-aware prompts.
    // getSessionPhaseBlueprint yields 'deepener' (unnumbered) when there's one, otherwise
    // 'deepener-1', 'deepener-2', etc. Post-blueprint edits (user add/remove) can also
    // produce arbitrary configurations; we look at the actual phase list.
    const phaseInstructions = buildPhaseInstructions(phases, targetWords, persona, method, affirmLines);

    // Save gen state for retry access
    _genState = { phases, stateMask, phaseResults, phaseTimes, sharedContext, phaseInstructions, persona, method, genStartTime: Date.now(), priorSummary: '' };

    const retryPhase = async (idx) => {
      // Guard: need gen state to exist and no concurrent AI call in flight
      if (!_genState) return;
      if (_aiInProgress) { notify.info('Please wait — another phase is still being generated.'); return; }
      const gs = _genState;
      const phaseId = gs.phases[idx];
      // Capture the current (original) phase text BEFORE regenerating so we can
      // offer a diff comparison after. Empty original = first-time
      // generation, no diff needed.
      const originalText = gs.phaseResults[phaseId] || '';
      _aiInProgress = true;
      gs.stateMask[idx] = 'streaming';
      renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, retryPhase);
      try {
        // Pass the original text as priorDraft so generateSinglePhase can
        // instruct the AI to avoid the previous opening + rhythm. This is the
        // difference between two-near-identical re-rolls and meaningful variety.
        const newText = await generateSinglePhase(gs, idx, { priorDraft: originalText });
        // Only show diff if there was prior content to compare against
        let chosen = newText;
        if (originalText && originalText.trim() && originalText.trim() !== newText.trim()) {
          const pick = await showPhaseDiffModal(originalText, newText, getPhaseLabel(phaseId));
          chosen = pick === 'old' ? originalText : newText;
        }
        gs.phaseResults[phaseId] = chosen;
        gs.stateMask[idx] = 'done';
        renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, retryPhase);
        assembleAndShowScript(gs);
        if (chosen === originalText) {
          notify.info(`Kept original "${getPhaseLabel(phaseId)}".`);
        } else {
          notify.success(`Phase "${getPhaseLabel(phaseId)}" regenerated successfully.`);
        }
      } catch (e) {
        gs.stateMask[idx] = 'error';
        renderGenProgress(gs.phases, gs.stateMask, null, retryPhase);
        notify.error(`Retry failed: ${e.message}. Click the red indicator to try again.`);
      } finally {
        _aiInProgress = false;
      }
    };

    // Show initial progress
    _genStateRetryHandler = retryPhase; // captured so syncGenStateWithPhases can re-bind clicks
    renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, `Estimated: ~${phases.length * 60}s remaining`, retryPhase);
    const genStartTime = Date.now();
    const stopTimer = makeElapsedTimer(s => {
      const avgTime = phaseTimes.length > 0 ? phaseTimes.reduce((a,b) => a+b, 0) / phaseTimes.length : 60;
      const remSec = Math.max(0, Math.round(avgTime * (phases.length - phaseTimes.length)));
      $('genEta').textContent = `${s}s elapsed · ~${remSec}s remaining`;
    });

    try {
      let priorSummary = '';

      for (let i = 0; i < phases.length; i++) {
        const phase = phases[i];
        const phaseStart = Date.now();
        stateMask[i] = 'streaming';
        renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, null, retryPhase);

        try {
          const result = await generateSinglePhase(_genState, i);
          phaseResults[phase] = result;
          priorSummary += `\n${phase.toUpperCase()}: ${result.length > 200 ? result.substring(0, 150).replace(/\x5BPAUSE \d+\]/g, '') + '...' : result.replace(/\x5BPAUSE \d+\]/g, '')}`;
          _genState.priorSummary = priorSummary;
          stateMask[i] = 'done';
          phaseTimes.push((Date.now() - phaseStart) / 1000);
        } catch (e) {
          console.error(`Phase "${phase}" failed:`, e);
          if (e.message.includes('AI') || e.message.includes('error') || e.message.includes('failed')) {
            stateMask[i] = 'error';
            notify.error(`"${phase}" failed: ${e.message}. Click the red indicator to retry.`);
          } else {
            stateMask[i] = 'warn';
            notify.warn(`"${phase}" had an issue: ${e.message}. Click the yellow indicator to retry.`);
          }
          // Continue to next phase — partial script is better than nothing
          phaseTimes.push(60); // estimate for ETA
        }
        renderGenProgress(phases, stateMask, null, retryPhase);
      }

      assembleAndShowScript(_genState);
      const totalTime = Math.round((Date.now() - genStartTime) / 1000);
      const failures = stateMask.filter(s => s === 'error' || s === 'warn').length;
      if (failures > 0) {
        notify.warn(`Script generated in ${totalTime}s with ${failures} phase(s) needing retry. Click indicators to fix.`);
      } else {
        notify.success(`Script generated in ${totalTime}s — ${phases.length} phases complete.`);
      }

    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
      notify.error('Script generation failed: ' + e.message);
    } finally {
      _aiInProgress = false;
      stopTimer();
      setLoading('generateScriptBtn', false, 'generate full script');
      setLoading('regenScriptBtn', false);
      if (scriptBuildProgress) scriptBuildProgress.style.display = 'none';
      // Hide streaming preview once generation completes
      setStreamingPreview('', '', { hide: true });
    }
  }

  /** Generate a single phase via aiTextPlugin */
  async function generateSinglePhase(gs, idx, opts = {}) {
    const phase = gs.phases[idx];
    const phaseLabel = getPhaseLabel(phase);
    // Custom blocks are user-authored and pass through verbatim. If the user
    // wants AI output for a custom block, they use the Reimagine button in
    // the phase editor (reimagineCustomPhase), which is a separate flow.
    if (phaseBase(phase) === 'custom') {
      const existing = (gs.phaseResults && gs.phaseResults[phase]) || scaffoldForPhase(phase);
      setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, existing, { done: true });
      return existing;
    }
    const summaryBlock = gs.priorSummary ? `\n\nSO FAR (summary — continue seamlessly, DO NOT repeat):\n${gs.priorSummary}` : '';
    const taskBlock = `\n\n═══ YOUR TASK ═══\n${gs.phaseInstructions[phase]}\n\nREMINDER: You are ${gs.persona.name}. Voice, vocabulary, cadence — match the role above completely. ${gs.method.pacing ? `Pacing must follow the ${gs.method.pacing} rule established earlier.` : ''} No ===PHASE=== markers. Start immediately:`;

    // Diversity block — only present on a re-roll. Tells the AI to avoid the
    // rhythm and openings of the previous draft so re-rolls don't cluster
    // around the same opening words / cadence the user already rejected.
    // Without this, repeated retries tend to converge.
    const diversityBlock = (opts.priorDraft && opts.priorDraft.trim())
      ? `\n\n═══ DIVERSITY (this is a RE-ROLL) ═══\nThe previous attempt began: "${opts.priorDraft.trim().slice(0, 120).replace(/\s+/g, ' ')}…"\nWrite something MEANINGFULLY DIFFERENT this time:\n  • Do NOT open with the same word or phrase.\n  • Do NOT repeat the same sentence rhythm.\n  • Choose different sensory details and metaphors.\n  • Same persona voice, same task — different execution.`
      : '';

    // Token budget — drop the prior-summary block first if we're over budget.
    // The sharedContext + task block are priority 5 (never trimmed).
    // The diversity block is priority 5 too — it's the whole point of a re-roll.
    const finalInstruction = trimToTokenBudget([
      { name: 'sharedContext', text: gs.sharedContext, priority: 5 },
      { name: 'priorSummary',  text: summaryBlock,     priority: 1 },
      { name: 'taskBlock',     text: taskBlock,        priority: 5 },
      { name: 'diversity',     text: diversityBlock,   priority: 5 },
    ], 900);

    // Streaming — render text as it arrives so users see progress
    // within ~1s instead of waiting ~30-60s for the full phase.
    let accumulated = '';
    const onChunk = (data) => {
      if (data.isFromStartWith) return;
      const chunk = data.textChunk || '';
      if (!chunk) return;
      accumulated += chunk;
      setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, accumulated);
    };

    let data;
    try {
      // Perchance ai-text-plugin returns a thenable that resolves when done.
      // Providing onChunk enables streaming — it's ignored if unsupported.
      const streamObj = root.aiTextPlugin({
        instruction: finalInstruction,
        // Stop sequences:
        //   '\n\n\n\n'  — original guard against runaway
        //   '\n\n[['    — chat-format bleed safety net (perchance-api skill §14)
        //   '\n[['      — same, with a single newline (some models emit this)
        stopSequences: ['\n\n\n\n', '\n\n[[', '\n[['],
        hideStartWith: true,
        onChunk,
      });
      data = await streamObj;
    } catch (e) {
      setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, accumulated, { done: true });
      throw new Error('AI call threw: ' + (e?.message || e));
    }

    // explicit error-before-text check
    if (!data || data.stopReason === 'error') {
      setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, accumulated, { done: true });
      throw new Error('AI returned an error');
    }

    let raw = (data.generatedText || accumulated || '').trim();
    let text = stripLeadingPhaseHeader(raw, phase);
    if ((!text || text.length < 15) && raw) {
      text = raw
        .replace(PHASE_MARKER_STRIP_RX, ' ')
        .replace(/^(?:[#>*-]+\s*)?(?:phase\s*[:\-]\s*)?[a-z][a-z0-9\s\-]{1,40}:?\s*/i, '')
        .trim();
    }
    setStreamingPreview(phaseLabel, text, { done: true });
    if (!text || text.length < 15) throw new Error('Phase returned too little text');
    return text;
  }

  /** Assemble all completed phases into a full script */
  function assembleAndShowScript(gs) {
    let fullScript = '';
    gs.phases.forEach(p => {
      if (!gs.phaseResults[p]) return;
      fullScript += `===${phaseIdToMarker(p)}===
${gs.phaseResults[p]}

`;
    });
    if (fullScript.trim().length > 50) {
      state.fullScript = fullScript.trim();
      state.generatedPhaseOrder = [...gs.phases];
      state.parsedScript = parseScript(state.fullScript);
      showScript();
      updateStepUI();
    }
  }

  function parseScript(text) {
    const phases = {};
    const ordered = [];
    const matches = [...text.matchAll(PHASE_MARKER_CAPTURE_RX)];
    if (!matches.length) return { ...phases, ordered: [] };
    for (let i = 0; i < matches.length; i++) {
      const marker = matches[i][1];
      const phaseId = markerToPhaseId(marker);
      const start = matches[i].index + matches[i][0].length;
      const end = i + 1 < matches.length ? matches[i + 1].index : text.length;
      const body = text.substring(start, end).trim();
      phases[phaseId] = body;
      ordered.push(phaseId);
      if (phaseId.startsWith('work')) phases.work = [phases.work, body].filter(Boolean).join('\n\n');
    }
    phases.ordered = ordered;
    return phases;
  }

  function getScriptMetrics(text) {
    const full = String(text || '');
    const spokenOnly = stripAllPhaseMarkers(full)
      .replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\x5D/gi, ' ');
    const words = spokenOnly.split(/\s+/).filter(w => w.length > 0).length;
    const pauses = (full.match(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\x5D/gi) || []).length;
    const pauseSecs = (full.match(/\x5BPAUSE\s+(\d+)\]/gi) || []).reduce((sum, m) => sum + parseInt(m.match(/\d+/)[0], 10), 0);
    const parsed = parseScript(full);
    const phaseCount = (parsed.ordered || []).length;
    const workBlocks = (parsed.ordered || []).filter(p => p.startsWith('work')).length;
    const affirmBlocks = (parsed.ordered || []).filter(p => p.startsWith('affirm')).length;
    const estimatedMin = Math.round(words / 50 + pauseSecs / 60);
    return { words, pauses, pauseSecs, phaseCount, workBlocks, affirmBlocks, estimatedMin, ordered: parsed.ordered || [] };
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // SESSION DIAGNOSTICS — pre-flight structural analysis
  // ====================================================================
  // Heuristic checks that surface tips, warnings, and structural issues
  // BEFORE the user starts a session. Complements validateSessionSafety()
  // (which gates startSession and blocks on critical gaps) — diagnostics
  // shows the user the issues earlier so they can fix them proactively.
  //
  // Each suggestion: { id, severity, title, detail, action? }
  //   severity: 'info' | 'warn' | 'error'
  //   action:   optional { label, fn } — button in the suggestion card
  //
  // Adapted from /mnt/user-data/uploads/Adaptive-Session-Studio — js/suggestions.js
  // ====================================================================

  function analyzeSessionScript() {
    const suggestions = [];
    const hasScript = !!state.fullScript;

    // No script yet — just a gentle nudge
    if (!hasScript) {
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'no_script',
        severity: 'info',
        title: 'No script generated yet',
        detail: 'Configure your session above, then click "generate full script" to produce the per-phase narration. You can also paste a custom script directly into the text area.',
      });
      return suggestions;
    }

    const metrics = getScriptMetrics(state.fullScript);
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    const isSleep = state.intentionType === 'sleep';

    // ── Structural safety (aligns with validateSessionSafety — surfaces the
    //    same concerns as the startSession gate, but earlier and fixable) ───
    const has = (base) => sections.some(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === base);
    const missingFinishers = [];
    if (!isSleep) {
      if (!has('lightener'))      missingFinishers.push('Lightener');
      if (!has('wake'))           missingFinishers.push('Wake');
      if (!has('reintroduction')) missingFinishers.push('Reintroduction');
    }
    if (missingFinishers.length) {
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'missing_finishers',
        severity: 'error',
        title: `Missing: ${missingFinishers.join(', ')}`,
        detail: 'Without these phases the session ends in trance. Add the missing phases from the buttons above. (Sleep-intention sessions skip this requirement.)',
        action: {
          label: 'Add missing phases',
          fn: () => { missingFinishers.forEach(m => addPhaseSection(m.toLowerCase())); },
        },
      });
    }

    const deepenerCount = sections.filter(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'deepener').length;
    const lightenerCount = sections.filter(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'lightener').length;
    if (!isSleep && deepenerCount !== lightenerCount) {
      const diff = deepenerCount - lightenerCount;
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'unbalanced_deepener',
        severity: 'error',
        title: 'Unbalanced Deepener / Lightener pairs',
        detail: diff > 0
          ? `${deepenerCount} Deepener${deepenerCount>1?'s':''} but only ${lightenerCount} Lightener${lightenerCount===1?'':'s'} — you will go deeper than you return. Add ${Math.abs(diff)} Lightener${Math.abs(diff)>1?'s':''} or remove extra Deepener${diff>1?'s':''}.`
          : `${lightenerCount} Lightener${lightenerCount>1?'s':''} without matching Deepeners (${deepenerCount}). Structurally inconsistent — remove ${Math.abs(diff)} Lightener${Math.abs(diff)>1?'s':''} or add matching Deepener${Math.abs(diff)>1?'s':''}.`,
      });
    }

    // ── Work section balance ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    if (metrics.workBlocks === 0) {
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'no_work_blocks',
        severity: 'info',
        title: 'Session has no Work blocks',
        detail: 'Work blocks are where the therapeutic content lives. Without any, the session is essentially just an induction + wake cycle with no content between.',
      });
    } else {
      // Sum spoken words per phase kind to assess proportions
      const wordsPerPhase = {};
      sections.forEach(s => {
        const base = phaseBase(s.phaseId);
        const wordCount = String(s.text || '').replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\x5D/gi, ' ').split(/\s+/).filter(w => w.length > 0).length;
        wordsPerPhase[base] = (wordsPerPhase[base] || 0) + wordCount;
      });
      const totalWords = Object.values(wordsPerPhase).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
      if (totalWords > 50) {
        const workPct = (wordsPerPhase.work || 0) / totalWords;
        if (workPct > 0.75) {
          suggestions.push({
            id: 'work_dominates',
            severity: 'warn',
            title: 'Work section is ' + Math.round(workPct * 100) + '% of session',
            detail: 'The work section dominates the session. Consider shorter Work blocks, more Settling/Induction time, or a longer Lightener to improve the arc. Sessions that are nearly all Work can feel front-loaded.',
          });
        }
        const settlingWords = wordsPerPhase.settling || 0;
        if (metrics.estimatedMin >= 10 && totalWords > 0 && settlingWords / totalWords < 0.05) {
          suggestions.push({
            id: 'settling_too_short',
            severity: 'info',
            title: 'Settling phase feels brief',
            detail: `Settling is under 5% of the total for a ${metrics.estimatedMin}-minute session. Longer settling (8–12%) gives the user time to arrive before the induction starts.`,
          });
        }
      }
    }

    // ── Affirmations cross-check ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    const hasAffirmToken = /\{\{affirmation\}\}/i.test(state.fullScript || '');
    const hasAffirmPhase = sections.some(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'affirm');
    const userAffirmRaw = $('userAffirmations')?.value?.trim();
    const userAffirmCount = userAffirmRaw ? userAffirmRaw.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).length : 0;

    if ((hasAffirmToken || hasAffirmPhase) && userAffirmCount === 0) {
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'affirmations_missing',
        severity: 'warn',
        title: 'Affirmations referenced but none defined',
        detail: hasAffirmToken
          ? 'The script uses {{affirmation}} tokens but no user affirmations are defined. Tokens will resolve to a generic fallback. Add personal affirmations in the Affirmations step for a more powerful session.'
          : 'The session includes Affirmation phases but no user affirmations are defined. The affirmation interludes will generate generic content. Add personal affirmations in the Affirmations step.',
      });
    }

    // ── Empty phase text ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const emptyPhases = sections.filter(s => !s.text || s.text.trim().length < 30);
    if (emptyPhases.length) {
      const labels = emptyPhases.map(s => getPhaseLabel(s.phaseId)).slice(0, 3).join(', ');
      const more = emptyPhases.length > 3 ? ` (+${emptyPhases.length - 3} more)` : '';
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'empty_phases',
        severity: 'warn',
        title: `${emptyPhases.length} phase${emptyPhases.length>1?'s have':' has'} little or no content`,
        detail: `${labels}${more} — ${emptyPhases.length>1?'each has':'it has'} fewer than 30 characters of script text. Regenerate ${emptyPhases.length>1?'these phases':'this phase'} or edit manually before starting.`,
      });
    }

    // ── Runtime extremes ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    if (metrics.estimatedMin >= 45) {
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'session_very_long',
        severity: 'info',
        title: `Estimated runtime is ${metrics.estimatedMin} minutes`,
        detail: 'Sessions over 45 minutes can be hard to stay engaged with, especially for less-experienced practitioners. Consider trimming Work blocks or reducing pause durations if this feels long.',
      });
    } else if (metrics.estimatedMin < 5 && metrics.estimatedMin > 0) {
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'session_very_short',
        severity: 'info',
        title: `Estimated runtime is only ${metrics.estimatedMin} minute${metrics.estimatedMin===1?'':'s'}`,
        detail: 'Very short sessions leave little room for actual trance. Consider a longer session length or adding more phases.',
      });
    }

    // ── Fractionation attempt (currently blocked at add-time, but detect
    //    anyway in case a script was pasted or imported with multiple Inductions) ─
    const inductionCount = sections.filter(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'induction').length;
    if (inductionCount > 1) {
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'multi_induction',
        severity: 'warn',
        title: 'Multiple Induction phases detected',
        detail: `The session has ${inductionCount} Induction phases. Fractionation (multi-induction cycles) is not fully supported yet — the session will play but structural tooling treats later inductions as unusual. Use nested Deepeners for progressive deepening within one cycle.`,
      });
    }

    // ── Positive: session looks complete ─────────────────────────────────────
    if (!suggestions.length) {
      suggestions.push({
        id: 'all_good',
        severity: 'info',
        title: 'Session looks good',
        detail: `~${metrics.estimatedMin} min · ${metrics.phaseCount} phases · ${metrics.workBlocks} work block${metrics.workBlocks===1?'':'s'}. No structural issues detected — ready to start.`,
      });
    }

    return suggestions;
  }

  function renderSessionDiagnostics() {
    const panel = $('sessionDiagnosticsPanel');
    const list = $('sessionDiagnosticsList');
    if (!panel || !list) return;
    // Hide if no script preview is visible — diagnostics are only useful in Step 4
    if (!$('scriptPreview')?.classList.contains('visible')) {
      panel.style.display = 'none';
      return;
    }
    const suggestions = analyzeSessionScript();
    if (!suggestions.length) { panel.style.display = 'none'; return; }
    panel.style.display = 'block';

    const ICONS = { info: 'ℹ', warn: '⚠', error: '✕' };
    const COLORS = {
      info:  { icon: 'var(--text-dim)',    bg: 'rgba(120,180,240,0.06)', border: 'rgba(120,180,240,0.2)' },
      warn:  { icon: 'var(--neon-amber)',  bg: 'rgba(184,154,74,0.08)',   border: 'rgba(184,154,74,0.25)'  },
      error: { icon: '#ff6b6b',            bg: 'rgba(255,107,107,0.08)', border: 'rgba(255,107,107,0.3)' },
    };
    const _esc = (s) => String(s).replace(/[<>&"']/g, c => ({ '<':'&lt;', '>':'&gt;', '&':'&amp;', '"':'&quot;', "'":'&#39;' }[c]));

    list.innerHTML = suggestions.map(s => {
      const c = COLORS[s.severity] || COLORS.info;
      const actionHtml = s.action
        ? `<button class="diag-action" data-diag-id="${_esc(s.id)}" style="margin-top:6px;padding:4px 10px;font-size:0.7rem;border:0.5px solid ${c.border};border-radius:4px;background:transparent;color:${c.icon};cursor:pointer;">${_esc(s.action.label)}</button>`
        : '';
      return `<div class="diag-card" style="border:0.5px solid ${c.border};background:${c.bg};border-radius:5px;padding:8px 10px;margin-bottom:6px;">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:8px;">
          <span style="color:${c.icon};font-size:0.85rem;flex-shrink:0;margin-top:1px;font-weight:600;">${ICONS[s.severity]}</span>
          <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
            <div style="font-size:0.78rem;font-weight:500;color:var(--text);margin-bottom:3px;">${_esc(s.title)}</div>
            <div style="font-size:0.72rem;color:var(--text-dim);line-height:1.55;">${_esc(s.detail)}</div>
            ${actionHtml}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');

    // Bind action buttons. Need to close over the captured suggestion since the
    // `action.fn` may reference state or DOM that will change after re-render.
    list.querySelectorAll('.diag-action').forEach(btn => {
      const id = btn.dataset.diagId;
      const s = suggestions.find(x => x.id === id);
      if (s?.action?.fn) {
        btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
          s.action.fn();
          renderSessionDiagnostics(); // refresh after action applied
        });
      }
    });
  }

  function normalizePhaseSections(sections) {
    const cleaned = (sections || []).filter(s => s && s.text && s.text.trim()).map(s => ({ ...s, text: s.text.trim() }));
    let workIdx = 0;
    let affirmIdx = 0;
    return cleaned.map(section => {
      const base = String(section.phaseId || 'work').replace(/-\d+$/, '');
      if (base === 'work') {
        workIdx += 1;
        section.phaseId = `work-${workIdx}`;
      } else if (base === 'affirm') {
        affirmIdx += 1;
        section.phaseId = `affirm-${affirmIdx}`;
      } else {
        section.phaseId = base;
      }
      return section;
    });
  }

  function getScriptSectionsFromState() {
    const ordered = state.parsedScript?.ordered?.length ? state.parsedScript.ordered : getPlaybackPhaseOrder();
    return ordered.map(phaseId => ({ phaseId, text: state.parsedScript?.[phaseId] || '' })).filter(s => s.text && s.text.trim());
  }

  function getSpokenScriptPreviewText() {
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    return sections.map(s => stripLeadingPhaseHeader(s.text, s.phaseId).trim()).filter(Boolean).join('\n\n');
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // UNDO / REDO — phase-editor snapshot stack
  // ====================================================================
  // Snapshot-based undo for the phase editor. Each mutating operation
  // (add, remove, move, reset, textarea edit) pushes the current state
  // BEFORE mutating. Undo pops the past stack (pushing the current state
  // to future). Redo reverses.
  //
  // Snapshot contains all four derived fields (scriptSections is the
  // source of truth, but parsedScript + fullScript + generatedPhaseOrder
  // can diverge from it during textarea edits, so all four are saved).
  //
  // Adapted from /mnt/user-data/uploads/Adaptive-Session-Studio — js/history.js
  // ====================================================================
  const HISTORY_MAX = 60;
  const _historyPast   = [];
  const _historyFuture = [];
  let _historyOnChange = null;
  let _historyPushDebounce = null;
  let _historyPushDebouncePending = null;

  function _historySnapshot() {
    return JSON.stringify({
      scriptSections:      state.scriptSections || [],
      generatedPhaseOrder: state.generatedPhaseOrder || [],
      fullScript:          state.fullScript || null,
      parsedScript:        state.parsedScript || null,
    });
  }

  function _historyApply(json) {
    try {
      const snap = JSON.parse(json);
      state.scriptSections      = snap.scriptSections      || [];
      state.generatedPhaseOrder = snap.generatedPhaseOrder || [];
      state.fullScript          = snap.fullScript;
      state.parsedScript        = snap.parsedScript;
      // Re-render the visible UI from the restored state
      if (state.fullScript != null) {
        const el = $('scriptText'); if (el) el.value = state.fullScript;
        showScript();
      } else {
        const el = $('scriptText'); if (el) el.value = '';
        $('scriptPreview')?.classList.remove('visible');
        renderPhaseEditor();
      }
      updateStepUI();
      syncGenStateWithPhases();
      _historyNotify();
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[history] apply snapshot failed:', e);
    }
  }

  function _historyNotify() {
    const ub = $('undoBtn'); if (ub) ub.disabled = !history.canUndo();
    const rb = $('redoBtn'); if (rb) rb.disabled = !history.canRedo();
    _historyOnChange?.();
  }

  const history = {
    onchange(fn) { _historyOnChange = fn; },
    push() {
      _historyPast.push(_historySnapshot());
      if (_historyPast.length > HISTORY_MAX) _historyPast.shift();
      _historyFuture.length = 0;
      _historyNotify();
    },
    /**
     * Transactional checkpoint for guarded mutations. Capture pre-state at
     * the top of a mutator; return a `commit()` closure. Call commit() after
     * mutation. If the state didn't change between begin and commit (guard
     * returned early, idempotent operation), commit is a no-op. Usage:
     *
     *   function addFoo() {
     *     const commit = history.beginChange();
     *     if (bailOut) return;
     *     ... mutate ...
     *     commit();
     *   }
     */
    beginChange() {
      const before = _historySnapshot();
      let committed = false;
      return () => {
        if (committed) return;
        committed = true;
        if (_historySnapshot() === before) return; // no change — skip
        _historyPast.push(before);
        if (_historyPast.length > HISTORY_MAX) _historyPast.shift();
        _historyFuture.length = 0;
        _historyNotify();
      };
    },
    /** Debounced push — for textarea input where per-keystroke snapshots
     *  would flood the stack. The snapshot is captured on the FIRST call
     *  in a typing burst (so it reflects pre-edit state), not on each call.
     *  Subsequent calls within the debounce window just reset the timer.
     *  Commits after `delayMs` of idle, only if state has actually changed. */
    pushDebounced(delayMs = 500) {
      if (_historyPushDebouncePending == null) {
        // First call in the burst — capture NOW, before the mutation hits
        _historyPushDebouncePending = _historySnapshot();
      }
      if (_historyPushDebounce) clearTimeout(_historyPushDebounce);
      _historyPushDebounce = setTimeout(() => {
        _historyPushDebounce = null;
        const pending = _historyPushDebouncePending;
        _historyPushDebouncePending = null;
        if (pending == null) return;
        // Only commit if the state has actually changed since snapshot.
        // Rapid typing that returns to the same text (e.g. select-all → retype
        // same text) should not produce a stack entry.
        if (_historyPast[_historyPast.length - 1] === pending) return;
        if (_historySnapshot() === pending) return; // no net change
        _historyPast.push(pending);
        if (_historyPast.length > HISTORY_MAX) _historyPast.shift();
        _historyFuture.length = 0;
        _historyNotify();
      }, delayMs);
    },
    canUndo() { return _historyPast.length > 0; },
    canRedo() { return _historyFuture.length > 0; },
    undo() {
      if (!_historyPast.length) return;
      _historyFuture.push(_historySnapshot());
      if (_historyFuture.length > HISTORY_MAX) _historyFuture.shift();
      _historyApply(_historyPast.pop());
    },
    redo() {
      if (!_historyFuture.length) return;
      _historyPast.push(_historySnapshot());
      _historyApply(_historyFuture.pop());
    },
    clear() {
      _historyPast.length = 0;
      _historyFuture.length = 0;
      if (_historyPushDebounce) { clearTimeout(_historyPushDebounce); _historyPushDebounce = null; }
      _historyPushDebouncePending = null;
      _historyNotify();
    },
    depth() { return { past: _historyPast.length, future: _historyFuture.length }; },
  };

  function setScriptFromSections(sections, opts = {}) {
    const cleaned = normalizePhaseSections(sections);
    state.scriptSections = cleaned.map(s => ({ ...s }));
    state.generatedPhaseOrder = cleaned.map(s => s.phaseId);
    state.fullScript = cleaned.map(s => `===${phaseIdToMarker(s.phaseId)}===
${s.text.trim()}`).join('\n\n').trim();
    state.parsedScript = parseScript(state.fullScript);
    if (!opts.skipRender) showScript();
    updateStepUI();
    // Keep the progress indicator row (#genPhases) in sync with the new phase
    // list so users can generate / retry for newly added blocks. No-op if
    // the user hasn't generated yet.
    syncGenStateWithPhases();
  }

  /**
   * For a given sections list, assign a `pairGroup` and `depth` to each phase.
   * - pairGroup: 'trance' | 'depth' | null — drives editor color coding.
   * - depth: integer (1-based) for deepener/lightener nesting — how deep this
   *   pair is nested. Deepeners number outward-to-inward; their matched
   *   Lighteners mirror that (LIFO — innermost unwinds first).
   * Returns an array of { pairGroup, depth } parallel to sections.
   */
  function computePairMetadata(sections) {
    // Walk forward: every Deepener pushes a depth level.
    // Walk lighteners in reverse order to pair them up with the deepest unclosed deepener.
    const deepenerStack = []; // each entry is {idx, depth}
    const meta = sections.map(() => ({ pairGroup: null, depth: null }));
    let curDepth = 0;
    sections.forEach((s, i) => {
      const base = phaseBase(s.phaseId);
      if (base === 'deepener') {
        curDepth++;
        deepenerStack.push({ idx: i, depth: curDepth });
        meta[i] = { pairGroup: 'depth', depth: curDepth };
      } else if (base === 'lightener') {
        // Pair with the most-recently-added unclosed deepener (LIFO).
        const pair = deepenerStack.pop();
        const depth = pair ? pair.depth : 1;
        meta[i] = { pairGroup: 'depth', depth };
        if (curDepth > 0) curDepth--;
      } else if (base === 'induction' || base === 'wake' || base === 'reintroduction') {
        meta[i] = { pairGroup: 'trance', depth: null };
      }
    });
    return meta;
  }

  function renderPhaseEditor() {
    const panel = $('phaseEditorPanel');
    const list = $('phaseEditorList');
    if (!panel || !list) return;
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    state.scriptSections = sections;
    if (!sections.length) {
      panel.style.display = 'none';
      return;
    }
    panel.style.display = 'block';
    const meta = computePairMetadata(sections);
    list.innerHTML = sections.map((s, i) => {
      const m = meta[i];
      const base = phaseBase(s.phaseId);
      const isCustom = base === 'custom';
      const isSounding = base === 'sounding';
      const rowClass = 'toggle-row phase-editor-row'
        + (m.pairGroup ? ' pair-' + m.pairGroup : '')
        + (isCustom ? ' is-custom' : '')
        + (isSounding ? ' is-sounding' : '');
      const depthAttr = m.depth ? ` data-depth="${m.depth}"` : '';
      const tag = m.pairGroup === 'trance'
        ? '<span class="phase-pair-tag tag-trance" title="Induction ↔ Wake / Reintroduction">↕ trance</span>'
        : m.pairGroup === 'depth'
          ? `<span class="phase-pair-tag tag-depth" title="Deepener ↔ Lightener (level ${m.depth})">↕ depth ${m.depth}</span>`
          : isCustom
            ? '<span class="phase-pair-tag" style="background:rgba(0,212,230,0.1);color:var(--neon-cyan);" title="User-authored block — bypasses AI generation">✎ custom</span>'
            : isSounding
              ? '<span class="phase-pair-tag" style="background:rgba(201,168,85,0.1);color:var(--accent-warm);" title="Meta-awareness pause — depth check / witness moment">◉ sounding</span>'
              : '';
      const preview = escapeHtml((s.text || '').replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\x5D/gi, ' ').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim().slice(0, 100) || 'empty');
      // Custom rows get an extra Reimagine action; the column count adjusts to fit
      const reimagineBtn = isCustom
        ? `<button class="preview-btn phase-reimagine" data-idx="${i}" title="Rewrite this block in your guide's voice">✨ reimagine</button>`
        : '';
      const colCount = isCustom ? 4 : 3;
      return `
      <div class="${rowClass}" data-phase-idx="${i}"${depthAttr} style="align-items:flex-start;">
        <div style="flex:1; min-width:0;">
          <label>${escapeHtml(getPhaseLabel(s.phaseId))}${tag}<span class="hint">${preview}</span></label>
        </div>
        <div style="display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(${colCount}, minmax(72px, auto)); gap:6px; margin-left:8px;">
          <button class="preview-btn phase-up" data-idx="${i}" ${i === 0 ? 'disabled' : ''}>↑</button>
          <button class="preview-btn phase-down" data-idx="${i}" ${i === sections.length - 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}>↓</button>
          <button class="preview-btn phase-remove" data-idx="${i}">remove</button>
          ${reimagineBtn}
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
    list.querySelectorAll('.phase-up').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', () => movePhaseSection(parseInt(btn.dataset.idx, 10), -1)));
    list.querySelectorAll('.phase-down').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', () => movePhaseSection(parseInt(btn.dataset.idx, 10), 1)));
    list.querySelectorAll('.phase-remove').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', () => removePhaseSection(parseInt(btn.dataset.idx, 10))));
    list.querySelectorAll('.phase-reimagine').forEach(btn => btn.addEventListener('click', () => reimagineCustomPhase(parseInt(btn.dataset.idx, 10))));
    // Refresh the global Reimagine mode toggle visibility (only shown when ≥1 custom block exists)
    if (typeof _refreshReimagineModeUI === 'function') _refreshReimagineModeUI();
    // Pair-highlighting: hovering a paired phase highlights its partner(s).
    list.querySelectorAll('.phase-editor-row').forEach((row, i) => {
      const m = meta[i];
      if (!m.pairGroup) return;
      row.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
        list.querySelectorAll('.phase-editor-row').forEach((other, j) => {
          if (j === i) return;
          const om = meta[j];
          if (m.pairGroup === 'trance' && om.pairGroup === 'trance') other.classList.add('highlight-pair');
          else if (m.pairGroup === 'depth' && om.pairGroup === 'depth' && om.depth === m.depth) other.classList.add('highlight-pair');
        });
      });
      row.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
        list.querySelectorAll('.phase-editor-row').forEach(r => r.classList.remove('highlight-pair'));
      });
    });
    // Refresh pre-flight diagnostics — phase list changes can fix or introduce issues
    renderSessionDiagnostics();
  }

  function movePhaseSection(idx, delta) {
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    const j = idx + delta;
    if (j < 0 || j >= sections.length) return;
    const commit = history.beginChange();
    [sections[idx], sections[j]] = [sections[j], sections[idx]];
    setScriptFromSections(sections);
    commit();
  }

  /**
   * Remove a phase, with pair-aware cascade:
   *  - Removing an Induction prompts to also remove Wake + Reintroduction (and any trailing trance-cycle partners).
   *  - Removing a Deepener auto-removes its paired Lightener (LIFO — the one that would close this depth level).
   *  - Removing a Lightener auto-removes its paired Deepener (preserves structural integrity).
   * User confirmation is requested when multiple phases will be removed.
   */
  async function removePhaseSection(idx) {
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    if (idx < 0 || idx >= sections.length) return;
    const target = sections[idx];
    const base = phaseBase(target.phaseId);

    // Indexes of partners to remove alongside the primary target.
    const partnerIndexes = [];

    if (base === 'induction') {
      // Remove this induction PLUS any remaining wake + reintroduction (the Emergence pair).
      sections.forEach((s, i) => {
        if (i === idx) return;
        const b = phaseBase(s.phaseId);
        if (b === 'wake' || b === 'reintroduction') partnerIndexes.push(i);
      });
    } else if (base === 'deepener') {
      // Find the matching Lightener for THIS deepener using LIFO pairing.
      const meta = computePairMetadata(sections);
      const targetDepth = meta[idx]?.depth;
      if (targetDepth != null) {
        // Walk forward from idx: the first Lightener at this depth is the partner.
        for (let k = idx + 1; k < sections.length; k++) {
          if (meta[k].pairGroup === 'depth' && phaseBase(sections[k].phaseId) === 'lightener' && meta[k].depth === targetDepth) {
            partnerIndexes.push(k);
            break;
          }
        }
      }
    } else if (base === 'lightener') {
      // Remove the paired Deepener for this Lightener.
      const meta = computePairMetadata(sections);
      const targetDepth = meta[idx]?.depth;
      if (targetDepth != null) {
        // Walk BACK from idx: find the matching deepener at same depth.
        for (let k = idx - 1; k >= 0; k--) {
          if (meta[k].pairGroup === 'depth' && phaseBase(sections[k].phaseId) === 'deepener' && meta[k].depth === targetDepth) {
            partnerIndexes.push(k);
            break;
          }
        }
      }
    } else if (base === 'wake') {
      // Removing Wake alone is structurally incomplete — prompt to also remove Reintroduction.
      const reintroIdx = sections.findIndex(s => phaseBase(s.phaseId) === 'reintroduction');
      if (reintroIdx >= 0 && reintroIdx !== idx) {
        const also = await confirmAsync('Also remove Reintroduction? Reintroduction without Wake leaves the user mid-emergence.', { okText: 'remove both', cancelText: 'only wake' });
        if (also) partnerIndexes.push(reintroIdx);
      }
    }

    const toRemove = [idx, ...partnerIndexes];
    if (toRemove.length > 1) {
      const names = toRemove.map(i => getPhaseLabel(sections[i].phaseId)).join(', ');
      const ok = await confirmAsync(`Remove ${toRemove.length} paired phases: ${names}?\n\nPhases in a pair should be kept together for safe session structure.`, { okText: 'remove all', cancelText: 'cancel' });
      if (!ok) return;
    }

    const commit = history.beginChange();
    // Remove in descending index order so splicing doesn't shift later indexes.
    toRemove.sort((a, b) => b - a).forEach(i => sections.splice(i, 1));
    setScriptFromSections(sections);
    commit();
    if (partnerIndexes.length > 0) notify.info(`Removed ${toRemove.length} paired phases.`);
  }

  /**
   * Scaffold text for a new phase. Depth-aware for nested deepener/lightener.
   */
  function scaffoldForPhase(phaseId, depth = 1) {
    if (phaseId === 'settling') return 'Find a comfortable position. Let the day settle. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseId === 'induction') return 'Begin the induction here. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseId === 'deepener' || phaseBase(phaseId) === 'deepener') {
      if (depth <= 1) return 'Deepen the state. Each breath takes you further. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
      if (depth === 2) return 'Now deeper still — another level down. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
      if (depth === 3) return 'Deeper, and deeper yet. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
      return `Descend another level — level ${depth}. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D`;
    }
    if (phaseId === 'lightener' || phaseBase(phaseId) === 'lightener') {
      if (depth <= 1) return 'Begin easing intensity down. Notice the room. Notice the body. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
      return `Come back up one level — from depth ${depth} toward ${depth - 1}. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D`;
    }
    if (phaseBase(phaseId) === 'work') return 'Continue the work here. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseBase(phaseId) === 'affirm') return 'Return to the user\'s affirmations here. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseBase(phaseId) === 'sounding') {
      // Sounding (a.k.a. depth check / witness moment) — meta-awareness pause.
      // Generic fallback; the AI re-roll on this phase produces a personalized
      // version using buildPhaseInstructions['sounding'].
      return 'Take a sounding now. Notice — without changing anything — how you feel in this moment. The weight of the body. The quality of the breath. The shape of your awareness right now. \x5BPAUSE 5\x5D';
    }
    if (phaseBase(phaseId) === 'custom') {
      // Custom phase — user-authored. Empty scaffold so the user knows it's
      // theirs to fill. Reimagine button lets them bounce drafts through AI.
      return '(Your custom text here. Edit this directly, or use Reimagine to have your guide rewrite it.) \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    }
    if (phaseId === 'wake') return 'In a moment, coming all the way back now. Five, returning. Four, breathing deeper. Three, energy returning. Two, eyes beginning to open. One, fully awake and alert. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    if (phaseId === 'reintroduction') return 'Welcome back. When you feel ready, slowly get up. Stretch. Shake it off. Go about your day. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
    return 'New phase text. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D';
  }

  /**
   * Add a new phase to the session. Pair-aware:
   *  - Adding an Induction auto-adds Wake + Reintroduction if missing (unless sleep intention).
   *  - Adding a Deepener auto-adds a paired Lightener in the LIFO unwind slot.
   *  - Work and Affirm are naked additions (no pair).
   *  - Lightener, Wake, Reintroduction can be added naked (for repair of an incomplete session).
   */
  function addPhaseSection(phaseId) {
    const commit = history.beginChange();
    const sections = getScriptSectionsFromState();
    const base = phaseBase(phaseId);
    const added = [];

    /** Build a uniquely-IDed section for a given base kind. */
    const buildSection = (kind, opts = {}) => {
      const existingCount = countPhaseBase(sections.concat(added), kind);
      let id = kind;
      // Numbered IDs for anything that can legitimately appear multiple times
      if (['work', 'affirm', 'deepener', 'lightener', 'sounding', 'custom'].includes(kind)) {
        const nextN = existingCount + 1;
        id = nextN > 1 ? `${kind}-${nextN}` : kind;
        // Rename the first occurrence to `${kind}-1` for consistency once we have 2+.
        // Done after insertion below.
      }
      return { phaseId: id, text: scaffoldForPhase(id, opts.depth || existingCount + 1) };
    };

    /** Insert a section at the correct canonical position, then register it. */
    const insertSection = (section) => {
      const insertIdx = findPhaseInsertionIdx(sections, phaseBase(section.phaseId));
      sections.splice(insertIdx, 0, section);
      added.push(section);
    };

    // Pair logic — also queues partners in canonical positions.
    if (base === 'induction') {
      // Multi-induction sessions (fractionation) aren't fully modeled yet — guard.
      if (countPhaseBase(sections, 'induction') > 0) {
