      const secs = elapsed % 60;
      const timeEl = $('sessionTime');
      if (timeEl) timeEl.textContent = `${mins}:${String(secs).padStart(2,'0')} elapsed`;
    }, 1000);

    const phases = getPlaybackPhaseOrder().filter(phase => state.parsedScript?.[phase]);
    renderSessionPhaseDots(phases);
    const phaseLabels = Object.fromEntries(phases.map(phase => [phase, getPhaseLabel(phase).toLowerCase()]));

    const durations = PHASE_DURATIONS[state.length] || PHASE_DURATIONS.medium;
    const expectedSec = phases.reduce((sum, phase) => {
      const base = phase.replace(/-\d+$/, '');
      if (base === 'affirm') return sum + 45;
      return sum + (durations[base] || 60);
    }, 0);
    const safetyCheck = () => {
      if (state._finishing || !state._sessionStartTime) return;
      // If user is paused, reschedule — don't force-end a user-paused session
      if (state.paused) { state._safetyTimeout = setTimeout(safetyCheck, 60000); return; }
      notify.warn('Session exceeded maximum expected duration — auto-finishing.');
      state._finishing = true;
      state.abortFlag = true;
      speechSynthesis.cancel();
      finishSession(false);
    };
    state._safetyTimeout = setTimeout(safetyCheck, (expectedSec * 2 + 300) * 1000);

    for (let pi = 0; pi < phases.length; pi++) {
      const phase = phases[pi];
      if (state.abortFlag) break;
      const phaseText = state.parsedScript[phase];
      if (!phaseText || phaseText.trim().length < 10) continue;

      // Update phase state
      state._currentPhase = phase;
      $('phaseIndicator').textContent = phaseLabels[phase];

      // Update phase dots
      updatePhaseDots(pi);

      // Update progress bar
      const pct = Math.round((pi / Math.max(phases.length, 1)) * 100);
      $('sessionProgressFill').style.width = pct + '%';

      // Modulate drone frequency per phase
      if (state.droneEnabled && drone.running) drone.setPhaseFreq(phase);

      const cleanText = stripLeadingPhaseHeader(phaseText, phase).trim();
      try { await speakScript(cleanText); }
      catch(e) { console.error(`Phase "${phase}" speak error:`, e); }
    }

    // Complete progress bar
    $('sessionProgressFill').style.width = '100%';
    updatePhaseDots(phases.length, phases.length);

    // Always finish the session — if abortFlag was set by emergencyEnd,
    // that path calls finishSession(true) itself, so only call if not aborting.
    // Guard against double-finish with a flag.
    if (!state.abortFlag && !state._finishing) {
      state._finishing = true;
      finishSession(false);
    }
  }

  // Interruptible sleep — checks abortFlag & paused state in 200ms chunks so
  // pause/end during a \x5BPAUSE n\x5D marker responds quickly instead of waiting
  // for the whole sleep to finish.
  async function interruptibleSleep(totalMs, bypassAbort = false) {
    const CHUNK = 200;
    let elapsed = 0;
    while (elapsed < totalMs) {
      if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) return;
      while (state.paused && !state.abortFlag) { await sleep(CHUNK); }
      const remaining = totalMs - elapsed;
      await sleep(Math.min(CHUNK, remaining));
      elapsed += CHUNK;
    }
  }

  async function speakScript(text, bypassAbort = false) {
    // Resolve \{\{user\}\}, \{\{nar\}\}, \{\{intention\}\}, \{\{affirmation\}\} tokens before
    // speech. Runs BEFORE sanitization so any expanded content (e.g. a
    // pasted affirmation with punctuation) is normalized by the passes below.
    let canonical = resolveTokens(text);
    // Sanitize: strip phase markers and malformed pause markers
    canonical = canonical.replace(PHASE_MARKER_STRIP_RX, '');
    canonical = canonical.replace(/\[\s*pause[^\]]*\]/gi, (m) => {
      const num = m.match(/\d+/);
      return num ? `\x5BPAUSE ${num[0]}\x5D` : '';
    });
    canonical = canonical.replace(/\[[^\]]+\]/g, m =>
      /^\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\x5D$/i.test(m) ? m : ''
    );
    // Normalize whitespace — strip newlines, collapse spaces
    canonical = canonical.replace(/[\r\n]+/g, ' ').replace(/  +/g, ' ').trim();

    const parts = canonical.split(/\x5BPAUSE\s+(\d+)\]/i);
    const display = $('textDisplay');
    const shouldDuck = drone.running && state.duckingEnabled;
    let isDucked = false;

    for (let i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {
      if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) break;
      while (state.paused && !state.abortFlag) await sleep(200);
      if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) break;

      if (i % 2 === 0) {
        // ── TEXT SEGMENT — split into sentences for per-sentence TTS ──
        const segment = parts[i].trim();
        if (!segment) continue;
        const sentences = segment.split(/(?<=[.!?])\s+/).filter(s => s.trim());

        // Duck FIRST — let it ramp down during display fade
        if (shouldDuck && !isDucked) { drone.duck(); isDucked = true; }

        for (const sentence of sentences) {
          if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) break;
          while (state.paused && !state.abortFlag) await sleep(200);
          if (!bypassAbort && state.abortFlag) break;

          if (display) {
            display.style.opacity = 0;
            await sleep(200);
            display.textContent = sentence;
            display.style.opacity = 0.5;
          }
          await speak(sentence);
          await sleep(120); // post-speak buffer — let last audio samples drain
        }

      } else {
        // ── PAUSE MARKER ──
        const seconds = parseInt(parts[i], 10) || 4;
        const tempo = state.tempoMultiplier || 1.0;
        const rateScale = 1 / Math.sqrt(Math.max(state.speechRate || 0.65, 0.4));
        const scaled = Math.max(1, Math.round(seconds * tempo * rateScale));

        // Only unduck for pauses ≥ 5s base (long dramatic pauses)
        // Short pauses: stay ducked to avoid pumping
        if (shouldDuck && isDucked && seconds >= 5) {
          drone.unduck(); isDucked = false;
          await interruptibleSleep(scaled * 1000, bypassAbort);
        } else {
          // Stay ducked through short pauses — cleaner audio
          await interruptibleSleep(scaled * 1000, bypassAbort);
        }
      }
    }
    // Always unduck at end of phase
    if (shouldDuck && isDucked) { drone.unduck(); isDucked = false; }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // LOCAL TTS — Hugging Face Transformers.js SpeechT5 (offline, free)
  // ====================================================================
  // Optional path that uses neural TTS running entirely in the browser.
  // Lazy-loaded only when the user opts in. After first download (~80 MB)
  // the model is cached by the browser's normal HTTP cache + IDB. No
  // network needed at runtime.
  //
  // Trade-offs vs the speechSynthesis path:
  //   + Higher quality on platforms with bad system voices (Linux, older Android).
  //   + Consistent voice across all devices.
  //   + No cloud round-trip.
  //   - First sentence has ~1-3s synth latency on fast hardware, more on slow.
  //   - No native onboundary word events — pulses are time-estimated.
  //   - Big first-load.
  //
  // Falls back to speechSynthesis on any failure (404, OOM, model error).
  const _localTTS = {
    enabled: false,         // user toggle
    ready: false,           // model loaded and synthesizer is callable
    loading: false,
    pipeline: null,         // the Transformers.js pipeline function
    synthesizer: null,
    speakerEmbeddings: null,
    speakerName: 'clb',
    audioCtx: null,
    currentSource: null,
    paused: false,
    pausedAt: 0,
    pausedBuffer: null,
    abortFlag: false,
    // CDN sources — pinned so updates don't break this app silently
    CDN_TRANSFORMERS: 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@xenova/transformers@2.17.2',
    SPEAKER_BASE: 'https://huggingface.co/datasets/Matthijs/cmu-arctic-xvectors/resolve/main/',
    SPEAKER_FILES: {
      clb: 'cmu_us_clb_arctic-wav-arctic_a0001.bin',
      slt: 'cmu_us_slt_arctic-wav-arctic_a0001.bin',
      bdl: 'cmu_us_bdl_arctic-wav-arctic_a0001.bin',
      rms: 'cmu_us_rms_arctic-wav-arctic_a0001.bin',
      ksp: 'cmu_us_ksp_arctic-wav-arctic_a0001.bin',
    },
    /** Lazy-load Transformers.js + SpeechT5 model + speaker embedding. Idempotent —
     *  multiple calls during loading wait on the same promise. */
    async init(speakerName = 'clb') {
      if (this.ready && this.speakerName === speakerName) return true;
      if (this.loading) return new Promise(r => {
        const tick = () => this.loading ? setTimeout(tick, 200) : r(this.ready);
        tick();
      });
      this.loading = true;
      this.speakerName = speakerName;
      const setStatus = (msg) => {
        const el = document.getElementById('localVoiceProgressText');
        if (el) el.textContent = msg;
      };
      const setBar = (pct) => {
        const fill = document.getElementById('localVoiceProgressFill');
        const wrap = document.getElementById('localVoiceProgress');
        if (wrap) wrap.style.display = '';
        if (fill) fill.style.width = Math.min(100, Math.max(0, pct)) + '%';
      };
      try {
        if (!this.pipeline) {
          setStatus('Loading the TTS engine…');
          setBar(5);
          // Dynamic import from CDN — works in modern browsers without a build step
          const mod = await import(/* @vite-ignore */ this.CDN_TRANSFORMERS);
          this.pipeline = mod.pipeline;
          // Disable local model loading attempts (we want CDN-hosted weights)
          if (mod.env) {
            mod.env.allowLocalModels = false;
            mod.env.useBrowserCache = true;
          }
          setBar(15);
        }
        if (!this.synthesizer) {
          setStatus('Downloading voice model (~80 MB, one-time)…');
          this.synthesizer = await this.pipeline('text-to-speech', 'Xenova/speecht5_tts', {
            quantized: false,
            progress_callback: (p) => {
              if (p.status === 'progress' && p.progress != null) {
                setBar(15 + p.progress * 0.7);
                setStatus(`Downloading voice model… ${Math.round(p.progress)}%`);
              }
            },
          });
          setBar(85);
        }
        // Load the speaker embedding (a small ~2KB tensor that conditions the voice)
        setStatus('Loading speaker voice…');
        const url = this.SPEAKER_BASE + this.SPEAKER_FILES[speakerName];
        const res = await fetch(url);
        if (!res.ok) throw new Error('speaker fetch ' + res.status);
        const buf = await res.arrayBuffer();
        this.speakerEmbeddings = new Float32Array(buf);
        setBar(100);
        setStatus('Ready. The first sentence may take 1-3 seconds; later ones are faster.');
        this.ready = true;
        return true;
      } catch (e) {
        setStatus('Failed to load: ' + (e?.message || e) + '. Will fall back to system voice.');
        console.warn('[localTTS] init failed:', e);
        this.ready = false;
        return false;
      } finally {
        this.loading = false;
      }
    },
    /** Synthesize and play one chunk. Resolves when playback ends. */
    async speak(text) {
      if (!this.ready || !text || !text.trim()) return;
      this.abortFlag = false;
      try {
        const out = await this.synthesizer(text, { speaker_embeddings: this.speakerEmbeddings });
        if (this.abortFlag) return;
        const audioData = out.audio;          // Float32Array
        const sr = out.sampling_rate || 16000;
        await this._playBuffer(audioData, sr);
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn('[localTTS] synth failed for chunk:', e);
        // Don't throw — caller treats as best-effort. Falling back here would
        // require restructuring; instead we log and silently drop the chunk.
      }
    },
    async _playBuffer(audioData, sampleRate) {
      if (!this.audioCtx) {
        this.audioCtx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
      }
      // Fire word-pulse pings on a timer for visualizer compatibility (no
      // real boundary events from neural TTS).
      const dur = audioData.length / sampleRate;
      const wordCount = Math.max(1, Math.round(dur / 0.4)); // ~150 wpm rough
      const pulseInterval = (dur / wordCount) * 1000;
      let pulsesFired = 0;
      const pulseTimer = setInterval(() => {
        if (this.abortFlag || pulsesFired >= wordCount) { clearInterval(pulseTimer); return; }
        if (state.audioReactive) state.audioReactive._voicePulseSpawnedAt = performance.now();
        pulsesFired++;
      }, pulseInterval);
      const buffer = this.audioCtx.createBuffer(1, audioData.length, sampleRate);
      buffer.copyToChannel(audioData, 0);
      const source = this.audioCtx.createBufferSource();
      source.buffer = buffer;
      // Apply user volume
      const gainNode = this.audioCtx.createGain();
      gainNode.gain.value = state.voiceVolume ?? 1.0;
      source.connect(gainNode).connect(this.audioCtx.destination);
      // Apply rate as playbackRate (rough analog of state.speechRate)
      source.playbackRate.value = Math.max(0.5, Math.min(2, state.speechRate || 1));
      this.currentSource = source;
      return new Promise((resolve) => {
        source.onended = () => {
          clearInterval(pulseTimer);
          if (this.currentSource === source) this.currentSource = null;
          resolve();
        };
        source.start(0);
      });
    },
    pause() {
      if (this.audioCtx && this.audioCtx.state === 'running') {
        try { this.audioCtx.suspend(); this.paused = true; } catch {}
      }
    },
    resume() {
      if (this.audioCtx && this.paused) {
        try { this.audioCtx.resume(); this.paused = false; } catch {}
      }
    },
    cancel() {
      this.abortFlag = true;
      if (this.currentSource) {
        try { this.currentSource.stop(0); } catch {}
        this.currentSource = null;
      }
    },
  };

  function speak(text) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
      // Local TTS path — opt-in, must be loaded
      if (state.useLocalTTS && _localTTS.ready) {
        _localTTS.speak(text).then(resolve).catch(() => resolve());
        return;
      }
      if (!('speechSynthesis' in window)) { setTimeout(resolve, text.length * 80); return; }
      // Only cancel if something is unexpectedly still speaking
      if (speechSynthesis.speaking || speechSynthesis.pending) speechSynthesis.cancel();
      setTimeout(() => _doSpeak(text, resolve), speechSynthesis.speaking ? 80 : 20);
    });
  }
  function _doSpeak(text, resolve) {
    const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
    u.voice = state.voice || getSelectedVoice();
    u.rate = state.speechRate; u.pitch = state.voicePitch || 0.85; u.volume = state.voiceVolume ?? 1.0;
    let settled = false;
    let lastBoundaryAt = Date.now();
    let boundaryEverFired = false;
    const done = () => { if (!settled) { settled = true; clearInterval(silenceWatch); resolve(); } };
    u.onend = done;
    u.onerror = done;

    // Word-level highlighting via onboundary (Chrome/Safari desktop)
    const display = $('textDisplay');
    u.onboundary = (e) => {
      lastBoundaryAt = Date.now();
      boundaryEverFired = true;
      // Fire voicePulse for audio-reactive visualizers (spec §2.2)
      if (e.name === 'word') {
        state.audioReactive._voicePulseSpawnedAt = performance.now();
      }
      if (e.name === 'word' && display) {
        const before = text.slice(0, e.charIndex);
        const word = text.slice(e.charIndex, e.charIndex + e.charLength);
        const after = text.slice(e.charIndex + e.charLength);
        display.innerHTML = `<span style="opacity:0.35">${escapeHtml(before)}</span><span style="opacity:1;color:var(--text)">${escapeHtml(word)}</span><span style="opacity:0.35">${escapeHtml(after)}</span>`;
      }
    };

    speechSynthesis.speak(u);

    // Pseudo-envelope fallback for browsers where onboundary never fires
    // (some Android Firefox builds, some TTS engines). Fires a synthetic
    // ~3.5Hz pulse after 500ms if no real boundary has arrived. Stops the
    // moment a real onboundary fires.
    const pseudoStart = setTimeout(() => {
      if (boundaryEverFired || settled) return;
      const baseTime = performance.now();
      const estDurMs = Math.max(500, text.length * 60); // ~60ms per char estimate
      const pulseInterval = 286; // ~3.5Hz
      const pulseTick = () => {
        if (boundaryEverFired || settled) return;
        const elapsed = performance.now() - baseTime;
        if (elapsed >= estDurMs) return;
        state.audioReactive._voicePulseSpawnedAt = performance.now();
        setTimeout(pulseTick, pulseInterval);
      };
      pulseTick();
    }, 500);
    const _origDone = done;
    const _doneWithCleanup = () => { clearTimeout(pseudoStart); _origDone(); };
    u.onend = _doneWithCleanup;
    u.onerror = _doneWithCleanup;

    // Double induction: fire a second utterance simultaneously
    if (state._doubleInduction && state._secondVoice) {
      const u2 = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
      u2.voice = state._secondVoice;
      u2.rate = state.speechRate * 0.92; u2.pitch = 0.75; u2.volume = 0.7;
      u2.onend = () => {}; u2.onerror = () => {};
      speechSynthesis.speak(u2);
    }

    // ACTIVE SILENCE WATCHDOG — every 2s, check if speech has made progress.
    // Only use boundary-based stuck detection if onboundary actually fires on
    // this platform. Many voices/browsers never fire it — in that case we rely
    // solely on the not-speaking check and hard ceiling.
    const speakStartedAt = Date.now();
    const silenceWatch = setInterval(() => {
      if (settled) { clearInterval(silenceWatch); return; }
      // CRITICAL: skip all checks while session is paused — speechSynthesis
      // reports speaking=false during pause, which triggers false done()
      if (state.paused) return;
      const silentFor = Date.now() - lastBoundaryAt;
      if (boundaryEverFired && speechSynthesis.speaking && silentFor > 8000) {
        // Chrome is stuck — boundaries were firing then stopped for 8s
        speechSynthesis.cancel();
        done();
      }
      // Grace period: don't check not-speaking until at least 1s after start
      if (Date.now() - speakStartedAt > 1000 && !speechSynthesis.speaking && !speechSynthesis.pending) {
        // Speech finished without firing onend (Firefox edge case)
        done();
      }
    }, 2000);

    // Hard ceiling — scaled by speech rate (slower rate = more time needed)
    // If paused, reschedule instead of killing — user might pause for minutes
    const rateMultiplier = 1 / Math.max(state.speechRate || 0.65, 0.4);
    const hardCeiling = Math.max(15000, text.length * 180 * rateMultiplier);
    const ceilingCheck = () => {
      if (settled) return;
      if (state.paused) { setTimeout(ceilingCheck, 5000); return; } // re-check after pause
      speechSynthesis.cancel(); done();
    };
    setTimeout(ceilingCheck, hardCeiling);
  }
  const sleep = ms => new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, ms));

  // ====================================================================
  // AUDIO RECORDER (ambience-only — TTS can't be captured via Web Audio)
  // ====================================================================
  let _recorder = null, _recordedChunks = [];

  function startRecording() {
    if (!drone.ctx || !drone.master) { notify.warn('Start a session with a soundscape first.'); return; }
    try {
      const dest = drone.ctx.createMediaStreamDestination();
      drone.master.connect(dest);
      _recorder = new MediaRecorder(dest.stream, { mimeType: 'audio/webm;codecs=opus' });
      _recordedChunks = [];
      _recorder.ondataavailable = e => { if (e.data.size > 0) _recordedChunks.push(e.data); };
      _recorder.onstop = () => {
        if (_recordedChunks.length === 0) return;
        const blob = new Blob(_recordedChunks, { type: 'audio/webm' });
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        a.download = `stillness-ambience-${Date.now()}.webm`;
        a.click();
        // Delay revoke so the browser actually initiates the download
        setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href), 5000);
        notify.success('Ambience recording downloaded.');
        _recordedChunks = [];
      };
      _recorder.start();
      notify.info('Recording ambience...');
      const btn = $('recordBtn');
      if (btn) { btn.textContent = '⏹ stop recording'; btn.classList.add('recording'); }
    } catch(e) { notify.error('Recording not supported in this browser.'); }
  }

  function stopRecording() {
    if (_recorder && _recorder.state === 'recording') {
      _recorder.stop(); _recorder = null;
      const btn = $('recordBtn');
      if (btn) { btn.textContent = '⏺ record ambience'; btn.classList.remove('recording'); }
    }
  }

  function toggleRecording() {
    if (_recorder && _recorder.state === 'recording') stopRecording();
    else startRecording();
  }

  async function finishSession(wasEmergency = false) {
    clearInterval(state._timeInterval);
    clearTimeout(state._safetyTimeout);
    state.paused = false; // don't leak paused state into the next session
    stopAudioReactiveLoop(); // stop the audio-reactive RAF loop
    resetStateEngine();      // clear engagement EMA, phase tracking, external signals
    clearRuntimeRuleState(); // clear per-rule runtime state (heldSec, lastFiredSec)
    clearTriggerWindowState(); // clear trigger window state (status, openedAt, lastFiredAt)
    state._rulesPreDuckVolume = null;
    // Webcam: stop the stream + clear signals. Per-session opt-in resets — checkbox
    // unticked so the next session starts off; user re-opts in if they want it.
    stopWebcam();
    const _wcCb = $('webcamOptInThisSession'); if (_wcCb) _wcCb.checked = false;
    // Playback dynamics — restore base speech rate so the next session starts at user's choice
    resetPlaybackDynamics();
    state._baseSpeechRate = null;
    closeLivePanel();
    stopRecording(); // Stop any active recording before tearing down audio
    await drone.stop(); stopVisuals(); speechSynthesis.cancel();
    // Clear lock-screen media session so it doesn't linger post-session
    if ('mediaSession' in navigator) {
      try {
        navigator.mediaSession.metadata = null;
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('play', null);
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('pause', null);
        navigator.mediaSession.setActionHandler('stop', null);
      } catch {}
    }
    document.body.classList.remove('in-session'); document.body.classList.remove('controls-hidden'); clearTimeout(_controlsTimer);
    switchScreen('post-screen');

    // Release wake lock
    try { state._wakeLock?.release(); } catch(e) {}

    // Save session to history — exclude paused time from duration
    let pausedMs = (state._pausedTotalMs || 0);
    if (state._pauseStartedAt) pausedMs += (Date.now() - state._pauseStartedAt); // finishing while paused
    const elapsed = state._sessionStartTime ? Math.max(0, Math.round((Date.now() - state._sessionStartTime - pausedMs) / 1000)) : 0;
    const currentProfile = getProfile();
    const scriptMetrics = getScriptMetrics(state.fullScript || '');
    const sessionRecord = {
      id: 'sess_' + Date.now(),
      date: Date.now(),
      guide: getPersona().name,
      method: getMethod().name,
      intention: state.intentionType,
      length: state.length,
      soundscape: state.soundscape,
      durationSec: elapsed,
      completed: !wasEmergency,
      preMood: state._preMood ?? null,
      preTension: state._preTension ?? null,
      preEnergy: state._preEnergy ?? null,
      // Full reproducibility data
      script: state.fullScript || '',
      personaId: state.selectedPersonaId,
      methodId: state.selectedMethodId,
      intentionText: $('intentionInput')?.value || '',
      voiceName: $('voiceSelect')?.value || '',
      userAffirmations: $('userAffirmations')?.value || '',
      affirmationMode: $('affirmationMode')?.value || 'woven',
      speechRate: state.speechRate,
      voicePitch: state.voicePitch,
      voiceVolume: state.voiceVolume,
      droneVolume: state.droneVolume,
      vizOverride: state.vizOverride,
      vizSettings: { ...state.vizSettings },
      duckingEnabled: state.duckingEnabled,
      phaseOrder: getPlaybackPhaseOrder(),
      profileName: currentProfile.name || 'Practitioner',
      profileSnapshot: currentProfile,
      workBlockCount: scriptMetrics.workBlocks,
      metrics: scriptMetrics,
      workflowVersion: 11,
      stepsTotal: 6,
    };
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    history.unshift(sessionRecord);
    if (history.length > 50) history.length = 50; // Keep last 50
    await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', history);
    await recordAnalytics(sessionRecord, wasEmergency);
    // Daily metrics aggregate — independent of per-session log, gives Smart Director
    // time-series shape (completion rate, mood trends) over the last 180 days.
    // postMood/depth still null at this point (filled in via post-checkin handler).
    recordSessionInMetricsHistory(sessionRecord, wasEmergency ? 'emergency' : 'completed').catch(e => console.warn('[metrics] record failed:', e));
    updateAdaptiveProfile(sessionRecord, wasEmergency); // non-blocking
    updateSessionMemory(state.fullScript, sessionRecord); // Memory system — non-blocking
    renderHeatmap(); // Refresh activity heatmap
    renderSparkline(); // Refresh rising-score sparkline
    renderSidebarStats(); // Refresh sidebar stats

    // Haptic marker — double-pulse on session end
    vibrateSessionMarker();

    // Remove warm overlay
    setSleepOverlay(false);

    // Clean up background engine
    bgEngine.clear();

    // Snapshot active program BEFORE advanceProgramDay mutates it — we need
    // {id, name, dayJustCompleted, totalDays, isFinalDay} to populate the post-session
    // program card. advanceProgramDay clears state._activeProgram and (on final day)
    // wipes the IDB record, so reading after-the-fact would lose this data.
    const _programSnapshot = (!wasEmergency && state._activeProgram?.prog && state._activeProgram?.ps)
      ? {
          name: state._activeProgram.prog.name,
          icon: state._activeProgram.prog.icon || '📅',
          dayJustCompleted: (state._activeProgram.ps.currentDay || 0) + 1, // currentDay is 0-indexed, so day 0 finishing = day 1 complete
          totalDays:        state._activeProgram.prog.days,
          isFinalDay:       (state._activeProgram.ps.currentDay || 0) + 1 >= state._activeProgram.prog.days,
        }
      : null;

    // Advance structured program (non-emergency only)
    if (!wasEmergency) advanceProgramDay();

    // Refresh method gating (may unlock new categories)
    applyMethodGating();

    // Build post-session summary
    const mins = Math.floor(elapsed / 60), secs = elapsed % 60;
    const persona = getPersona(), method = getMethod();
    // Pull personalization signals — first name (if user opted in), completed
    // session count (post-this-session), and the just-finished program day.
    const profile = getProfile();
    const firstName = (profile.useFirstName && profile.name) ? profile.name : '';
    const sessionCount = await getSessionCount(); // includes this one (recordSession ran above)
    const ordinalSuffix = (n) => {
      const v = n % 100;
      if (v >= 11 && v <= 13) return 'th';
      return ['th','st','nd','rd','th','th','th','th','th','th'][n % 10];
    };
    const summaryEl = $('postSummary');
    const sessionMarker = !wasEmergency && sessionCount > 0
      ? `<div class="post-row" style="opacity:0.85;"><span class="post-label">milestone</span><span class="post-value">${sessionCount}${ordinalSuffix(sessionCount)} completed session</span></div>`
      : '';
    summaryEl.innerHTML = `
      <div class="post-card-title">session summary</div>
      <div class="post-row"><span class="post-label">guide</span><span class="post-value">${escapeHtml(persona.name)}</span></div>
      <div class="post-row"><span class="post-label">method</span><span class="post-value">${escapeHtml(method.name)}</span></div>
      <div class="post-row"><span class="post-label">duration</span><span class="post-value">${mins}:${String(secs).padStart(2,'0')}</span></div>
      <div class="post-row"><span class="post-label">completion</span><span class="post-value">${wasEmergency ? 'ended early' : 'completed'}</span></div>
      ${sessionMarker}
    `;

    // Show trigger/suggestion reminder if relevant
    const triggerBox = $('postTriggerBox');
    if (state.craftedSuggestion && state.craftedSuggestion.trigger && state.craftedSuggestion.trigger !== 'ongoing state') {
      triggerBox.style.display = '';
      triggerBox.innerHTML = `
        <div class="post-trigger-title">your trigger</div>
        <div class="post-trigger-text">${escapeHtml(state.craftedSuggestion.trigger)}</div>
        <div class="post-trigger-sub">→ ${escapeHtml(state.craftedSuggestion.coreResponse || '')}</div>`;
    } else if (state.craftedSuggestion && state.craftedSuggestion.coreResponse) {
      triggerBox.style.display = '';
      triggerBox.innerHTML = `
        <div class="post-trigger-title">suggestion installed</div>
        <div class="post-trigger-text">${escapeHtml(state.craftedSuggestion.coreResponse)}</div>`;
    } else {
      triggerBox.style.display = 'none';
      triggerBox.innerHTML = '';
    }

    // For demonstration methods, remind user of the test
    if (method.category === 'demonstration' && !wasEmergency) {
      triggerBox.style.display = '';
      triggerBox.innerHTML += `<div style="margin-top:8px; padding-top:8px; border-top:1px solid var(--glass-border);">
        <div class="post-trigger-title" style="color:var(--accent-purple);">test now</div>
        <div class="post-trigger-text" style="font-size:0.82rem;">Try the ${escapeHtml(method.name)} effect now.</div>
      </div>`;
    }

    // Intention-aware reflection prompt — short, contextual nudge for what to
    // notice / do after the session. Hidden on emergency end (the user needs
    // grounding, not philosophical reflection).
    const reflectionBox = $('postReflectionBox');
    if (reflectionBox) {
      if (!wasEmergency) {
        const reflection = POST_SESSION_REFLECTIONS[state.intentionType] || POST_SESSION_REFLECTION_FALLBACK;
        reflectionBox.style.display = '';
        reflectionBox.innerHTML = `
          <div class="post-card-title">a moment to notice</div>
          <div class="post-trigger-text" style="font-size:0.86rem;line-height:1.55;color:var(--text-dim);">${escapeHtml(reflection)}</div>`;
      } else {
        reflectionBox.style.display = 'none';
        reflectionBox.innerHTML = '';
      }
    }

    // Program continuation hint — uses _programSnapshot captured BEFORE
    // advanceProgramDay mutated state. On the final day this is the only place
    // we can still surface the completion celebration; advanceProgramDay clears
    // the IDB record on day N=total.
    const programBox = $('postProgramBox');
    if (programBox) {
      if (_programSnapshot) {
        const sn = _programSnapshot;
        const nextDayHint = sn.isFinalDay
          ? `🎉 You completed all ${sn.totalDays} days of <strong>${escapeHtml(sn.name)}</strong>. The structured arc is yours now.`
          : `Day ${sn.dayJustCompleted} of ${sn.totalDays} complete in <strong>${escapeHtml(sn.name)}</strong>. Day ${sn.dayJustCompleted + 1} unlocks tomorrow — return when you're ready.`;
        programBox.style.display = '';
        programBox.innerHTML = `
          <div class="post-card-title">${sn.icon} program progress</div>
          <div class="post-trigger-text" style="font-size:0.86rem;line-height:1.55;color:var(--text-dim);">${nextDayHint}</div>`;
      } else {
        programBox.style.display = 'none';
        programBox.innerHTML = '';
      }
    }

    // Emergency cooldown — duration from safetyConfig (default 30s, user-tunable)
    const statusIcon = $('postStatusIcon');
    if (wasEmergency) {
      const cooldownSec = getSafetyConfig().emergencyCooldownSec;
      state._cooldownUntil = Date.now() + cooldownSec * 1000;
      if ($('groundingBox')) $('groundingBox').style.display = 'block';
      // Reorientation card — anchors back to consensus reality (clinical
      // post-emergency protocol, Quinn ERP / Brown-Fromm). Time + place +
      // "session has ended" framing.
      const reorientCard = $('reorientCard');
      const reorientWhen = $('reorientWhen');
      if (reorientCard && reorientWhen) {
        const now = new Date();
        const day = now.toLocaleDateString(undefined, { weekday: 'long', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
        const time = now.toLocaleTimeString(undefined, { hour: 'numeric', minute: '2-digit' });
        reorientWhen.innerHTML = `It's <strong>${day}</strong> at <strong>${time}</strong>.`;
        reorientCard.style.display = '';
      }
      // Reset the interactive grounding checkboxes so a previous session's
      // state doesn't carry over
      document.querySelectorAll('#groundingBox .grounding-step.interactive').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('done'));
      if (statusIcon) { statusIcon.textContent = '⚠'; statusIcon.style.color = 'var(--neon-amber)'; }
      // Personalized message — use first name if user opted in. Tone is gentle,
      // not chiding (the user already chose to end early; respect that choice).
      const earlyMsg = firstName
        ? `${firstName}, you ended early. That's okay — take a moment to re-orient.`
        : 'You ended early. That\'s okay — take a moment to re-orient.';
      if ($('postMessage')) $('postMessage').textContent = earlyMsg;
    } else {
      if ($('groundingBox')) $('groundingBox').style.display = 'none';
      if ($('reorientCard')) $('reorientCard').style.display = 'none';
      if (statusIcon) { statusIcon.textContent = '✓'; statusIcon.style.color = 'var(--neon-cyan)'; }
      // Welcome-back message — first name if opted in, with light variation by
      // session count so the very first session feels notably different from the
      // 50th. Avoids the same string forever.
      let welcomeMsg;
      if (sessionCount === 1) {
        welcomeMsg = firstName
          ? `Welcome back, ${firstName}. Your first session is recorded.`
          : 'Welcome back. Your first session is recorded.';
      } else if (sessionCount > 0 && sessionCount % 10 === 0) {
        welcomeMsg = firstName
          ? `${firstName}, that's ${sessionCount} sessions — the practice is becoming yours.`
          : `That's ${sessionCount} sessions — the practice is becoming yours.`;
      } else {
        welcomeMsg = firstName
          ? `Welcome back, ${firstName}. Notice how you feel.`
          : 'Take a moment. Notice how you feel.';
      }
      if ($('postMessage')) $('postMessage').textContent = welcomeMsg;
    }

    // Reset post-session state controls
    const moodFeedback = $('moodFeedback');
    if (moodFeedback) moodFeedback.textContent = '';
  }

  // Persona-specific re-alert scripts
  const PERSONA_REALERTS = {

  function emergencyEnd() {
    if (state._finishing) return;
    state._finishing = true;
    state.abortFlag = true;
    // If currently paused, resume speech engine + drone + unpause state
    // so the rescue sequence can actually play
    if (state.paused) {
      state.paused = false;
      if (state._pauseStartedAt) {
        state._pausedTotalMs = (state._pausedTotalMs || 0) + (Date.now() - state._pauseStartedAt);
        state._pauseStartedAt = null;
      }
      try { speechSynthesis.resume(); } catch {}
      if (state.useLocalTTS && _localTTS.ready) { try { _localTTS.resume(); } catch {} }
      if (drone.ctx && drone.running) { try { drone.ctx.resume(); } catch {} }
      $('pauseBtn').textContent = 'pause';
    }
    speechSynthesis.cancel();
    if (state.useLocalTTS && _localTTS.ready) _localTTS.cancel();
    // DEBUG: skip rescue sequence if debug mode is on (consolidated debugMode toggle).
    // This setting intentionally defaults OFF and is NOT saved with settings.
    if (state._debug?.skipRescue) {
      sdLog('rescue skipped — debug mode on');
      finishSession(true);
      return;
    }
    const persona = getPersona();
    const reAlert = PERSONA_REALERTS[persona.id] ||
      "And now... \x5BPAUSE 2\x5D bringing your awareness back. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D Wiggling fingers and toes. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D Taking a deeper breath. \x5BPAUSE 3\x5D Opening your eyes. Fully alert.";
    speakScript(reAlert, /* bypassAbort */ true).then(() => finishSession(true));
  }
  function togglePause() {
    state.paused = !state.paused;
    $('pauseBtn').textContent = state.paused ? 'resume' : 'pause';
    if (state.paused) {
      state._pauseStartedAt = Date.now();
      speechSynthesis.pause();
      if (state.useLocalTTS && _localTTS.ready) _localTTS.pause();
      if (drone.ctx && drone.running) drone.ctx.suspend();
      document.body.classList.remove('controls-hidden'); // always show controls when paused
      clearTimeout(_controlsTimer);
    } else {
      if (state._pauseStartedAt) {
        state._pausedTotalMs = (state._pausedTotalMs || 0) + (Date.now() - state._pauseStartedAt);
        state._pauseStartedAt = null;
      }
      speechSynthesis.resume();
      if (state.useLocalTTS && _localTTS.ready) _localTTS.resume();
      if (drone.ctx && drone.running) drone.ctx.resume();
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (!state.paused && !speechSynthesis.speaking && speechSynthesis.paused) {
          speechSynthesis.cancel();
        }
      }, 300);
      showSessionControls(); // restart auto-hide timer
    }
  }

  // ====================================================================
  // HANDLERS + INIT
  // ====================================================================
  // Stepper clicks (only backward)
  $('stepper').addEventListener('click', e => {
    const item = e.target.closest('.step-item');
    if (!item || !item.classList.contains('clickable')) return;
    goToStep(parseInt(item.dataset.step));
  });
  $('btnNext').addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(state.currentStep + 1));
  $('btnBack').addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(state.currentStep - 1));
$('jumpGuideBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(1));
  $('jumpMethodBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(2));
  $('jumpIntentionBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(3));
  $('jumpAffirmationsBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(4));
  $('jumpConfigBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => goToStep(5)); // Step 5 is Configure; step 4 is Affirmations
  $('btnSkipToScript').addEventListener('click', () => {
    state._skippedToScript = true;
    markFeatureUsed(FEAT.SKIP_SCRIPT);
    state.currentStep = 6;
    state.stepsCompleted = { 1: false, 2: false, 3: false, 4: false, 5: false, 6: false };
    // Show the script editor area with empty textarea for pasting
    $('scriptText').value = '';
    $('scriptStats').innerHTML = 'Paste or type your script here. Use <code>===SETTLING===</code>, <code>===INDUCTION===</code>, etc. markers to define phases, or just paste plain text.';
    $('scriptPreview').classList.add('visible');
    // Hide generate button and summary since we skipped config
    showEl('generateScriptBtn', false);
    showEl('genProgress', false);
    updateStepUI();
    notify.info('Paste your script into the editor below, then press Begin Session. You can still jump back with the back button if you want the guided builder again.');
    // Focus the textarea
    setTimeout(() => $('scriptText')?.focus(), 300);
  });

  // scriptText input handler — updates state when user edits/pastes
  $('scriptText').addEventListener('input', () => {
    const text = $('scriptText').value.trim();
    // Debounced undo checkpoint — coalesces rapid typing into one snapshot.
    // Snapshot captures the PRE-input state (this handler fires BEFORE the
    // state.fullScript assignment below, so the current state still reflects
    // what was there before this keystroke).
    history.pushDebounced(500);
    if (text.length > 20) {
      if (state.fullScript && text !== state.fullScript.trim()) {
        _scriptEditedSinceGen = true;
      }
      state.fullScript = text;
      state.parsedScript = parseScript(text);
      state.generatedPhaseOrder = state.parsedScript.ordered || [];
      const spokenOnly = text.replace(/===\s*[A-Z0-9-]+\s*===/gi, ' ').replace(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi, ' ');
      const words = spokenOnly.split(/\s+/).filter(w => w.length > 0).length;
      const pauses = (text.match(/\x5BPAUSE\s+\d+\]/gi) || []).length;
      const pauseSecs = (text.match(/\x5BPAUSE\s+(\d+)\]/gi) || []).reduce((sum, m) => sum + parseInt(m.match(/\d+/)[0], 10), 0);
      const phaseCount = (state.parsedScript.ordered || []).length;
      $('scriptStats').innerHTML = `<strong>${words}</strong> words · <strong>${pauses}</strong> pauses (${pauseSecs}s) · <strong>${phaseCount}</strong> phases · estimated: <strong>${Math.round(words / 50 + pauseSecs / 60)} min</strong><br>Edit below before starting.`;
      renderPhaseEditor();
    } else {
      state.fullScript = null;
      state.parsedScript = null;
      state.generatedPhaseOrder = [];
      renderPhaseEditor();
    }
    updateStepUI();
  });

  // Fix Timings button
  $('autoTempoBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
    markFeatureUsed(FEAT.TIMING_FIX);
    const text = $('scriptText').value.trim();
    if (!text) { notify.warn('Generate or paste a script first.'); return; }
    const fixed = fixScriptTimings(text);
    $('scriptText').value = fixed;
    state.fullScript = fixed;
    state.parsedScript = parseScript(fixed);
    _scriptEditedSinceGen = false;
    showScript();
    const stripCount = (state.autoTempoOptions?.stripChars || '').length;
    const stripNote = stripCount ? ` (${stripCount} character${stripCount === 1 ? '' : 's'} stripped per options)` : '';
    notify.success(`Pause timings recalculated based on content${stripNote}.`);
  });

  // ── Auto-tempo cleanup options modal ──────────────────────────────────────
  // Two character groups: SAFE (formatting/decorative — won't break sentence
  // structure) and CAUTION (used by the sentence splitter — strip only if
  // your scripts have unusual punctuation).
  const _AUTO_TEMPO_CHARS_SAFE    = ['*', '_', '#', '~', '`', '|', '\\', '/', '<', '>', '=', '+', '^', '&', '%', '$', '@'];
  const _AUTO_TEMPO_CHARS_CAUTION = ['(', ')', '{', '}', '[', ']', '-', '!', '?', '.', ',', ';', ':', "'", '"'];

  function _renderAutoTempoCharGrid(targetId, charList) {
    const container = $(targetId);
    if (!container) return;
    const active = new Set(state.autoTempoOptions?.stripChars || '');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    charList.forEach(ch => {
      const btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.type = 'button';
      btn.className = 'auto-tempo-char-btn' + (active.has(ch) ? ' active' : '');
      btn.textContent = ch;
      btn.title = active.has(ch) ? `Click to KEEP "${ch}"` : `Click to STRIP "${ch}"`;
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if (!state.autoTempoOptions) state.autoTempoOptions = { stripChars: '', stripOrphanPunctuation: true };
        const cur = new Set(state.autoTempoOptions.stripChars || '');
        if (cur.has(ch)) cur.delete(ch); else cur.add(ch);
        state.autoTempoOptions.stripChars = Array.from(cur).join('');
        _renderAutoTempoOptsModal(); // re-render both grids + preview
        saveUserSettings();
      });
      container.appendChild(btn);
    });
  }

  function _renderAutoTempoOptsModal() {
    const opts = state.autoTempoOptions || { stripChars: '', stripOrphanPunctuation: true };
    const cb = $('autoTempoStripOrphan'); if (cb) cb.checked = opts.stripOrphanPunctuation !== false;
    _renderAutoTempoCharGrid('autoTempoCharGridSafe',    _AUTO_TEMPO_CHARS_SAFE);
    _renderAutoTempoCharGrid('autoTempoCharGridCaution', _AUTO_TEMPO_CHARS_CAUTION);
    const preview = $('autoTempoStripPreview');
    if (preview) {
      const chars = opts.stripChars || '';
      preview.textContent = chars
        ? `Will strip these characters: ${chars.split('').map(c => `"${c}"`).join(' ')}`
        : 'No characters will be stripped (default behavior).';
    }
  }

  $('autoTempoOptsBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    _renderAutoTempoOptsModal();
    $('autoTempoOptsModal')?.classList.add('visible');
  });
  $('autoTempoOptsCloseBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    $('autoTempoOptsModal')?.classList.remove('visible');
  });
  $('autoTempoOptsResetBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    state.autoTempoOptions = { stripChars: '', stripOrphanPunctuation: true };
    _renderAutoTempoOptsModal();
    saveUserSettings();
    notify.info('Auto-tempo options reset to defaults.');
  });
  $('autoTempoStripOrphan')?.addEventListener('change', e => {
    if (!state.autoTempoOptions) state.autoTempoOptions = { stripChars: '', stripOrphanPunctuation: true };
    state.autoTempoOptions.stripOrphanPunctuation = !!e.target.checked;
    saveUserSettings();
  });
  // Click-outside-to-close (consistent with other modals using this pattern)
  $('autoTempoOptsModal')?.addEventListener('click', e => {
    if (e.target.id === 'autoTempoOptsModal') $('autoTempoOptsModal').classList.remove('visible');
  });

  // Filter tabs
  $('personaFilterTabs').addEventListener('click', e => {
    if (!e.target.dataset.filter) return;
    state.personaFilter = e.target.dataset.filter;
    document.querySelectorAll('#personaFilterTabs .filter-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.filter === state.personaFilter));
    renderPersonaGrid();
  });
  $('methodFilterTabs').addEventListener('click', async e => {
    if (!e.target.dataset.filter) return;
    const cat = e.target.dataset.filter;
    // Practice-unlock gating: block locked categories
    if (cat === 'rapid' || cat === 'advanced') {
      const count = await getSessionCount();
      const threshold = cat === 'rapid' ? 3 : 7;
      if (count < threshold) {
        notify.info(`${cat.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + cat.slice(1)} methods unlock after ${threshold} completed sessions (${count} so far).`);
        return;
      }
    }
    state.methodFilter = cat;
    document.querySelectorAll('#methodFilterTabs .filter-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.filter === state.methodFilter));
    renderMethodGrid();
  });

  // Step 3
  $('intentionType').addEventListener('change', () => { updateIntentionHint(); saveUserSettings(); });
  $('intentionInput').addEventListener('input', () => { hideCrafted(); updateStepUI(); saveUserSettings(); });
  $('userAffirmations')?.addEventListener('input', () => { saveUserSettings(); updateStepUI(); markFeatureUsed(FEAT.AFFIRMATIONS); });
  $('affirmationMode')?.addEventListener('change', () => { state.affirmationMode = $('affirmationMode').value; saveUserSettings(); });
  $('craftBtn').addEventListener('click', craftSuggestion);
  $('recraftBtn').addEventListener('click', craftSuggestion);
  $('editCraftedBtn').addEventListener('click', toggleEditCrafted);

  // Local AI voice toggle (Phase 6 — Hugging Face SpeechT5 in browser)
  $('localVoiceToggle')?.addEventListener('change', async (e) => {
    const on = e.target.checked;
    state.useLocalTTS = on;
    saveUserSettings();
    const status = $('localVoiceStatus');
    const speakerSel = $('localVoiceSpeaker');
    if (!on) {
      _localTTS.enabled = false;
      _localTTS.cancel();
      if (status) status.textContent = 'Disabled. The system voice above will be used.';
      if (speakerSel) speakerSel.style.display = 'none';
      return;
    }
    _localTTS.enabled = true;
    if (status) status.textContent = 'Loading… first-time download is ~80 MB. Subsequent loads are instant.';
    if (speakerSel) speakerSel.style.display = '';
    const ok = await _localTTS.init(state.localVoiceSpeaker || 'clb');
    if (!ok) {
      // Loading failed — uncheck and revert
      e.target.checked = false;
      state.useLocalTTS = false;
      saveUserSettings();
      if (speakerSel) speakerSel.style.display = 'none';
    } else {
      if (status) status.textContent = '✓ Ready. Local AI voice will be used for the next session.';
    }
  });
  $('localVoiceSpeaker')?.addEventListener('change', async (e) => {
    state.localVoiceSpeaker = e.target.value;
    saveUserSettings();
    if (_localTTS.ready) {
      // Re-init with new speaker — only re-fetches the small embedding (~2KB),
      // not the full model
      await _localTTS.init(e.target.value);
    }
  });
  $('soundscapeSelect')?.addEventListener('change', e => {

  // ── Playback + transition controls (backported from Slideshow) ──
  function buildBgTransitionGrid() {
    const grid = $('bgTransitionGrid');
    if (!grid) return;
    const enabled = new Set(state.bgEnabledTransitions || BG_DEFAULT_ENABLED);
    grid.innerHTML = Object.keys(BG_TRANSITIONS).map(k => {
      const checked = enabled.has(k) ? ' checked' : '';
      return `<label>
        <input type="checkbox" value="${k}"${checked}>
        <span>${BG_TRANSITIONS[k].label}</span>
      </label>`;
    }).join('');
  }
  function syncBgEnabledFromGrid() {
    const boxes = document.querySelectorAll('#bgTransitionGrid input[type="checkbox"]');
    state.bgEnabledTransitions = Array.from(boxes).filter(b => b.checked).map(b => b.value);
    saveUserSettings();
  }
  buildBgTransitionGrid();

  $('bgTransitionGrid')?.addEventListener('change', syncBgEnabledFromGrid);
  $('bgTxAll')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('#bgTransitionGrid input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(b => b.checked = true);
    syncBgEnabledFromGrid();
  });
  $('bgTxNone')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('#bgTransitionGrid input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(b => b.checked = false);
    syncBgEnabledFromGrid();
  });
  $('bgTxInvert')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('#bgTransitionGrid input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(b => b.checked = !b.checked);
    syncBgEnabledFromGrid();
  });

  $('bgOrderSeg')?.addEventListener('click', e => {
    const btn = e.target.closest('button[data-order]');
    if (!btn) return;
    state.bgPlaybackOrder = btn.dataset.order;
    $('bgOrderSeg').querySelectorAll('button').forEach(b => b.classList.toggle('active', b === btn));
    saveUserSettings();

  $('bgTransitionDurSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {

  });
  $('bgTransitionDurSlider')?.addEventListener('change', saveUserSettings);

  // ── Background image generation queue system ──
  // _bgQueuePending = images queued but not yet started
  // bgEngine.activeGenerations = images currently being generated
  // The runner drains _bgQueuePending by launching generations up to BG_MAX_PARALLEL at a time.
  let _bgQueuePending = 0;
  let _bgQueueRunning = false;

  function _bgUpdateQueueUI() {
    const statusEl = $('bgQueueStatus');
    const removeBtn = $('bgRemoveQueuedBtn');
    const total = _bgQueuePending + bgEngine.activeGenerations;
    if (total > 0) {
      if (statusEl) {
        const parts = [];
        if (_bgQueuePending > 0) parts.push(`${_bgQueuePending} queued`);
        if (bgEngine.activeGenerations > 0) parts.push(`${bgEngine.activeGenerations} generating`);
        statusEl.textContent = parts.join(' · ');
        statusEl.style.display = '';
      }
      if (removeBtn) removeBtn.style.display = '';
    } else {
      if (statusEl) statusEl.style.display = 'none';
      if (removeBtn) removeBtn.style.display = 'none';
    }
    // Update button labels to reflect queue
    const btn = $('bgPreviewBtn');
    const batchBtn = $('bgPreviewBatchBtn');
    if (btn) btn.textContent = total > 0 ? `generate image (+1)` : 'generate image';
    if (batchBtn) batchBtn.textContent = total > 0 ? `generate 4 (+4)` : 'generate 4 (parallel)';
  }

  async function _bgQueueRunner() {
    if (_bgQueueRunning) return; // already draining
    _bgQueueRunning = true;
    const wrap = $('bgPreviewWrap');
    const status = $('bgPreviewStatus');
    const grid = $('bgPreviewGrid');
    const saveBtn = $('bgSaveLastBtn');
    if (wrap) wrap.style.display = '';
    bgEngine.prompt = $('bgPromptInput')?.value || '';
    while (_bgQueuePending > 0) {
      // Launch up to BG_MAX_PARALLEL at a time
      const batch = Math.min(_bgQueuePending, BG_MAX_PARALLEL - bgEngine.activeGenerations);
      if (batch <= 0) {
        // All slots busy — wait for one to free up
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 200));
        _bgUpdateQueueUI();
        continue;
      }
      _bgQueuePending -= batch;
      _bgUpdateQueueUI();
      if (status) status.textContent = 'Sending to Perchance AI... (typically 10-30 seconds)';
      const promises = Array.from({ length: batch }, () =>
        bgEngine.generateOne().then(url => {
          _bgUpdateQueueUI();
          if (url && grid) {
            const img = document.createElement('img');
            img.src = url;
            grid.appendChild(img);
            if (saveBtn) saveBtn.style.display = '';
          }
          return url;
        })
      );
      await Promise.all(promises);
      // Update status after each micro-batch
      const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
      const el = $('bgCacheCount'); if (el) el.textContent = manifest.length;
      if (status) {
        const remaining = _bgQueuePending + bgEngine.activeGenerations;
        status.textContent = remaining > 0
          ? `${manifest.length} image${manifest.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} in cache. ${remaining} remaining...`
          : `Done. ${manifest.length} image${manifest.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} in cache.`;
      }
      renderBgGallery();
    }
    _bgUpdateQueueUI();
    _bgQueueRunning = false;
    // Final status
    if (status && bgEngine.activeGenerations === 0) {
      const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
      if (manifest.length > 0) {
        status.textContent = `Done. ${manifest.length} image${manifest.length === 1 ? '' : 's'} in cache.`;
      } else {
        status.textContent = typeof root !== 'undefined' && root.textToImagePlugin
          ? 'Generation failed — server may be busy. Try again.'
          : 'Plugin not found. Add textToImagePlugin = ' + '\u007B' + 'import:text-to-image-plugin' + '\u007D' + ' to the top editor.';
      }
    }
  }

  function _bgQueueAdd(count) {
    _bgQueuePending += count;
    _bgUpdateQueueUI();
    _bgQueueRunner(); // start draining if not already running
  }

  function _bgQueueRemove() {
    if (_bgQueuePending > 0) {
      _bgQueuePending--;
      _bgUpdateQueueUI();
      if (_bgQueuePending === 0 && bgEngine.activeGenerations === 0) {
        const status = $('bgPreviewStatus');
        if (status) status.textContent = 'Queue cleared.';
      }
    }
  }

  $('bgPreviewBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => _bgQueueAdd(1));
  $('bgPreviewBatchBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => _bgQueueAdd(4));
  $('bgRemoveQueuedBtn')?.addEventListener('click', _bgQueueRemove);
  $('bgAutoGenToggle')?.addEventListener('change', e => { state.bgAutoGen = e.target.checked; saveUserSettings(); });
  $('bgSaveLastBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
    if (manifest.length > 0) {
      await bgCacheDownload(manifest[manifest.length - 1].id);
      notify.success('Image saved to your device.');
    }
  });
  $('bgManageBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => { renderBgGallery(); $('bgGalleryModal')?.classList.add('visible'); });
  $('bgGalleryCloseBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => $('bgGalleryModal')?.classList.remove('visible'));
  $('bgClearAllBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    if (!await confirmAsync('Clear all cached background images?')) return;
    await bgCacheClear(); renderBgGallery(); notify.info('Background cache cleared.');
  });
  $('bgDownloadAllBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    const manifest = await bgCacheGetManifest();
    if (!manifest.length) { notify.info('No images to download.'); return; }
    notify.info(`Downloading ${manifest.length} image${manifest.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}...`);
    for (const entry of manifest) {
      await bgCacheDownload(entry.id);
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 300)); // stagger to avoid browser blocking
    }
  });
  $('bgFileInput')?.addEventListener('change', e => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (!file) return;
    $('bgFileName').textContent = file.name;
    state._bgFile = file;
    saveUserSettings();
  });
  $('bgYoutubeUrl')?.addEventListener('input', e => { state.bgYoutubeUrl = e.target.value; saveUserSettings(); });
  $('bgUrlInput')?.addEventListener('input', e => { state.bgStaticUrl = e.target.value; saveUserSettings(); });

  // Slider batch save — fires only on release (change), not every drag tick (input)
  ['speechRate', 'voicePitch', 'voiceVolume', 'droneVolume'].forEach(id => {
    $(id)?.addEventListener('change', () => saveUserSettings());
  });

  // Ducking toggle
  $('duckingToggle')?.addEventListener('change', e => {
    state.duckingEnabled = e.target.checked;

  });

  // Visual effect tuning sliders
  // Viz tuning sliders
  [['vizSpeed','speed','×',1],['vizIntensity','intensity','×',1],['vizComplexity','complexity','×',1],['vizTrail','trail','',2]].forEach(([id, key, suffix, decimals]) => {
    $(id)?.addEventListener('input', e => {
      state.vizSettings[key] = parseInt(e.target.value, 10) / 100;

    $(id)?.addEventListener('change', () => saveUserSettings());

  // Step 6 — Generate & Begin

  $('addInductionPhaseBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => addPhaseSection('induction'));

  // Reimagine mode toggle (affects Custom block ✨ buttons)

  $('normalizePhaseOrderBtn')?.addEventListener('click', resetPhaseOrderToDefault);
  $('undoBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => history.undo());
  $('redoBtn')?.addEventListener('click', () => history.redo());

  // Keyboard shortcuts: Ctrl/Cmd+Z = undo, Ctrl/Cmd+Shift+Z = redo.
  // Only fires while Step 4 (script preview / phase editor) is visible AND
  // focus is not inside a textarea/input (users expect native undo there).
  document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
    if (!(e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) || e.key.toLowerCase() !== 'z') return;
    const preview = $('scriptPreview');
    if (!preview || !preview.classList.contains('visible')) return;
    const tag = (document.activeElement?.tagName || '').toLowerCase();
    if (tag === 'textarea' || tag === 'input') return; // let native undo win
    e.preventDefault();
    if (e.shiftKey) history.redo(); else history.undo();
  });

  // Pre-session mood emoji buttons
  document.querySelectorAll('.mood-emoji').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      document.querySelectorAll('.mood-emoji').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('selected'));
      btn.classList.add('selected');
      state._preMood = parseInt(btn.dataset.val, 10);
    });
  });
  // Pre-session tension and energy sliders
  $('preTensionSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state._preTension = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
    const el = $('preTensionVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
  });
  $('preEnergySlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    state._preEnergy = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
    const el = $('preEnergyVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
  });

  // Post-session mood slider (0-10)
  // Debounce timer for post-mood persistence — fires 600ms after last drag step
  // so a slider drag from 5 to 8 doesn't write 4 entries / inflate metrics samples.
  let _postMoodPersistTimer = null;

  $('postStateSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    const val = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
    const el = $('postStateVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
    const fb = $('moodFeedback');
    const delta = val - (state._preMood ?? 5);
    if (fb) fb.textContent = delta > 0 ? `+${delta} improvement` : delta === 0 ? 'same as before' : `${delta} — be gentle with yourself`;
    // Persist + downstream effects after debounce — avoids amplifying per-day
    // metric samples and adaptive corrections on every drag step.
    clearTimeout(_postMoodPersistTimer);
    _postMoodPersistTimer = setTimeout(async () => {
      _postMoodPersistTimer = null;
      try {
        const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
        if (history.length > 0) {
          history[0].postMood = val;
          history[0].preMood = state._preMood ?? null;
          history[0].preTension = state._preTension ?? null;
          history[0].preEnergy = state._preEnergy ?? null;
          history[0].depth = parseInt($('depthSlider')?.value ?? 5, 10);
          await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', history);
        }
        recordPostMood(val);
        // Patch today's metrics-history aggregate with the post-checkin signals.
        // Single call per debounced settle, so per-day samples accumulate cleanly
        // (one mood/depth sample per session, not one per slider step).
        updateMetricsHistoryWithPostCheckin({
          postMood: val,
          preMood:  state._preMood ?? null,
          depth:    parseInt($('depthSlider')?.value ?? 5, 10),
        }).catch(err => console.warn('[metrics] post-checkin patch failed:', err));
        // Retroactively correct adaptive reward now that real postMood is known
        try {
          const adaptive = await getAdaptive();
          const h = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
          if (h.length > 0 && adaptive.ts > 0) {
            const rec = h[0];
            const oldReward = ((5) - (rec.preMood ?? 5)) + (rec.completed ? 1 : -1);
            const newReward = (val - (rec.preMood ?? 5)) + (rec.completed ? 1 : -1);
            const correction = newReward - oldReward;
            if (Math.abs(correction) > 0.01) {
              const bump = (map, key) => { if (key) map[key] = (map[key] || 0) + correction; };
              bump(adaptive.w.p, rec.personaId); bump(adaptive.w.m, rec.methodId);
              bump(adaptive.w.s, rec.soundscape); bump(adaptive.w.ln, rec.length);
              await idbSet(ADAPTIVE_KEY, adaptive);
            }
          }
        } catch {}
      } catch (err) { console.warn('[postMood] persistence failed:', err); }
    }, 600);
  });

  // Depth slider
  $('depthSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    const el = $('depthVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
  });

  // Alertness check — auto-trigger grounding if low
  $('alertnessSlider')?.addEventListener('input', e => {
    const val = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
    const el = $('alertnessVal'); if (el) el.textContent = e.target.value;
    // Howard Alertness Scale: if alertness < 5, show grounding exercise
    const groundingBox = $('groundingBox');
    if (groundingBox) {
      if (val < 5) {
        groundingBox.style.display = 'block';
        if ($('moodFeedback')) $('moodFeedback').textContent = 'You seem drowsy — please do the grounding exercise before standing up.';
      } else {
        groundingBox.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }
  });

  // Journal save

    if (!text) return;
    const history = (await idbGet('stillness_history_v1')) || [];
    if (history.length > 0) { history[0].journal = text; await idbSet('stillness_history_v1', history); }
  });

  // Backup/restore
